Zvavakaita izvi zvakashorwa nevakawanda avo vaiti VaChiwenga vaishandisa chisoja pazvinhu zvinoda nhaurirano .
Vana chiremba vadiki vanoti vari kuda kuti hurumende ivape michina yekushandisa muzvipatara , mishonga pamwe nembatya dzekuzvidzivirira kana vari pabasa pamwe nekuwedzerwa mari dzemihoro idzo dzavanoti dzakafanana nemutero wembwa .
Asi hurumende inotiwo homwe yayo yakabooka zvekuti haikwanise kuvawedzera mari .
Hatina kukwanisa kunzwa divi regurukora rezvehutano , VaObadiah Moyo , sezvo vabva vapinda mumusangano navana chiremba panguva yatanga toenda pamhepo .
Dare rinonzwa nyaya dzevashandi , re Labor Court , raramba kutambira chikumbiro chehurumende sezvo hurumende yanga isina kuunza magwaro akakwana panyaya yayo yairi kunetsana navanachiremba vasiri kuenda kubasa .
Gweta ranga rakamirira vanachiremba veZimbabwe Hospital Doctor's Association mudare reLabor Court , VaDoug Coltart , vati dare rati panga pasina mapepa akakwana kubva kuHealth Services Board , HSB , nokudaro nyaya iyi haikwanisi kunzwikwa zviri pamutemo .
Dare rati gweta reHSB riunze mapepa asipo aya mangwana , unova musi weChitatu .
Asi vana chiremba vatiwo kuendesana kumatare hazvisizvo zvinounza mari yekuti vakwanise kuenda kumabasa , nekudaro hazvigadzirisi dambudziko riripo .
Vakafanobata chigaro chemutevedzeri wemutungamiri weZimbabwe Hospital Doctors Association , Doctor Masimba Ndoro , vati basa ravo rinovasungira kuti vavepo mazuva ese nekudaro vanofanirwa kuwaniswa mari yekuti izvi zviitike .
Vana chiremba vadiki vakatanga kusaenda kumabasa musi wa3 Gunyana vachiti havana zvikwanisiro zvakakwana zvekuti vaende kumabasa .
Vana chiremba vakuru pasi peZimbabwe Senior Hospital Doctors' Association vakatangawo kusaenda kumabasa nemusi weChina chapfuura vachinyunyutawo nenyaya yemihoro pamwe nekushaya zvekushandisa zvakakwana muzvipatara .
Vana chiremba vakuru ava vanyorawo gwaro vachitsutsumwa nezvekutyityidzirwa kwavari kuita vakati hazvibatsiri kuti vana chiremba vave kuzvipatara kusina zvikwanisiro zvinoita kuti vachengetedze hupenyu hwevarwere .
Vana chiremba vashorawo hurumende vachiti mari yakawedzerwa nezvikamu makumi matanhatu kubva muzana vachiti havana kubvumirana nazvo .
Zvichakadaro , mamwe madhokotera makuru maviri amiswa basa neUniversity of Zimbabwe pasina muhoro vachipomerwa mhosva yekubatana nevamwe kuramwa mabasa pamwe nekupesvedzera vamwe vavo kuti vasaende kubasa .
Vamiswa basa ava ndiDr .
Bothwell Mbuvayesango , vanove nyanzvi mukuvhiya vana , pamwe naDr .
David Chimuka , nyanzvi mukurapa chirwere chemoyo .
Dr . Mbuvayesangano vakaita mukurumbira munyika mushure mekubudirira kwavakaita kuopareta mapatya aive akaberekwa misoro yavo yakabatana muna 2014 , ukuwo Dr . Chimuka vachizivikanwa nezvikuru munyaya dzekuopareta moyo .
Sangano reZimbabwe Association of Doctors for Human Rights rashora zvikuru kumiswa basa kwaitwa basa Dr . Mbuvayesangano naDr .
Chimuka .
Hatina kukwanisa kunzwa kubva kuUniversity of Zimbabwe pamwe nekunzwa kudivi rehurumende nezviri kuitika izvi munyaya dzehutano .
Asi mugwaro rabudiswa negurukota rezveutano , VaObadiah Moyo , vabvuma kuti vana chiremba havana kuteerera kurudziro yehurumende yekuti vadzokere kumabasa .
VaMoyo vati hurumende yave kumirira zvichabuda kumatare , mushure mezvo vozivisa nyika pamire hurumende .
Vanachiremba vakatanga kusaenda kubasa musi 3 Gunyana vachiti havana mari dzinovakwanira kunge vachienda kumabasa avo .
Hurumende yanyorerana chibvumirano neimwe kambani yekunze kwenyika kuitira kuti ibatsirwe mukutengesa marasha kunyika dzakaita seIndia neJapan .
Vachitaura pakunyoreranwa kwechibvumirano ichi ne Victoria Consulting , gurukota rinoona nezvezvicherwa , VaWinston Chitando , vati donzvo rehurumende nderekuti nyika iwanirwe kwekutengesera marasha kuIndia uye kuitira kuti iwane mari yekushandisa mukuchera marasha aya .
VaChitando vati Zimbabwe inofungidzirwa kuti ine marasha anosvika mabhiriyoni makumi maviri nemashanu ematani asi pagore kuri kucherwa matani ari pakati pemamiriyoni maviri nemamiriyoni matatu .
VaChitando vatiwo India ndiyo inotenga marasha akawanda pagore zvichienzaniswa nedzimwe nyika .
Vachitaura pamusangano mumweyo , mutungamiriri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , vati Zimbabwe inofanirwa kutora mukana wekudyidzana wakanaka uripo pakati payo neIndia .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kuziva kuti kambani yeVictoria Consulting yakamboshanda nenyika dzipi , uye kuti vakuru vayo ndivanani .
Asi vaimbove mutevedzeri wegurukota rezvezvicherwa muhurumende yemubatanidzwa , VaGift Chimanikire , vati havaoni kuti zvakanaka kuti Zimbabwe itsvage misika yekutengesera marasha kunze kwenyika , ipo pari zvino kusiri kucherwa marasha anokwana munyika .
Nyanzvi mune zvehupfumi , VaNyasha Muchichwa , vatiwo havaoni zvakakosha kuti Zimbabwe itsvake kambani yekunze inonotsvakira Zimbabwe misika yemarasha .
VaMuchichwa vatiwo zviri nani kuti kushandiswe hukama hwagara huripo nedzimwe nyika .
Dandemudande rebazi rezvezvicherwa rinoti Zimbabwe ine marasha akanaka , uye ine nzvimbo makumi maviri nepfumbamwe dzine marasha .
Makambani maviri chete munyika , Hwange Colliery neMakomo Resources , ndiwo ari kunyanyochera marasha .
Nhengo nhanhatu dzebato reMDC inotungamirwa naVaNelson Chamisa , idzo dzakasungwa muHarare neChishanu , dzabvisiswa mari yechibatiso inoita chiuru chemadhora emuZimbabwe pamunhu kuitira kuti dzitongwe dzichibva kudzimba dzadzo .
Vapihwa mukana wekubvisa mari yechibatiso nemutongi wedare remajisitireti , Amai Bianca Makwande , vatevedzeri vaviri vaVaChamisa ; VaTendai Biti naAmai Lynett Karenyi Kore ; munyori anoona nezvekudyidzana nedzimwe nyika , Muzvare Gladys Hlatywayo ; mutevedzeri wemunyori wezvekudyidzana nedzimwe nenyika , VaLovemore Chinoputsa ; nhengo yeNational Standing Committee ,
uye vari mutevedzeri wemunyori mukuru webato , VaDavid Chimhini naAmai Vongai Tome .
Vanhu ava vanzi vabvise mari inoita chiuru chemadhora pamunhu zvichitevera kusungwa kwavakaitwa nezuro zvichitevera gakava riripo panyaya yemuzinda weMDC weMorgan Tsvangirai House .
Amai Makwande vati vasungwa ava vazodzoke kudare musi wa 24 Chikunguru uye kuti vagare pamakero avakanyoresa kumapurisa kudzamara nyaya yavari kupomerwa yapera kutongwa .
Vachitaura neStudio7 mushure memutongo uyu , rimwe regweta evatanhatu ava , VaAlec Muchadehama , vati dare ratiwo vanhu vavari kumirira vasakanganise kuferefetwa kwenyaya iyi .
VaMuchadehama vatiwo kunyangwe hazvo vatanhatu ava nezuro vaipomherwa mhosva yekukonzera musindo pasi pemutemo we Criminal Law ( Codification and Reform ) Act , vasungwa ava vange vambouya kumatare mangwanani vakadzorerwa kumapurisa uko kwazonowedzerwa mhosva yekutyora mutemo une chekuita nekudzivirirwa kwechirwere cheCOVID - 19 .
Magweta evatanhatu ava anyunyutawo kudare nemabatirwo avanoti akaitwa vasungwa .
VaMuchadehama vati vasungwa ava havana kuchengetedzwa zvakanaka zvaiita kuti vasabatirire kana kutapurira vamwe chirwere cheCOVID - 19 pavaive muhusungwa .
Mutungamiri webato iri , VaNelson Chamisa , vati vacharamba vachirwira shanduko munyika zvisinei nekusungwa kuri kuitwa nhengo dzavo
Amai Makwande varamba kuti mutevedzeri wemutauriri wevechidiki mubato iri , VaWomberaishe Nhende , avo vari kurapwa mune chimwe chipatara , vasarambe vari muhusungwa .
VaNhende vanonzi vakakuvara nezuro apo vakasungwa ndokubva vaendeswa kuchipatara .
Mune imwe nyaya yanga iri mumatare , Zimbabwe Lawyers for Human Rights inoti mupurisa akasungwa mushure mekufananidza mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , nekondomu rakashandiswa , amiswawo mutare akabvisiswa mari yechibatiso inoita mazana matatu emadhora .
Mupurisa uyu , Shungudzemoyo Kache , achatongwawo achibva kumba kwake .
Mukuru weProphetic Healing and Deliverance ( PHD ) Ministries , VaWalter Magaya , vari kuramba vakaomesa musoro panyaya yavakasungirwa muZimbabwe vachiti vava kushanda nedzimwe nyika kuitira kuti vakwanise kuparura mushonga weAguma uyo wavanoti unorapa HIV / AIDS , gomarara nezvimwe .
Vachitaura neStudio7 kumucheto kwemunamato wavakaita mudhorobha reFrancistown muBotswana neChitatu manheru , VaMagaya vakati havazi kuzodzokera shure nehurongwa hwavo hwakavakasungisa nemapurisa muna Mbudzi 2018 mushure mekushambadza kuti vakanga wana mushonga unorapa HIV / AIDS .
Mushure mekubvuma mhosva yekushambadza zvisiri pamutemo kuti vawana mushonga unorapa HIV / AIDS , VaMagaya vakabhadhariswa faindi yemazana manomwe emadhora ekuAmerica muna Kukadzi gore rakapera .
Asi zvakaitika izvi hazvina kuodza VaMagaya moyo , avo vakaudza Studio7 kuti vari mubishi kushanda nedzimwe nyika dzavasina kuda kudoma idzo vakati dziri kuona mushonga weAguma uri mhinduro kudambudziko reHIV / AIDS .
VaMagaya vakati HIV / AIDS yanetsa muAfrica , nokudaro inoda kuti nyika dzose dziise misoro pamwe chete mukutsvaga mhinduro kudambudziko iri .
VaMagaya vakati vakaona zvakakodzera kuti vashande nedzimwe nyika nokuti Zimbabwe haina chivimbo chokuti mushonga uyu ungapedza matenda anetsa munyika .
Asi pamutongo wakapihwa VaMagaya muZimbabwe , kambani yavo yeAretha Medical Company , yakawanikwa isina kunyoresa neMedicines Control Authority of Zimbabwe , uye inonzi haina kupihwa mvumo neHealth Professions Authority kuti iite tsagiridzo dzekuona kuti mushonga weAguma unoshanda here kana kuti kwete .
Mumwe chiremba pachipatara chakazvimirira chega muFrancistown , VaSengaphi Khuzwayo , vashora VaMagaya vachiti munhu ari kutsvaga mari .
VaMagaya vakambokonzeresa mutauro munyika mushure mekunge vasungwa nemhosva yekubata mumwe mudzimai chibharo , asi nyaya iyi yakazoraswa nedare redzimhosva mushure mekunge mumhangari abvisa nyaya iyi zviri pamutemo .
Kushaikwa kwavana chiremba muzvipatara zvehurumende kwave kuisa hupenyu hwemadzimai akazvitakura panjodzi kana vakaita dambudziko sezviri kuitika pachipatara chikuru chemuChinhoyi .
Muzvare Lisa Sibanda ndemumwe mudzimai akatarisana nedambudziko rekutadza kusununguka zvakanaka .
Muzvare Sibanda vanoti mwana wavo , uyo anga , asati asvika nguva yekuzvarwa , akafira mudumbu pavakauya nemusiwe Chipiri , asi hapana chiremba akavayamura vachiti vakatozoyamurwawo nemumwe mukoti uyo akaita kuti mwana abude akafa .
Muzvare Sibanda vanoti dambudziko guru rave rekuti vasukwe chibereko chavo zvekuti vakanonokerwa sezvavari kuitwa , zvinogona kuvhiringa hutano hwavo .
Muzvare Sibanda vanoti vari kusangana nedambudzikowo rekushaya mvura zvekuti zvimbudzi zvepachipatara ichi hazvichapindika uye vave kutochingidzira mvura inenge ichinaya .
VaErasmus Zindoga , avo vakauya nemudzimai wavo kubva kuKariba , vanoti havasati vawana rubatsiro kubva kunana chiremba vachiti mumwe chiremba wavakaona pachipatara apa , akaramba kurapa mudzimai wavo .
VaZindoga vanoti vakatohaya motokari kubva kuKariba kuuya kuChinhoyi mufambo une makiromita mazana maviri nemakumi mashanu sezvo zvinhu zvisina kumirawo zvakanaka pachipatara chemuKariba .
Hatina kunzwa kuti madzimai mangani ari kusangana nematambudziko akadai pachipatara chemuChinhoyi icho chinotambira vanorwara kubva munzvimbo dzinosanganisira Kariba , Hurungwe , Karoi , Makonde neZvimba .
Vakafanobata chigaro chemukuru webazi rezvehutano mudunhu reMashonaland West , VaTapiwa Dhliwayo , vanoti semaziviro avo vanachiremba vanofanirwa kunge vari pabasa mudunhu rose .
Asi vabvuma kuti vanamukoti havasi ivo vanofanirwa kurapa madzimai anenge ayita dambudziko pakusununguka sezviri kuitika pachipatara chemuChinhoyi .
Mutauriri wekanzuru yeChinhoyi , VaTichaona Mlauzi , vakaburitsa chiziviso svondo rapera vachiti guta reChinhoyi , iro rine vagari vanosvika zviuru zana namakumi maviri , rine dambudziko remvura nekuda kwemapambu matatu akafa ayo ari kugadzirwa .
Sangano re Cancer Association of Zimbabwe rinokurudzira veruzhinji kuti vawongororwe gomarara rezamhu pachine nguva uye chirwere ichi chisati chakomba .
Vanhu vanodarika zviuru zvishanu vari kubatwa nezvirwere zvakasiyana siyana zvegomarara pagore rega rega muZimbabwe , asi vazhinji vacho vanozoona vana chiremba chirwere ichi chakomba .
Mutungamiri wesangano iri , Amai Junior Mavhu , vanoti pari zvino vane zvirongwa zvekuwongorora madzimai nevanhurume kuti vanegomarara rezamu here kuitira kuti vawane rubatsiro pane nguva .
Chirwere chegomarara chinonzi chirikuuraya vanhu vazhinji munyika nyanya madzimai kunyangwe hazvo chichiwanikwawo muvanhurumwe .
Rimwewo sangano reCancer Centre riri kukurudzira vakadzi nevarume kuti vashandise mukana wemwedzi waGumiguru kuti vaongororwe chirwere chegomarara , pamwe nekudzidziswa nezvechirwere ichi zviripachena apo varikucherechedza mwedzi weWorld Breast Cancer Month .
Pasi rese riri kucherechedza mwedzi uno senguva yinofanira kuyeuchidzwa vanhu kuti vagare vachiziva nezvechirwere che Gomarara rezamu uye kuti vanobatsirika sei kana chikavawira .
Kurudziro ya Amai Mavhu ndeyekuti munhu wese anofanira kugara achitariswa nguva nenguva kuti chirwere ichi chigone kubaywa nekurapwa chisati chapararriramumuviri .
Zimbabwe yasvitsa makore maviri neMugovera kubva musi wakapfurwa vanhu vatanhatu vakafa muHarare mushure mekunge vanhu vakawanda vapinda mumigwagwa vachiratidza kusafara kwavo nemafambisirwo aitwa sarudzo dzegore ra 2018 .
Kuurayiwa kwevanhu ava kwakaitika pasi rose richiona sezvo vatori venhau vakabva kunyika dzakasiyana siyana , vakange vari muZimbabwe vachiona mafambiro aiita sarudzo yekutanga mutungamiri weZanu PF , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , vachikwikwidza musarudzo yemutungamiri wenyika zvichitevera kubviswa pachigaro nechisimba kwakaitwa vaive mutungamiri webato iri
, muchakabvu Robert Mugabe .
VaMnangagwa vaikwikwidzana naVaNelson Chamisa veMDC Alliance , kusanganisirawo vatungamiri vemapato madiki anopikisa .
Mushure mekupfurwa kwevanhu ava , hurumende yakamanikidzwa kuumba komisheni yekuti iferefete zvakaitika .
Komisheni iyi yaiva nevaimbove mutungamiri weSouth Africa , VaKgalema Motlanthe , sasachigaro wayo .
Komisheni iyi yakaburitsa gwaro rinoratidza kuti mauto nemapurisa ndiwo akauraya vanhu vatanhatu ava , ikati vakauraya vanhu ava vanofanirwa kumiswa pamberi pematare edzimhosva .
Yakatiwo hurumende iripe hama dzevanhu vakaurayiwa ava .
Komisheni yaVaMotlanthe yakatiwo hurumende inofanirwa kuendesa vana vevafi ava kuchikoro , uye kuti mapurisa nemauto asaise mutemo mumaoko awo kana vanhu vachinge vachiratidzira .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzekodzero dzevanhu dzinoti hurumende haisati yatevedzera zviri muMotlanthe Commission .
Asi gurukota rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , Amai Monica Mutsvangwa , vanoti hurumende inoziva zviri muMotlanthe Commission uye ine hurongwa hwekuona kuti zvakatarwa nekomisheni iyi , zvazadziswa .
Mumwe wemakomishina akanyora gwaro iri , VaLovemore Madhuku , avo vanove zvakare mutungamiri weNational Constitutional Assembly , vanoti komisheni yavo yakaita basa rayo ikapedza , chitsvambe chasarira kuhurumende yaVaMnangagwa kuona kuti yatevedzera zviri mugwaro ravakanyora .
VaMadhuku vatiwo komisheni yavo yakabuda nechisungo chekuti hurumende iripe hama dzevafi nekuti vanhu ava vakapfurwa nemasoja nemapurisa .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzekodzero dzevanhu uye vari mukuru weHuman Rights Watch kuchamhembe kweAfrica , VaDewa Mavhinga , vanoti hurumende haisi kuratidza chido chekuzadzisa zviri muMotlanthe Commission Report .
VaMavhinga vanoti pava nemakore maviri gwaro iri raburitswa , asi hapana kana musoja ati asungwa sezvakakurudzirwa nekomisheni yaVaMotlanthe .
Nzvimbo dzakawanda dzasara dzakachena mushure mekunge mutungamiriri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , makurukota avo , nhengo dzeparamende nevemabhizimisi , vabatana neveruzhinji mukuchenesa nzvimbo dzavanoshandira nekugara pasi pechirongwa cheNational Clean - Up Campaign icho chakaparurwa mwedzi mitatu yapfuura .
VaMnangagwa vafumira kuchipatara cheParirenyatwa nemakurukota avo vakabatsira kutsvaira nzimbo dzine tsvina pahipatara ichi .
Vachitaura vapedza kuchenesa pachipatara apa , VaMnangagwa vati chirongwa ichi chiri kufarirwa uye chakanaka chose sezvo chichiita kuti vanhu vave nehutano hwakanaka .
Vati vakaparura zuva iri senzira yekuyeuchidza vanhu kuti ndizvo vanofanira kugara vachiita zuva nezuva .
VaMnangagwa vatiwo vanhu vanofanira kusiyana nemweya wekurasa marara pese pese uye vanofanira kudzidza kubva kunyika dzakaita seRwanda uko kusisabvumirwe vanhu kupfirira dzimba neuswa kana kufamba vanhu vasina kupfeka shangu .
Gurukota rezvemitambo , Muzvare Kirsty Coventry , nevashandi vemubazi ravo , vatanga kutsvaira muna Simon Muzenda Street vakazopedzesera muAfrica Unity Square umo vatsvaira pamwe nevashandi veMeikles Hotel neTM Supermarket .
Vatiwo veruzhinji vashamisika kuvaona vari mumugwagwa vachitsvaira uye vanhu vanofanira kugara vachichenesa nzvimbo dzavanogara .
Vashandi vekambani yeZimbabwe Newspapers vapindawo mumigwagwa yakapoteredza muzinda wekambani iyi uye kambani iyi yatengawo mabhini ikaisa mumigwagwa iyi kuitira kuti vanhu varasire marara .
Mutauriri weZimpapers , Muzvare Beatrice Tonhodzayi , vaudza Studio 7 kuti tsvina yanyanya munharaunda yavanoshandira ndosaka vaona zvakakodzera kubatana nehurumende mukuchenesa guta nenyika .
Vatiwo vashandi vekambani iyi kumahofisi ayo ari mumatunhu ese munyika , vapindawo muchirongwa cheNational Clean - Up Campaign nhasi .
Meya veHarare , VaHebert Gomba , makanzura eguta , nevashandi vekanzuru vatsvairawo nekunonga marara mumisha yakasiyana siyana muHarare .
Vachitaura neStudio 7 mushure mekutsvaira marara nevashandi veOK Machipisa panzvimbo yemabhizimisi yeMachipisa muHighfields , VaGomba vati vafara nekubuda kwaita vanhu nhasi vachiti guta ratombochenawo .
Vati kunyange hazvo basa rekuchenesa guta richida kuti vanhu vaite mushandirapamwe , kanzuru yavo iri kuedza pese painogona napo kuitira kuti guta rigare rakachena .
VaMnangagwa vakaparura zuva iri , iro rinocherechedzwa chishanu chekutanga mwedzi wega wega senzira yekuti vanhu vagare vakachenesa nzvimbo dzavanogara pamwe nekuti vave nehutano hwakanaka .
Bazi rezvemari rinoti richawedzera mari pamwe chete nekuunza mari ine huremu hwakakura munyika senzira yekugadzirisa dambudziko remari munyika .
Vachitaura pamusangano wavaita nevatori venhau muHarare nhasi , munyori mubazi iri , VaGeorge Guvamatanga , vati zvanga zvisingagoni kuti vatange nekuunza mari ine huremu hwakakura izvo zvakaita kuti vatange nemari yemadhora maviri neyemadhora mashona .
VaGuvamatanga vatiwo bazi ravo rinoziva kuti mari iri munyika ishoma , uye hurumende ichagadzirisa dambudziko iri .
Vachibvunzwa kuti vachatora matanho api kupedza dambudziko rekutengeswa kwemari pamukoto , mutevedzeri wegurukota rezvemari , VaClemence Chiduwa , vati vanhu vanotenga zvinhu kunze kwenyika vachabvunzwa kuti mari iyi vakaiwana sei .
Imwe nyanzvi munyaya yezvehupfumi vachishanda nesangano reLabor and Economic Development Research Institute of Zimbabwe , VaNyasha Muchichwa , vati hurumende inogona kukunda nyaya yekutengeswa kwemari pamukota kana chete ikaisa mari inokwana munyika kusanganisira mari yekunze .
VaMuchichwa vatiwo nyaya yekusunga vanotengesa mari mumugwagwa haigadzirisi dambudziko iri sezvo vanozviita vachingoregera kwemazuva mashoma asi vachizosimidzira mabasa aya zvakare .
Bazi rezvemari rabvumawo kuti mari yakaiswa kubazi rezveutano haikwani zvichienzaniswa nematambudziko aripo panyaya yehutano asiwo vakati vacharamba vachigadzirisa .
Gurukota rezvemari , VaMthuli Ncube , vaudzawo vatori venhau pamusangano uyu kuti vari kufadzwa nematanho avakatora panyaya dzekuvandudza hupfumi hwenyika uye zvinhu zviri kufamba negwara .
Asi vaimbove gurukota rezvemari muhurumende yemubatanidzwa , uye vari mumwe wevatevedzeri vatatu veMDC , VaTendai Biti , vanoti dambudziko remari riri kunetsa munyika sezvo bhanga guru renyika , re Reserve Bank of Zimbabwe , riri kuita mamwe mabasa arinofanirwa kunge risingaite , izvo zviri kupa kuti nyika irasikirwe nemari yakawanda .
VaBiti , avo vanove zvakare sachigaro wekomiti yeparamende inoona nezvemari , vanoti bazi rezvemari , pamwe nebhanga guru renyika , zvinofanirwa kushanda zvichitevedza mitemo , uye nenzira dzinoita kuti mari dzenyika dzisanganyangarika sezvakaita mari dzakakwereteswa vamwe vakuru vakuru munyika nebhanga guru renyika .
Asi bazi rezvemari iri rinoti veruzhinji vanofanira kuziva kuti panga pave nemakore akawanda zvakanyanya mari yenyika isingashandiswi mukuvaka nyika , nekudaro kugadzirisa zvinonetsa kuchatora nguva .
Muimbi Rise Kagona anotaura zvenhoroondo yake munyaya dzemagitare uye kushanda nemuimbi , mushakabvu Biggie Tembo .
Vana vana vakafa husiku humwe chete neChina izvo zvinonzi hazvisimboitika nguva dzakawanda kana vanamukoti vari pabasa .

Kunyange hazvo huwandu hwevanhu vari kubatwa nechirwere cheCOVID - 19 huri kuramba huchikwira , vanhu vakawanda havasi kutora matanho ekuzvidzivirira sezviri kukurudzirwa nesangano reWorld Health Organization , akaita sekupfeka mamasiki kumeso kwavo .
Kunyange hazvo zviri pachena kuti veruzhinji vari kutapurirana chirwere ichi munyika , kumisika yemabhazi pamwe nekumabhanga vanhu vanenge vakaungana , kana kumanikidzana , izvo zvinoita kuti kutapurirana kweCovid - 19 kuve nyore .
Studio7 yaona vanhu vazhinji vange vasina kupfeka mamasiki apo vanga vachisangana neveruzhinji muguta reHarare .
Mumwe mugari wemuHarare , VaPaul Majaira , avo vanga vasina kuzvidzivirira vati dzimwe nguva vanombokanganwa kuzvidzivirira .
Mumwe murume uyo asina kuda kudomwa nezita anga akamirira kutora mari pane rimwe bhanga muguta apo vanhu vanga vakatsokodzerana abvuma kuStudio7 kuti ane ruzivo rwekuti huwandu hwevari kubatwa nechirwere cheCOVID - 19 munyika huri kukwira .
Asi ati kunyange hazvo achiziva kuti kumira vakapatsanurana kunobatsira , nyaya yekutya kupindirwa ndiyo inoita kuti vanhu vabatane vari mumitsetse .
VaSimon Zhou , avo vanga vakamirira bhazi kuti vaende kuMt Pleasant Heights , vati vanga vava nemaawa mana vari panzvimbo imwe chete , izvo zvinogona kuti vabate chirwere ichi .
Vatiwo vanhu havasi kutariswa temperature kana kupihwa zvekuzora maoko ava pavanenge vachipinda mumabhazi eZupco sezvaiitika pakatanga kuvhurwa nyika .

Dr . Madzorera vakurudzirawo kuti munguva ino yechando dai veruzhinji vagara kudzimba .
Mutevedzeri wegurukota rezvehutano , Va John Mangwiro , vaudza Studio7 parunhare kuti vari kuwedzera kudzidzisa veruzhinji nezvechirwere ichi pamwe nekuwedzera vanhu vanoongororwa kuitira kudzivirira kutapuriranwa kwechirwere ichi .

Vana chiremba vanoshandira muzvipatara zvehurumende pamwe nevamwe vashandi vemuzvipatara vakawanda varatidzira pachipatara cheMpilo Central Hospital muBulawayo vachiratidza kusafara kwavo nekupambwa kunonzi kwakaitwa mumwe wavo , Doctor Peter Magombeyi nemusi weMugovera muHarare .
Vana chiremba ava , avo vange vachisanganisira nevamwe vekuUnited Bulawayo Hospitals , vambovharidzira misiwo yepachipatara cheMpilo vachiimba uye vakabata zvinyorwa zvange zvichiratidza kusafara kwavo nekupambwa kwaDoctor Magombeyi , avo vanonzi vakatorwa pamba pavo muHarare nevamwe vanhu vasati vaziikanwa kuti ndavanaani .
Doctor Mthabisi Bhebhe , vanove munyori mukuru weMpilo Hospital Doctors Association , vanoti havazi kufara nezvakaitika uye vanoda kuti Doctor Magombeyi vawanikwe vari vapenyu .

Mumwe chiremba , Doctor Tawanda Manjonjo , avo vanoti vakamboshanda vose naDoctor Magombeyi , vanoti vanachiremba vakawanda vave kutyira hupenyu hwavo , asi vanotiwo kunze kwekunge Doctor Magombeyi vawanikwa , vachadzokera kubasa chete kana zvichemo zvavo zvagadziriswa .
Mukuru wechipatara cheMpilo , VaLeonard Mabandi , vanoti sekuziva kwavo vanachiremba vange vavimbisa kuti vachadzokera kubasa mushure mekuratidzira kwechinguva chidiki .
Mumwe murume angozvidoma nezita rekuti Walter , uyo anoti ange ane mudzimai wake ange achirapwa , anoti varwere vakawanda vange vasina kuonekwa navanachiremba .
Vanachiremba vari pakati pekuramwa mabasa apo Doctor Magombeyi vakapambwa .
Vanachiremba vave namasvondo maviri vasingaendi kumabasa vachiti havachakwanisa kuwana mari dzekufambisa .
Hurumende inoti iri kugadzira mutemo wekurambidza vanachiremba kuramwa mabasa , asi nyanzvi munyaya dzekodzero dzevanhu dzinoti izvi hazvienderani nebumbiro remutemo wenyika .

Vati zvavakasangana nazvo zvakakonzera kuti vatore nguva yekuti vanyatsoongorora zviri kuitika vachiti vakaona zvange zvisingafungirwi nesangano ravo .

Vamwe vagari vemuGweru vanoti vave kutyira kupararira kwechirwere checoronavirus kana kuti Covid - 19 zvichitevera kuchengetedzwa muguta iri kwezvimwe zvizvarwa zvemuno zvakabva kunze kwenyika .
Vanhu vanoda kusvika zana nemakumi maviri vakachengetedzwa paGweru Polytechnic kutanga nemusi weChishanu svondo rapera .
Kune vamwezve vanhu vanosvika makumi matatu vakachengetedzwa paMkoba Teachers' College kutanga nezuro .
Vanhu ava ndevamwe vari pakati pezvizvarwa zveZimbabwe zviri kudzorwa kubva kunyika dzeSouth Africa neBotswana .
Munyori mukuru mubazi rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko VaNick Mangwana vachinyora padandemutande ravo reTwitter vanoti Mkoba Teachers College inokwanisa kugara vanhu mazana mashanu vari kubva kunze kwenyika .
Vakatiwo Gweru Polytechnic yatozara .
Mumwe mugari Amai Enita Nyati vaudza Studio 7 kuti vanotyira kupararira kwechirwere checoronavirus nekuti vamwe vevanhu ava vanogona kuve vainacho vachitiwo vanhu ava vanogona kutiza munzvimbo dzavakachengetedzwa .
Asi mumwewo mugari Muzvare Nyasha Mahwende vati vanhu ava vanofanirwa kubatwa zvakanaka sezvo zviri zvizvarwa zvemuZimbabwe uye vari hama neshanwari dzevamwe vanhu .
Vatiwo kunze kwekutyira kupararira kwechirwere vari kutyirawo kuti vamwe vevanhu ava vanogona kuita zviri kunze kwemutemo vakatsinhirawo kuti vanofanirwa kuchengetedzwa zvakasimba .
Studio 7 yanyimwa mvumo yekupinda panzvimbo mbiri idzi nevange vakachengetedza vachiti tinofanirwa kupiwa mvumo kubva kumahofisi ehurumende emudunhu reMidlands .
Taedza kunzwa kubva kugurukota redunhu reMidlands VaLarry Mavima pamwe nevakafanobata chigaro chemukuru wedunhu munyaya dzezvehutano kana kuti Provincial medical director Dr Reginald Mhene asi patasvika kumahofisi avo vanzi vange vari mumusangano .
Vanoziva zviri kuitika vanoti kuBotswana nekuSouth Africa kwavaive vari vamwe vevanhu ava vainzi vari munyika idzi zvisiri pamutemo vakambosungwa , izvo zvakavaisa panjodzi yekubata chirwere checoronavirus .
Meya weguta reGweru VaJosiah Makombe vabvuma kuStudio 7 kuti chipatara chinorapwa varwere vecoronavirus kana kuti Isolation District Hospital chichiri kunadzurudzwa pari zvino .
Vakurudzira vagari kuti vatevedzere zvinokurudzirwa pakudzivirira chirwere checoronavirus asi vati havafanirwe kutya vachiti vane chivimbo chekuti kana pakaitika vanowanikwa vaine chirwere ichi vanokwanisa kurapwa .
Mukuru webato rePeople's Democratic Party Amai Lucia Matibenga avo vanovewo mugari wemuguta reGweru vati ibasa rehurumende kuchengetedza vanhu vari kudzoka ava zvakanaka uye kuwonawo kuti vamwe vagari vose vakachengetedzeka .
Mudunhu reMidlands hamusati maita munhu akabatwa nechirwere checoronavirus .
Asi kudzoka kumusha kuri kuramba kuchiita zvizvarwa zveZimbabwe kubva kunyika dzakatipoteredza kuri kuita kuti vamwe vabatire hura mumaoko vachityira chirwere ichi .
Hofisi yemutungamiri wenyika neChitatu yakaita musangano navana chiremba vari kuramwa mabasa kekutanga kubva zvakatanga vanachiremba ava kuratidzira musi wa 1 Zvita gore rapera .
Vamwe vana chiremba vakuru vari vana mazvikokota kana kuti maRegistrars nemaConsultancy vange vatangawo kuramwa mabasa neChitatu .
Vanhu vakawanda munyika vanoti vanhu vari kurasikirwa nehupenyu nekuda kwekuramwa mabasa kwavana chiremba uku .
Mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , vakadzoka kubva kuzororo neChipiri kuti vazobatana nevaikafanobata chigaro chemutungamiri wenyika , General Constantino Chiwenga , kuyedza kugadzirisa dambudziko rekuramwa mabasa kwavanachiremba iri .
Munyori mubazi rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , VaNick Mangwana , vatenda kuti VaMnangagwa vakadzoka kubasa kuzobatsira kudzimura moto .
Nemusi weChipiri VaChiwenga vainge vambodya marasha vachiti vanachiremba vanofanira kudzokera kumabasa .
Vana chiremba vakuru vari pasi peZimbabwe Medical Association vange vapa hurumende maawa makumi mana nemasere kugadzirisa nyaya yavanachiremba vadiki vabva vatangawo kuramwa mabasa .
Asi hofisi yaVaMnangagwa yabva yaita musangano nevatungamiri veZimbabwe Hospital Doctors Association , Dr Elias Muzoremba , vachinzwa zvichema zvavana chiremba ava .
Mutsamba yavo kuvatori venhau , vana chiremba ava vati vaudza hofisi yemutungamiri wenyika kuti iri kuudzwa zvisizvo nebhodhi rinofanira kugadzirisa zvichemo zvavo reHealth Services Board .
Vana chiremba ava vanoti vari kuda kuti hurumende igadzirise nyaya yekushomeka kwemishonga muzvipatara nezvimwe zvikwanisiro uye kuti vapihwe mari dzavanotambira nemadhora ekuAmerica sezvo mari dzemaRTGS dzisisina simba .
Pari zvino vana chiremba ava vari kutambira mazana matatu nemakumi maviri nemadhora mapgumbamwe pamwedzi .
Asi mari iyi inouya ari maRTGS .
Asi imwe nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfumi vachidzidzisa paNelson Mandela Metropolitan University , Muzvinafundo Gift Mugano , vaudza Studio 7 kuti hurumende haikwanise kubhadhara mari iyi zvachose nemamiriro akaita zvinhu .
Tabvunzawo Dr Mugano kuti sezvo makambani mamwe ave kubhadharisa nemadhora ekuAmerica pazvinhu zvavanotengesa pangaitwa sei kugadzirisa mari dziri kutambirwa navanachiremba .

Vakawanda munyika vari kuchema chemawo kuti makadhi emaHealth Insurance haasi kushanda uye pakutenga mishonga kuma pharmacy vari kunzi vauye nemadhora ekuAmerica zvapa kuti vangogume vogara kumba .
Chikwata chenyika chenhabvu chemaWarriors chasimuka chakananga kuSouth Africa kumakundano eCosafa .
Chikwata ichi chakatarisana nehondo mbiri mumakwikwi eCosafa Cup neye Africa Cup of Nations , ayo chinofanira kukunda zvine mutsindo kutanga neCosafa Cup neMugovera .
Pamusoro pekushandisa Cosafa Cup segadziriro yeAfcon , Zimbabwe inofanira zvekare kudzivivira mukombe uyu , uyo yakatora kechitanhatu gore rapera , ichitarisira kusimbisa zita rayo seshasha yenhabvu kuchamhembe kweAfrica zvekare gore rino .
Nemhaka yekushaikwa kwemari , Zimbabwe haina kukwanisa kuwana zvikwata zvekutamba nazvo mitambo yekuedzana masimba makundano eAfcon asati atanga zvekuti murairidzi wemaWarriors , Sunday Chidzambwa , ari kuti Cosafa ndiyo yatove nzira yekusimbisa chikwata chake .
Chidzambwa ari kudawo kuwedzera mbiri yake mumakwikwi eCosafa mushure mekuve murairidzi wekutanga kutora mukombe uyu kanokwana kana kubvira makundano aya avambwa muna 1997 .
Chidzambwa akatora mukombe weCosafa Cup muna 2003 , 2009 , 2017 na 2018 .
Vamwewo vatambi vemuZimbabwe saTendai Darikwa , Admiral Muskwe , naAlec Mudimu vari kudawo kuonekwa mumakwikwi eCosafa Cup aya ayo vaingonzwa nazvawo vasingazive kuti akamira sei .
Gore rino , Zimbabwe ine chikwata chakasimbisisa kudarika makore ese emakundano aya sezvo iri kushadisa chikwata chavo chiri kuenda kuAfcon kusanganisira vamwe vatambi vakaita sa Knowledge Musona , naMarvelous Nakamba .
Nhengo yeZimbabwe Warriors Fan Club , VaShingirai Miti , vanoti hapana kwikwidzo iripo kuCosafa nekuti mukombe uyu wagara uri weZimbabwe .
Akatora mukombe weCosafa , maWarriors ari kutarisra kudarika kekutanga kubva mugungano rawo kumakundano eAfcon ayo ari kusangana neEgypt mumutambo wawo wekutanga .
Mutambi wechikwata ichi , Ronald Pfumbidzai , anoti havasi kuenda kuEgypt kunowedzera zvikwata zvinenge zviriko .
Zimbabwe iri mugungano regroup A neEgypt , Democratic Republic of Congo ne Uganda umo maneja wema Warriors , VaWellington Mpandare , vane chivimbo chekuti vanobudamo .
Zimbabwe iri kusimuka kubva muSouth Africa panopera makundano eCosafa musi wa 8 Chikumi yakananga kuNigeria munzira yayo yekuenda kuAfcon kuEgypt .
Kune vanoita zvemitambo vakawanda , nguva yezororo reKisimisi inguva yekuonana nehama neshamwari , vamwe vachitorawo mukana uyu kuita zvakasiyana siyana .
Asi gore rino panguva iyo vamwe vari kushanyira hama neshamwari mushure megore rese vasingaonane , murairidzi weFC Platinum , Lizwe Sweswe , nechikwata chake havasi kuwana mukana wakadai sezvo vanenge vari muCairo , kuEgypt , mumutambo wavo nechikwata cheAl Ahly mumakwikwi eCaf Champions League .
Uyu unenge wave mutambo wechitatu weFC Platinum mumakwikwi aya , mushure mekurohwa 2 - 1 neAl Hilal yekuSudan mumutambo wekutanga , vachizokundwa zvakare 3 - 0 neEtoile duSahel yekuTunisia .
Sweswe anoti vachange vari pabasa vachishanda vachitarisarirawo kuti kisimisi ichavapa rombo rakanaka rekukunda mushure mekurohwa mumitambo yese miviri yavatamba mumakwikwi aya .
Mumwe murairidzi wenhabvu , Darlington Dodo weCaps United , anoti mushure mekutadza kutora mukombe weCastle Lager Premier Soccer League , ino ndiyo nguva yekugadzirisa paive pasina kumira zvakanaka .
Asi mukuru wekumahofisi eZimbabwe Olympic Committee , Muzvare Anna Mguni , vanoti vakananga kumusha kwavo kunoona hama neshamwari idzo vasina kuona kwenguva refu .
Mutambi webasketball , Nyarai Musambudzi , ane hurongwa hwakafana nehwaMuzvare Mguni asi iye anenge akananga kuMasvingo Murairidzi wechikwata cheTriangle , Taurayi Mangwiro , anoti kwaanoshandira kure nekunogara mhuri yake zvekuti panguva ino zvenhabvu zvave kumbomira achipa nguva kumhuri yake .
Izvi ndizvo zviri muhurongwa zvekare hwemutambi wechikwata chenyika chenetball , icho chakaita mukurumbira kuWorld Cup , Ursula Ndlovu , uyo anoti nguva yakawanda yakapera ari mukamba zvekuti ikozvino achange aine hama neshamwari dzake kuBulawayo vachifara pamwe chete .
Asi sachigaro weZimbabwe Volleyball Association , VaRingisai Mapondera , vanoti hapana chinodarika mutambo weVolleyball paKisimisi .
VaMapondera vanoti vachange vakaungana nehama neshamwari pamba pavo muHarare vachitamba mutambo uyu mukupemberera kwavo nguva ino .
Kune vamwewo vakaita saVaMapondera kusanganisira mutambi wetsiva , Charles Manyuchi , avo vari kuti vari kutora nguva ino kugadzirira zvakasimba mitambo yavo yemwaka unotevera vachitarisira goho rakasimba gore rinouya .
Asi vezvemitambo neZimbabwe yese vari kupinda muzororo panguva iyo zvinhu zvisina kumira zvakanaka munyaya dzemari , dambudziko riri kuratidza kuti hurumende iri kukundikana kurigadzirisa .
Sangano rinomiririra vadzidzisi vekumaruwa , reAmalgamated Rural Teachers Union of Zimbabwe , ARTUZ , rinoti razivisa hurumende kuti inofanirwa kugadzirisa zvichemo zvaro mukati memazuva gumi nemana , kutadza kwayo , ropinda mukuramwa mabasa .
Sangano iri rinoti riri kuda kuti mihoro yevadzidzisi inge iri mumadhora ekuAmerica , kana kuti ichibhadharwa nemari inowirirana nemazana mashanu emadhora ekuAmerica .
Gwaro reARTUZ rakasvitswa nemusi weChishanu mumaoko ehurumende kuburikidza nemapazi evashandi vehurumende , rePublic Service Commission nerezvemari .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa kudivi rehurumende panyaya iyi , sezvo gurukota rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , Amai Monica Mutsvangwa , vange vasiri kubatika panharembozha yavo .
Mutungamiri weARTUZ , VaObert Masaraure , vanoti sevarairidzi , vanodawo kurarama kwakanaka , asi hazvisi kuitika semadiro avo .
VaMasaraure vanoti kunyange hazvo hurumende ichiti iri kunetseka munyaya dzehupfumi , inogona kugadzirisa zvinhu kana ikarwisa huori mumapazi ayo , pamwe nekufambisa mari dzehurumende nenzira kwadzo .
VaMasaraure vanoti mari yakawanda yehurumende iri kupedzerwa muzvinhu zvisinganyanyobatsiri nyika zvakaita senzendo dzekunze kwenyika , kutenga zvikakarara zvemotokari nezvimwe zvinogona kumbosendekwa parutivi kutira kuti vashandi vehurumende vawane mihoro yakanaka .
VaMasaraure vanoti semaonero avo , munyika mune mari inogona kugadzirisa zvinhu zviri kunetsa , asi dambudziko riripo nderekuti homwe yenyika haisi kubatwa zvakanaka , uye havasi kuona chido chekugadzirisa zvinhu kubva kuvakuru vakuru muhurumende .
Vari kunze kwenyika vari kuchema - chema nekukwira kwaita mari yavanofanirwa kubhadhara kuitira kuti vawane mapasipoti matsva kana kumutsiridza anenge apera kushanda .

Vachitaura nevatori venhau , gurukota rezvemukati menyika , VaKazembe Kazembe , vakati bazi ravo rinoziva nezvetarisiro hombe ine vanhu yekuti ringe richidhinda mapasipoti nekukasika , uye kuti vanhu vari kutambura kuwana magwaro aya , zvikuru vari kunze kwenyika vanenge vaine magwaro apera kushanda .
VaKazembe vakati nekuda kuona kuti zvizvarwa zvenyika zviri kunze zvine magwaro akarongeka munyika dzazvigere , hurumende yakaona zvakakodzera kukwidza mutengo , uye magwaro aya achiburitswa nekukasika .
Asi vamwe vari kunze kwenyika vari kuona sekunge hurumende yatora danho iri kuti iunganidze mari yekunze .
Munhu anenge achitora pasipoti ari munyika anobhadhara mari inoita madhora makumi mashanu nematatu emaRTGS , kuchitiwo anoda inobuda mukati memazuva matau achibhadhariswa madhora emunyika mazana maviri nemakumi mashanu nematatu .
Anoda pasipoti inobuda mukati mezuva rimwechete anobhadhariswa madhora mazana matatu nemakumi masere .

Chikwata chenhabvu chevanhukadzi chemaMighty Warriors chatarisana nemutambo mukuru muhupenyu hwacho , zvekuti veruzhinji vari kuda kuti Zimbabwe ikunde kuitira kuti ipinde munhoroondo yemitambo munyika .
Hapana chimwe chiri kutarisirwa neveruzhinji kunze kwekukunda apo maMighty Warriors ari kupinda munhandare yeRufaro Stadium neSvondo mumutambo wavo mukuru kupinda yose kubvira muna 1980 apo Zimbabwe yakatanga kukwikwidza mune zvemitambo nedzimwe nyika .
Chikwata chenhabvu chevanhukadzi ichi chiri kusangana nemaIndomitable Lionesses ekuCameroon mumutambo ucharatidza kuti Zimbabwe iri kukwanisa kubudirira here kana kuti kwete kuenda kumakundano makuru ezvemitambo epasi rose emaOlympic Games ayo achaitirwa kuRio de Janeiro gore rinouya .
MaMighty Warriors akarohwa 2 - 1 apo zvikwata zviviri izvi zvakasangana muYaounde masvondo maviri apfuura asi vari kungoda kukunda 1 - 0 chete kuti vabudirire kuenda kumabiko emitambo epasi rose aya .
Vakabudirira kuenda kumakundano aya , ma Mighty Warriors anoita chikwata chechipiri mumakore makumi matatu nemashanu kukwikwidza kumakundano aya zvichitevera magolden hockey girls a 1980 .
Asi maMighty Warriors anopinda munhoroondo sechikwata chekutanga kukwikwidza nekubudirira kuenda kumakundano aya sezvo mahockey girls akaenda kuMoscow mushure mekukokwa zvikwata zvashota kukwikwidza .
Nhengo yeWarriors Fan Club , VaZivanai Moroyiwa , vanoti vanonokerwa nemutambo uyu vachiti ivo maMighty Warriors achafadza veruzhinji nekuita zvatadzwa kuitwa nechikwata kana chimwe chete zvacho pamakore makumi matatu nemashanu apfuura .
Muteveri wechikwata che Caps United , VaTonderayi Matimura , vanoti vachitarisa matambiro akaita maMighty Warriors apo zvikwata izvi zvakasangana masvondo maviri apfuura , vane chivimbo chekuti maMighty Warriors anodzora pamwe nekukunda zvekare .
VeZimbabwe Football Association vaona kukosha kwechaunga mumutambo uyu zvekuti varonga ivo kuti veruzhinji vabhadhare mari inoita iyo dhora rimwe chete rekuona mutambo wakakosha uyu .
Muongorori wezvemitambo , VaAndrew Rwodzi , vanoti vanhu vakawanda vachange vari munhandare iyi sezvo dhora iri mari yekuti munhu wese anokwanisa kubhadhara kuti aone mutambo wakakosha uyu .
Va Matimura vanoti vachange varimowo munhandare iyi sezvo dhora iri mari isingavaremere pane madhora matatu ayo anomboshevedzerwa neveZifa .
Murairidzi wechikwata ichi , Shadreck Mlauzi , avaka chikwata chakasimba zvikuru chinosanganisa vechikuru pamwe nevechidiki zvekuti ari kutarisira kuti vatambi vakaita sa Rudo Neshamba na Rutendo Machingura vachabaka moto neSvondo pamberi pevatsigiri vavo .
Panguva imwe cheteyo chikwata chemaWarriors chichange chiri muBabourfields Stadium umo chiri kusangana neLesotho mumutambo weAfrica Nations Championship uyo une huremu husingasvika pane mutambo wemaMighty Warriors .
Murairidzi wechikwata ichi , Kalisto Pasuwa , akadzinga vatambi vatatu Hardlife Zvirekwi na Justice Jangano veCaps United pamwe naRonald Chitiyo weDynamos nenyaya dzehunhubu asi VaMuroyiwa vanoti kunyange zvakadai maWarriors haamise tuzvikwata tudiki twakaita seLesotho .
MaWarrriors ari kutarisira kukunda mumitambo miviri iri kusangana zvikwata zviviri izvi kuti akwanise kuenda kumafainari eAfrica Nations Championships kechina kakateverana mushure mekuenda kumakundano a2009 , 2012 , na 2014 .
Asi maziso nepfungwa dzeveruzhinji dziri pamutambo wemaMighty Warriors .

VaHaruzivishe vanoti kusvika panguva yataenda pamhepo vanga vachiri pamapurisa kuti vaedze kuona kuti vanhu vangani vasungwa muchiitiko ichi , asi vanoti vanga vachiziva nezvemunhu mumwechete .

Hurumende yatiwo ine humbowo hwemavhidhiyo anoratidza vechidiki ava vachitema mapurisa , uhwo huchashandiswa mudare redzimhosva pakuroverera vakasungwa ava nemhosva .
Hatina kukwanisa kunzwa divi remapurisa panyaya iyi .
Rimwe sangano rinomirira zvizvarwa zveZimbabwe zviri kugara pamwe nekushanda muSouth Africa , reZimbabwe Community in South Africa , rinoti riri kushushikana zvikuru nekuwanda kwehumbavha mumisha inogara veruzhinji muJohannesburg dziri kuparwa nevanhu vanofungidzirwa kuti zvizvarwa zveZimbabwe .
Sangano iri rinoti mhosva idzi , idzo dziri kunyanya kuparwa mumisha yeHillbrow , Berea neYeoville uko kunogara zvizvarwa zvekune dzimwe nyika kusanganisira Zimbabwe zvakawanda , dzinosanganisira dzekubvuta , kubata kwiyo , kubaya nemapanga pamwe nekuponda .
Mutauriri wesangano reZimbabwe Community in South Africa , VaBongani Mkwananzi , vanoti vave kuronga kusangana nemapurisa kuti vasvitse nyunyuto iyi , uye kuti vakurudzire mapurisa kuti atore matanho akasimba pamusoro pedambudziko iri .
Vanoti musi wa 6 Kukadzi , unove mwedzi unouya , sangano ravo riri kutarisira kusangana nemapurisa anobata matunhu aya kuti vaise musoro pamwechete mukugadzirisa dambudziko iri .
Vanotiwo mapurisa anofanirwa kunge achichengetedza nzvimbo idzi , asi nguva zhinji haawanikwe , izvo zvinozoita kuti mbavha nemakororoaya vaite madiro aJojina .
VaMkwananzi vanoti vakawanda vari kubirwa vanotoziva vamwe vevanhu vari kupara dzimhosva idzi kuburikidza nemitauro yavo , zvekuti mapurisa akazvipira kurwisana nedambudziko iri anofanirwa kunge achishanda nezvizvarwa zveZimbabwe zvinogara munzvimbo idzi .
Vamwe vataurawo neStudio7 vari kukurudzira kuendeswa kwemauto munzvimbo idzi kuitira kuti amise kuparwa kwedzimhosva uku .
Zvizvarwa zvemuSouth Africa zvagara zvinopomera zvizvarwa zvekune dzimwe nyika mhosva yekuwedzera kuparwa kwedzimhosva , nyaya dzekutengeswa kwezvinodhaka , pamwewo nechipfambi .
Vanhu vakawanda vanoti gore ra2019 igore richapinda munhoorondo yemakore akaomera nyika mune zvematongerwo enyika pamwe nezveupfumi .
Mukati megore iri makaitikawo zvakawanda zvinoshungurudza vanhu , nezvimwewo zvinofadza vamwe .
Mukutanga kwegore ra2019 , mauto akapomerwa mhosva yekuuraya vanhu vanosvika gumi nevaviri mushure mekunge vanhu vapinda mumigwagwa vachida kuratidzira .
Vakawandawo vanorwira kodzero dzevanhu pamwe nevatungamiri vevashandi nevemapato anopikisa vanonzi vakasungwa pamwe nekushungurudzwa nemapurisa , vamwe vavo vachikandwa mumajeri .
Mapurisa anopomerwawo mhosva yekushandisa chisimba chakanyanya pakuparadza misangano yebato rinopikisa neMDC kwaaiita muna 2019 , uye kurambidza bato iri kuita misangano .
Munyaya dzezvehupfumi , hurumende yakadzika mutemo unorambidza kushandiswa kwemari yekunze .
Kunyange hazvo yakaisawo mari yemunyika yemhando yeRTGS vamwe vanoti hazvina zvazvakagadzirisa sezvo dambudziko remari rakaramba richipinga nyika ndare , izvo zviri kukonzera kusagadzikana mune zvehupfumi .
Zvipatara zvakapindawo dambudziko rekushaiwa vanachiremba kubva muna Gunyana kusvika pari zvino mushure mekunge varamwa mabasa vachida kuti hurumende igadzirise mihoro yavo .
Mutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa vakaumbawo zvakare dare revatungamiri vemapato akakwikwidza kusarudzo yemutungamiri wenyika , rePolitical Actors' Dialogue , POLAD , iro ravanoti ndiro riri kutungamira nhaurirano dzekugadzirisa zvinetswa zvemunyika .
Asi mutungamiri webato reMDC , VaNelson Chamisa vakaramba kupinda muPOLAD vachiti vanongoda nhaurirano pakati pavo naVaMnangagwa chete , kwete nemapato asina chaakakohwa musarudzo .

Muimbi akaita mukurumbira pasi rose , Dorothy Masuka , ashaya .
Masuka , uyo akaberekerwa muZimbabwe muna 1935 , ashaya ari pamba pake muJohannesburg kuSouth Africa .
Muzukuru waMasuka , Fortune Hute , audza Studio7 kuti ambuya vake vanga vachinetseka nechirwere High Blood Pressure .
Masuku aive mwana wechina mumba maive nevana vanomwe .
Akaenda kuSouth Africa ave nemakore gumi nemaviri , uko akanotanga kuimba achiri mwana wechikoro .
Panguva iyi ndipo akatanga kufarira musambo weJazz .
Ava nemakore gumi nematanhatu , akasiya chikoro ndokunoimba nechikwata chaPhilemon Mogotsi che African Ink Sports , icho chairidza chiri muDurban .
Asi haana kugara kwenguva yakareba nechikwata ichi muDurban zvichitevera kusungwa kwaakaitwa ndokudzoserwa kuJohannesburg nehurumende yerusarura ganda yaitonga South Africa munguva iyi .
Nepamusana pekunetswa nehurumende yechichena mu South Africa , Masuka akatiza munyika iyi achidzokera kuBulawayo , uko akanoshanda nechikwata che Golden Rhythm Crooners .
Nekupindana kwemakore , Masuka akabatana naHugh Masekela naMiriam Makeba vachiimba musambo weJazz vari kunze kweSouth Africa .
Muna 1961 , Masuka akakokwa kunoimbira VaPatrice Lumumba kuDemocratic Republic of Congo .
Izvi hazvina kufadza hurumende yevachena muSouth Africa , izvo zvakaita kuti Masuka asatsike gumbo rake muSouth Africa kwemakore makumi matatu nerimwe .
Panguva iyi Masuku akashanda ari munyika dzinoti Malawi , Tanzania neZambia , asi nguva zhinji yake aive muZambia , akazodzokera kuSouth Africa muna 1992 zvichitevera kuburitswa mujeri kwaVaNelson Mandela .
Muna 1990 Masuka akaburitsa dambarefu rakanetsa zvikuru rinonzi Pata Pata .

Bazi rezvehutano rinoti huwandu hwevanhu vafa nekuda kwechirwere cheCovid - 19 munyika hwakwira kusvika pagumi nevasere kana kuti 18 mushure mekunge vamwe vanhu vashanu vashaya .

Izvi zvinotevera kubatwa kwevamwe vanhu vatatu nechirwere ichi nezuro .
Pavanhu ava , vaviri vakabva kuSouth Africa uye mumwe akachitapurirwa munyika .
Harare ndiyo ine vanhu vakawandisa vabatwa nechirwere ichi vanosvika mazana maviri nemakumi masere nemasere kana kuti 288 ichiteverwa neBulawayo ine vanhu zana nemakumi masere nevatatu 183 , Mashonaland Central ndiyo ine vanhu vashoma vabatwa nechirwere ichi vanova gumi nemumwe .

Vanhu vavhenekwa chirwere ichi munyika vadarika zviuru makumi masere nezvisere kana kuti 88 000 .

MaGreen Machine ave kusangana neTP Mazembe yekuDRC munharaunda inotevera .
Zvakamira zvakadai , Ngezi Platinum Stars iri kuitawo mabiko mushure mekunge chikwata ichi chakarova Pamplemouses yekuMauritius 1 - 0 ndokuenderera mberi nemakundano eCaf Confederation Cup , 2 - 1 mumitambo miviri .
Ngezi Platinum Stars iyo iri kutamba muAfrica kekutanga yave kusangana ne CD Libolo yekuAngola munharaunda inotevera umo varikutarisira kukunda zvekare .
Murairidzi weNgezi Platinum Stars , Tonderayi Ndiraya , anoti anovimba kuti vatambi vake vacharamba vakadaro kusvika makundano aya asvika kwamvura yacheka makumbo .

Sangano reWomen of Dominion riinoti rine hurongwa hwekuti riwanire mushonga vanhu vanorarama nehusope muZimbabwe .
Mishonga iyi yakanangana nekudzivirira kuti vanorarama nehusope vasaite chiwere chegomarara .
Women of Dominion inounza pamwe chete madzimai ari mumakereke akasiyana siyana muAmerica nemuZimbabwe uye rinoita misangano kamwe chete pagore .
Gore rino musangano uyu wakaitirwa kuDelaware .
Vachitaura pamucheto wemusangano uyu , vanowona nezvekufambiswa kwezvirongwa mugungano remadzimai iri , Doctor Natsai Zhou vanoti sangano ravo riri kushanda nevamwe vanamazvikokota munyika kuitira kuti pawanikwe mishonga inobatsira vanorarama nehusope inoshanda uye ichitengeka nyore .
Mubatanidzwa uyu wakange uri wemazuva mana wakaipindwa nemadzimai emuZimbabwe anobva muAmerica , Canada , Britain nevashoma vakabva kuZimbabwe kwekare .
"""" Taimbo kurudzira kuti madzimai anouya kumisangano yedu vaunze mishonga , nguwani dzekupfeka nemagirazi ekudzivirira zuva .
Asi parizvino tirikuona kuti mishonga iyi haisi kunyatso batsira vanorarama nehusope .
Shuwiro yedu ndeyekuti titsvage vanogadzira mishonga iyi kumusha kuitira kuti mitengo idzike uye kuti tigadzirise zvinoenderana nemararamiro anoita vanorarama nehusope munyika , """" Doctor Zhou vaudza Studio 7 .
Mumwe mudzimai anorarama nehusope amai Spelile Machingamidze vanoti mishonga iriko parizvino iri kudhura .
Vanoti danho iri rakanaka zvikuru sezvo richabatsira kuti nyanzvi dzemunyika dzikwanise kugadzira mafuta anoenderana navo asingadure asi zvizhinji zvinozoda kuti zviitwe kuti mafuta aya anyatsoshanda kwavari .
Amai Spelile Machingamidze vanorarama nehusope vanoti parizvino mishonga inonyatsokuvabatsira irikudhura uye inogadzirwa munyika ichirikuda kuti inyatsogadziriswa kuti ishande zvakanaka .
"""" Tinotambira danho ririkuda kutorwa nesangano reWomen Of Dominion International iri nekuti vakakwanisa kuwana vanogadzira mishonga iyi zvine hunyanzvi zvinokwanisa kuti batsira zvakanyanya . """"
Amai Machingamidze vakaudza Studio 7 .
Sangano rePremier Soccer League , PSL , rinoti riri kuda kushandura nguva inotanga mitambo yenhabvu munyika sezvinoitwa kune dzimwe nyika dzinotanga mutambo uyu muna Nyamavhuvhu .
Kwemakore makumi mana nhabvu yemuZimbabwe yanga ichiramba kuita shanduko ichitanga mitambo muna Kurume kusvika muna Mbudzi kwete kutanga muna Nyamavhuvhu kusvika muna Chivabvu sezvinongoitwawo kune dzimwe nyika pasi rese .
Asi vanoziva zviri kuitika muPSL vanoti chirwere cheCoronavirus ndicho chamanikidza shanduko mumaitiro aya zvekuti vanotungamira gungano iri vari kuda kuti mitambo yemuno itevere nzira yemitambo yepasi rese kutanga mwaka uno .
Zvikwata zvakatopedza kunyoresa vatambi vazvo vemwaka uno nePSL neChipiri kugadzirira kuzotanga kwemitambo .
Mukuru wekumahofisi ePSL , VaKennedy Ndebele , vanoti vari kutarisa nzira dzese dzinokwanisa kuti mitambo itambwe kusanganisira kutanga muna Nyamavhuvhu .
Asi VaNdebele vabuda pachena kuti pari zvino havakwanise kubuda nechisungo chakasimba chekutanga kwemitambo iyi sezvo pasina anoziva kuti Coronavirus iyi ichatisvitsa kupi .
Muna 1997 vePSL vakamboda kuita kuti mitambo iyi itange muna Nyamavhuvhu ichipera muna Chivabvu , asi zvakakona nekuti dzinhandare dzemuno dzaive dzisina zvekudhonzesa mvura zvakakwana kana kuchinge kwanaya .
Asi dzinhandare dziri kugadziriswa dzichitarisirwa kuve dzapera muna Nyamavhuvhu .
VaNdebele vanoti vachaita musangano sekanzuru yePSL kana zvinhu zvichinge zvajeka nezvechirwere ichi kuona kuti mitambo vanoifambisa sei .
Nhabvu pamwe nemimwe mitambo yese yakambomiswa nemhaka yeCoronavirus izvo zviri kunzi nemuteveri wemutambo uyu , VaJustice Muzanenhamo , zvinobatsira kuti chirwere ichi chisapararire .
Vachitarisa matengerwo anga achiitwa vatambi nezvikwata , muongorori wemutambo wenhabvu , VaKelvin Mushonga , vanoti mitambo ichanakidza zvikuru apo ichatanga .
PSL yakamirira kunzwa kune vanoipa mari veDelta Beverages kuti makwikwi emwaka uno achange aine mari yakawanda zvakadii .
Chikwata cheFC Platinum chirikuvhura makundano enhabvu egore rino asi paine mibvunzo .
Vanotevera mutambo wenhabvu havasi kugutsikana nematambiro arikuita FC Platinum pamusha payo mumitambo yeCaf Champions League vakatarisana nemutambo mukuru neOrlando Pirates yekuSouth Africa iyo yakatora mukombe uyu muna 1995 .
Nhoroondo yenhabvu muAfrica inotaura kuti zvikwata zvinokunda nemutsindo pamusha ndizvo zvinowanzoenderera mberi nemakundano asi matambiro eKugona Kunenge Kudada muMandava Stadium asimudza mibvunzo mumukana wavo wekusvika kuma kota fainari .
FC Platinum yakatatarika zvinotyisa neCnaps yekuMadagascar ndokuzokunda 1 - 0 mumutambo uyo vaitarisirwa kukanda zvibodzwa pamadiro , ndokuzoita zvekare mangange 0 - 0 ne Otoyo Oho yekuCongo .
Muteveri wenhabvu VaFrancis Mwendamberi vanoti Kugona Kunenge Kudada inofanira kuwedzera mwando pamatambiro ayo pamusha kana ichida kubudirira mumakwikwi aya .
Pamusoro peOrlando Pirates , FC Platinum iri mugungano rimwechete ne Esperance yekuTunisia iyo ine mukombe uyu pamwe ne Horoya yeku Guinea .
Zvikwata zviviri zvinopedza zviri pamusoro mugungano iri ndizvo zvinoenderera mberi nemakwikwi aya .
Muteveri wechikwata cheDynamos VaObert Masvotore vanoti FC Platinum isatarise mazita kana mukurumbira une zvikwata zvavari kusangana nazvo .
Mumwe muteveri wemutambo uyu VaTatenda Makazhu ndivo vanofunga kuti Kugona Kunenge Kudada inokwanisa kusvika mufainari yemakundano aya .
Asi murairidzi wePirates Milutin Sredojevic audza mapepanhau ekuSouth Africa kuti ari kutya kutamba nechikwata cheFC Platinum nenyaya yekuti chikwata chitsva mumakundano aya uye ati anoremekedza murairidzi wacho Norman Mapeza zvakanyanya .
Ati sezvo Pirates iri kutamba neFC Platinum mumutambo wekutanga kuMandava Stadium kuZvishavane , zvinonetsa zvikuru kuenda iko nemugwagwa .
Asi Pirates iri kubheja kuti inosimudza mukomb weChampions League kechipiri munhoroondo yayo .
Asi FC Platinum ichange isina mutambi akatamba zvinonwisa mvura mwaka uno kana kuti Soccer Star of the Year , Rodwell Chinyengetere , uyo ave kuenda kunotambira Baroka FC ku South Africa naWinston Mhango uyo arikuenda kuSouth Africa zvekare .
Kugona Kuenge Kudada irikutarisira kusvika kana kudarika chidanho chakasvikwa neDynamos iyo yakasvika mufainari yeCaf Champions League muna 1998 nemuma semi finari muna 2008 .
Mhuri yemuAmerica iri kucherechedza zuva remagamba , reVeterans Day , apo nyika iyi inoremekedza pamwe nekurangarira magamba akarwa muhondo dzakasiyanasiyana ari pasi pemauto enyika iyi .
Mutungamiri wenyika iyi , VaDonald Trump , vari kuNew York , uko kuri kuitwa mhemberero huru , uye vaisawo maruva muMadison Square kuremekedza vakarwa hondo ava .
Zuva remagamba iri rinocherechedzwa musi wa11 Mbudzi gore roga - roga zvizvarwa zvenyika iyi zvichitenda magamba anodarika mamiriyoni gumi nemapfumbamwe akarwa muhondo dzakasiyanasiyana nenzira dzakasiyanasiyana .
Pazuva iri vamwe vezvitoro vanoderedza mitengo yezvinhu zvavo kana vachitengesera vakarwa hondo kana vakamboshanda muchiuto , vamwewo vezvitoro vachicherechedza kusanganisira vachiri muchiuto .
Chimwe chizvarwa cheZimbabwe chiri muno muAmerica , Doctor Wangu Mazodze , avo vanoongorora zvematongerwo enyika , vanoti nyika yeAmerica inokoshesa magamba ayo zvakanyanya zvichienzaniswa neZimbabwe .
Doctor Mazodze vanoti musiyano mukuru uri pakuti kuZimbabwe vakarwa hondo yerusununguko vakaiswa muhapwa dzevezvematongerwo enyika zvekuti vave kushandiswa nevemapato ezvematongerwo enyika , asi ukatarisa muAmerica , vakarwa hondo vese vanomirira nyika , kwete mapato ezvematongerwo enyika .
Dzimba dzakavakwa nebazi reUnited States Centers for Disease Control and Prevention riri muZimbabwe , pachishandiswa homwe ye United States President's Emergency Plan for AIDS and Relief ( PEPFAR ) , dziri kupa mukana wekuti vanhu vaongororwe zvine chiremera ropa ravo kana riine hutachiona hweHIV .
Bazi re Centers for Disease Control riri kuita chirongwa ichi rakabatana nebazi rezvehutano .
Dzimba idzi dzinonzi muchirungu Porta Cabins dzakavakirwa kuwanisa makirinika nzvimbo dzakasununguka dzekuvheneka ropa kuti rionekwe kuti rine HIV here kana kuti kwete .
Nhepfenyuro yeStudio7 yakashanyira chimwe chipatara chekanzuru cheAmaveni muKwekwe icho chinova chezvimwe zvezvipatara zvakavakirwa zvivakwa izvi .
Mumwe wevana mukoti vari pachipatara cheAmaveni apa , Amai PatriciaTendai Shumba , vanoti kubva pakavakwa ma cabin aya , huwandu hwevanhu vari kuoongororwa ropa hwawedzera .
Mumwe wevanamukoti pakirinika yeAmaveni iyi , avo vakaongorora ropa rameya weKwekwe , VaMatenda Madzoke , pamberi pevatori venhau senzira yekukurudzira veruzhinji kuti vaongororwe ropa ravo , Amai Loice Chikono , vanoti vanhu vasatya kuongororwa ropa ravo sezvo kwave nemapiritsi anoraramisa veruzhinji .
VaMadzoke vanoti kuvakwa kwema cabin uku kuri kubatsira zvikuru vagari vemuguta ravo .
Vanotiwo kuvakwa kwezvivakwa izvi kunzvimbo yakavandika kunopawo mukana kune avo vanonyara kuonekwa neruzhinji vachivhenekwa ropa kana kutora mapiritsi .
VaMadzoke vanotiwo pamakirinika mashanu ekanzuru ari muguta reKwekwe , maviri ndiwo chete ane ma cabin aya .
Vanotiwo shuviro yavo ndeyekuti makirinika eguta ravo ese awane pakasununguka pekuongororera vanhu ropa .
Padandemudande rayo , muzinda weAmerica muZimbabwe unoti pasi pechirongwa ichi kwakavakwa ma porta cabins zana nemakumi mana munzvimbo dzakasiyasiyana munyika .
Zimbabwe , sedzimwe nyika pasi rese , iri kurwisawo kupedza dambidziko reHIV / AIDS panosvika gore ra2030 .
Magwaro akabudiswa neZIMSTAT muna 2015 anoratidza kuti huwandu hwevanhu vane neHIV / AIDS hwuri kudzikira munyika .
Mutungamiri wenyika , VaRobert Mugabe , vakadomwa nesangano reWorld Health Organisation , WHO , semunyarikani achange akamirira Africa munyaya dzezvirwere zvisingatapuriranwe , kana kuti non communicable diseases .
VaMugabe , avo vane makore makumi mapfumbamwe nematu , vakadomwa mazuva maviri apfuura pamusangano uri kuitirwa ku Uruguay .
VaMugabe vakaenda kumusangano uyu vachiperekedzwa negurukota nezvekunze , VaWalter Mzembi , gurukota rezvehutano , VaDavid Parirenyatwa , pamwe nemamwe makurokota ehurumende .
Vachitaura vari kuUruguay , VaMzembi vaudza Studio7 kuti ichokwadi kuti VaMugabe vadomwa semunyarikani izvo zviri kufadza nyika .
"""" Ichokwadi VaMugabe vawana ruremekedzo rwekuve , WHO Ambassador for NCD's , Africa , """" VaMzembi vaudza Studio7 .
VaMugabe vachange vari pachinzvimbo ichi kwemakore maviri , uye basa iri haribhadharwe mari .
Asi dzimwe nyanzvi munyaya dzehutano dzinoti dziri kushamiswa nezvaitwa neWHO zvekudoma mutungamiri ari kukundikana kugadzirisa nyaya dzehutano munyika make izvo zviri kupa kuti vakuru vakuru muZimbabwe varapwe kunze kwenyika .
VaMugabe pachavo vanogara vachibuda munyika vachinorapwa kuSingapore .
Mumwe mutongi wedare reHigh Court muBulawayo apa mutongo wekuti mapurisa anofanirwa kuunza kudare mukati memazuva matatu anotevera VaTawanda Muchehiwa avo vasingaziikanwe kuti varipi mushure mekunge vasungwa nemapurisa nemusi weChina .
Mutongi wedare reHigh Court , Justice Martin Makonese , vapa mutongo uyu zvichitevera chikumbiro chechimbi - chimbi chaitwa negweta , VaNqobani Sithole , chekuti mapurisa aunze VaMuchehiwa kudare .
VaMuchehiwa muzukuru wemutapi wenhau Mduduzi Mathuthu uyo ari kudiwa nemapurisa .
VaSithole vati vaita chikumbiro ichi nekuti VaMuchehiwa havazi kuziikanwa kwavari kubva musi wavakasungwa nemusi weChina chapfuura , pamwe chete nedzimwe hama mbiri dzaMathuthu .
VaSithole vati dzimwe hama mbiri idzi dzave kumba mushure mekuregerwa nemapurisa .
Mathuthu , uyo anove mupepeti webepanhau repadandemutande rinonzi ZimLive , ari kupomerwa mhosva yekukurudzira mhirizhonga .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kutaura naMathuthu , sezvo vanhu vasiri kuziva kuti aripi , kunyange hazvo ari kugara akaburitsa zviri kuitika padandemutande rake reTwitter .
Mutevedzeri wemutauriri webato reMDC Alliance , VaClifford Hlatywayo , vati pane nhengo dzavo dzine chitsama dzakasungwa munzvimbo dzakasiyana - siyana munyika mose nezuro iro raive zuva rakange rakarongwa kuratidzira munyika mose .
VaHlatywayo vatiwo vamwe vanhuwo zvavo vakashungurudzwa kana kurohwa nemapurisa nevechiuto munzvimbo dzakasiyana - siyana munyika .
Tabata mutauriri wemapurisa , Assistant Commissioner Paul Nyathi , kuti tinwe kuti kune vanhu vangani vakasungwa munyika nezuro uye kuti kune vakamhang'ara here kuti vakarohwa nemapurisa nemasoja vakati tizovafonera mushure mekanguva .
Patazoedza kunzwa kwavari zvekare nharembozha yavo yange isingachabatike .
Mune imwewo nyaya kunyange hazvo vanhu vange vari vashoma pane mamwe mazuva , nhasi zvitoro , mabhangi , nemamwe mabhizimisi zvange zvakavhura vanhu vachiita mabasa avo semazuva ose uye mudhorobha mange muine masoja nemapurisa mashoma .
Mumwe mugari anotengesa mune chimwe chitoro chinotengesa zvekudya kusanganisira muriwo nezvimwe zvirimwa , uyo angozvidoma nezita rekuti Amai Tanaka , ati akwanisa kuuya kubasa pasina kunetseka .
Mumwewo mugari uyo angozvidoma nezita rekuti James , uyo anotengesa muriwo nezvimwe pamusika wemuna Fifth Avenue ati akwanisawo kupinda mudhorobha pasina kunetseka kunyange hazvo kwange kuine maroadblock mumugwagwa waanoshandisa kupinda mudhorobha .
Sangano re 31st July Movement rakanga rakurudzira kuti vanhu vapinde mumigwagwa vachiratidzira nezuro , asi murongi wekuratidzira uku , VaJacob Ngarivhume , vakabva vasungwa ndokunyimwa mukana wekubvisa mari yechibatiso .
Chikumbiro chekuti vapihwe mukana uyu chava kuknzwikwa nedare repamusoro nemusi weMuvhuro .
Mutungamiri weMDC - T , VaMorgan Tsvangirai , vari kukurudzira kuti munyika muitwe hurukuro dzekuyedza kugadzirisa nyaya yehupfumi nezvematongerwo enyika izvo zvisina kumira zvakanaka munyika .
Vachitaura neStudio7 neMuvhuru , VaTsvangirai vati rwendo rwuno vanoda kuti nhaurirano idzi dzive chete dzevana veZimbabwe pasina vavakidzani kana vamwe vekunze vanopindira .
VaTsvangirai vati vana veZimbabwe vanofanirwa kugara pasi vega pasina veSADC , African Union neUnited Nations vanenge vachipindira votaurirana chokwadi chinofanirwa kuitwa .
VaTsvangirai , avo vakanga vari muhurumende yemubatanidzwa neZanu PF kwemakore mashanu vanoti zviri pachena kuti Zanu PF yakundikana zvayakavimbisa musarudzo nokudaro zvizvarwa zvenyika zvinofanirwa kuchigara pasi zvozeya gwara rekutora .
VaTsvangirai , avo vaiva mutungamiri wehurumende asina masimba muhurumende yemubatanidzwa vanoti zvinhu hazvina kumira zvakanaka muzvinhu zvose munyika kubva kudzidzo kusvika kuhupfumi .
Asi mutauriri weZanu - PF , VaRugare Gumbo , vanoti hapana chiri kunetsa munyika chingape kuti hurumende ye Zanu - PF igare pasi nemapato anopikisa kuti vagadzirise .
Asi VaTsvangirai vanoti vanhu vose vavari kutaura navo vari kubvuma kuti vanoda kuti vatungamiri vezvematongerwo enyika vaite mubatira pamwe chuma chemuzukuru padambudziko rakatarisana nenyika .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzehupfumi dzinoti kunyange hazvo mitengo yezvinhu yadzikira munyika , vanhu havana mari yekuti vatenge zvinhu izvi .
Gavhuna vebhanga guru renyika reReserve Bank of Zimbabwe Doctor John Mangudya vanoti Zimbabwe haisi kuzobatabata mari dzinobva kunze kwenyika uye vari kurwisa kudzikisa kukwira kwemitengo yezvinhu .
Vachitura hurongwa hwekufambiswa kwemari kana kuti Monetary Policy Statement , Doctor Mangudya vati hurumende haina chidokwadokwa chekubatabata mari dzinotumirwa kubva kunze kwenyika , uye vati vanenge vatumirwa mari idzi vakasununguka kuita zvavanoda nadzo .
VaMangudya vatiwo vari kushandawo kuona kuti mitengo yezvinhu zvakasiyana - siyana hairambi ichikwira , vachiti panozopera gore vari kutarisira kuti inflation inge yadzika kusvika pazvikamu makumi mashanu kubva muzana .
Gavhuna vebhanga guru ava vatiwo vari kufadzwa nerwendo rwatorwa nenyika mukuzvirumura kubva mukushandisa madhora ekuAmerica .
VaMangudya vati zvinotora makore kuti nyika ibude mukushandisa mari yekunze kwenyika uye hazvigoneki nenguva pfupi .
Vati pari zvino zvikamu makumi matatu nezvinomwe kubva muzana zvemari iri mumabhanga imari yekunze asi zvikamu makumi matanhatu nezvitatu kubva muzana yave mari yemuno .
VaMangudya vati vanotarisira kuti mari dzekunze dziri mumabhanga dzirambe dzichiderera zvishoma nezvishoma .
Imwe nyanzvi mune zvehupfumi , VaPersistance Gwanyanya , yaudza Studio 7 kuti panoda kushandwa zvakanyanya kuti zvishuviro zvebhanga guru zvekuona kuti mitengo yadzika zvazadzikiswa .
VaGwanyanya vabvumiranawo naVaMangudya kuti zvinoda makore kuti Zimbabwe izonyatsoti yabuda mukushandisa mari yekunze kwenyika .
Imwe nyanzvi mune zvehupfumi vari nhengo yeMDC , VaTapiwa Mashakada , vatiwo kusabatwabatwa kwe mari dzevanhu dzinobva kunze ndizvo zvinototarisirwa , sezvo bumbiro remitemo yenyika risingazvibvumidzi kuita izvi .
Vati RBZ inofanirwa kuramba ichiremekedza izvi .
Asi VaMashakada vati havaoni hurumende ichibudirira mukudzikisa mitengo yezvinhu nekuda kwekuchinjiwa kwemari mumigwagwa , vachiti maonero avo ndeekuti mitengo icharamba ichikwira .
Kunyangwe hazvo mabhanga nevanemarezinesi ekuita izvi vari ivo vanofanirwa kuchinja mari pamutemo , vanhu vazhinji vanonochinja mari dzavo dzekunze kwenyika mumigwagwa nekuti vanowana mari yakawanda kudarika yavanopiwa mumabhanga .
VaMangudya vati mitengo yezvinhu iri kunyanyokwidzwa nemafungiro everuzhinji , kunyanya vachitoredzera zvakamboitika , asi vakurudzira veruzhinji kuti vachitarisa zvemberi kwete shure kwakabviwa .
Sechave chigariro musoro wetsuro kushaya nyanga , mutengo wemafuta ekufambisa dzimotokari wakwidzwa zvakare kutanga munyika yose .
Boka rinoongorora pamwe nekutara mitengo yemafuta edzimotokari , reZimbabwe Energy Regulatory Authority , ZERA , rakazivisa neSvondo usiku kuti mutengo wemafuta uyu unenge uchizosiyana zvichienderana nemadhorobha nemaguta , uchidhurisisa kunzvimbo dziri kure .
Semuenzaniso , peturu muHarare yakwira kubva paRTGS $ 9 . 12 kuenda paRTGS $ 10 . 1 parita , dhiziri richikwirawo kubva paRTGS $ 9 . 36 kuenda paRTGS $ 10 . 32 parita .
Asi mitengo iyi yakasiyana nemitengo yekuBulawayo sezvo rita repeturu rave kutengeswa nemari inoita $ RTGS10 . 39 , kuchitiwo dhiziri richiita $ RTGS10 . 69 parita .
Mitengo yekuVictoria Falls ndiyo inenge iri pamusorosoro munyika yose sezvo rita redhiziri rakwidzwa kuenda paRTGS $ 10 . 86 parita , kuchitiwo peturu yave kuita RTGS $ 10 . 56 parita .
ZERA yazivisa kuti mitengo iyi yasiyaniswa pachitariswa mutengo wekusvitsa mafuta aya kunzvimbo dzakasiyanasiyana idzi .
Vemichovha inotakura veruzhinji vanoti mitengo iyi ichavaomesera zvikuru sezvo ivo vachamanikidzwa kukwidzawo mari dzinoripirwa nevanhu vanenge vachifamba zvichienderana nekuti vanenge vachienda kunzvimbo dzipi .
Munyori anoona nezvemabasa musangano revemichovha reGreater Harare Association of Commuter Omnibus Operators , VaCaleb Dominic Bepeta , vanoti chiri kunetsa ndechekuti mitengo iri kungokwira asi mihoro yevanhu vavanotakura isina kwairi kuenda .
Zimbabwe yabatana nedzimwe nyika dzemu Africa mukucherechedza zuva re Africa Day vanhu vachiita zvirongwa zvakasiyana siyana .
Mukupembererera zuva reAfrica Day , mudzimai wemutungamiri weMDC , Amai Elizabeth Tsvangirai , vashanyira musha weBumhudzo Old People Home kuSt Mary's Chitungwiza uko kwavanopa zvekudya , zvekupfeka nemachira kuvakweguri vanogara pamusha uyu .
Vachitenda Amai Tsvangirai nerubatsiro rwavapiwa , Gogo Betty Samombe , mumwe wevakweguri vanogara paBumhudzo , vati vane tarisiro yekuti nhamo yavo yezvekudya yombotapudzika .
Amai Tsvangirai , avo vakakurira mumusha we St Mary's , vatiwo nekuda kwekuondomoka kuri kuita hupfumi hwenyika , vanhu vazhinji vari kutambura .
Amai Tsvangirai vatiwoshuviro yavo ndeyekuti vanhu vasaise zvematongerwo enyika mukati munyaya dzekubatsira vanoshaya .
Amai Tsvangirai vakurudzira kuti vanhu varangarire kwavakakurira vakati machechi ane mukurumbira abatsirewo veruzhinji vari kutambura .
Vanotungamirira Bumhudzo Old People's Home , Major Cynthia Nyaruberu , vati vakatarisana nematambudziko akasiyana - siyana nekuda kwemamiriro ehupfumi .
Amai Nyaruberu vati pamusoro pedambudziko rezvekudya , Bumhudzo , iyo yakavakwa gore ra1974 , yasakara zvikuru zvokuti vanotoda kubatsirwa kunatsurudza nzvimbo iyi .
Musha weBumhudzo une vakweguri makumi matatu nemumwe , uye mukurisa aripo ane makore zana nemashanu .
Bato reMDC inotungamirwa naVaMorgan Tsvangirai , rinoti zuva re Africa Day izuva rekucherechedza magamba akarwira kusunungura dunhu re Africa , iro rakatarisana nehudzvanyirira munguva iyo vanhu vachiti vakazvisunungura .
MDC inoti mukurangarira zuva ranhasi , pane mufaro pamwe nekusuwa kuri muvanhu vemuAfrica .
Bato iri rati Africa ine hupfumi hwakanyanyisa , asi zvinoshamisa ndezvekuti Africa ine vanhu varombo vakawanda , avo vanorarama nemari iri pasi pedhora pazuva .
Bato iri rapedzisira richiti Africa inofanirwa kubatsira Zimbabwe kuti iite sarudzo dzakachena gore rinouya .
Vashandi vekanzuru yeChitungwiza vanoti vatanga kushanda zvishoma nezvishoma kuitira kuti vakuru veguta vanzwe zvichemo zvavo uye kuti paitwe hurukuro nekanzuru .
Mutungamiri wesangano rinomirira vashandi vekanzuru , reChitungwiza Municipal Workers Union , VaEphraim Katsina , vaudza Studio7 kuti vashandi ava , avo vanosanganisira vana mukoti , havana kuramwa mabasa asi vachashanda zvishoma nezvishoma .
VaKatsina vati vashandi vanoda mbatya dzekuzvidzivirira kubva kuzvirwere kana vari pabasa , vachiti vamwe vashandi vari kufamba mamaira matanhatu kuenda kubasa sezvo makombi asiri kufamba zvakakwana pamusoro pekutevedzera kwawo mitemo yakadzikwa nehurumende yekurwisana nehutachiwona hweCoronavirus .
Vatizve vashandi havana mari yavari kutambiriswa .
VaKatsina vati vanokurudzira kanzuru kuti igare pasi nevashandi kuti vaite hurukuro dzinobatsira vanhu vese vemuguta , kwete kutyityidzira nekutuka vashandi kwavanoti kuri kuitwa nevamwe vakuru mukanzuru .
Asi vakafanobata chigaro chemunyori weguta , Dr Tonderai Kasu , vati havakwanisi kutaura nesu pamusoro penyaya iyi .
Asi vatumira gwaro rinoti zviri kuitwa nevashandi ava hazvisi pamutemo , vachiti hurumende yakagara yavimbisa kuti ichapa vashandi vezvehutano mbatya dzekuzvidzivirira vachiti vashandi vamhanyira kumbomira kushanda .
Chimwe chizvara chemuZimbabwe chakasarudzwa kuva kanzura mune rimwe dhorobha remunyika yeSweden chinoti , panofanirwa kuve nemafungiro matsva mune zvematongerwo enyika muZimbabwe kuitira kuti pasave nekupokana kunounza mhirizhonga kana kudeuka kweropa , zvisinei kuti vanhu vanotsigira mapato akasiyana - siyana .
VaTichaona Maphosa murume ane makore makumi mana nerimwe uye ndikanzura webato reSwedish Social Democratic Party , mudhorobha reUmea riri kumaodzanyemba kwakadziva kumabvazuva kwenyika yeSweden .
VaMaphosa vakatanga kuenda kunotsvaga mikana iri nani kunze kwenyika vachangopedza chikoro mugore ra1997 apo vakaenda kuAmerica asi vakadzoka kumusha mushure megore nekuda kwetsaona yaive yaitika mumhuri mavo .
Vagara munyika kwemakore ane chitsama VaMaphosa vakazowana mukana wekuenda kuSweden , asi sevamwe vanhu vakawanda vanotsvaga mafuro manyoro kunze kwenyika , vakashanda kubva pasi kuti vasvike pavari iko zvino .
Kunze kwekuita basa ravo rekutonga maguta kana kuti city planner VaMaphosa vanoratidza chido chikuru chekuita mabasa anobatsira vamwe vanhu .
Vanoti vakawana mukana wekupinda mune zvematongerwo enyika nekuti vaigara vachisangana nevamwe vebato reSwedish Social Democratic Party avo vakazovakumbira kuti vakwikwidze pachigaro chehukanzura muguta ravanogara gore rapera .
Pakuverengwa kwakaitwa vanhu munyika mugore ra2012 , Zimbabwe ine vanhu mamiriyoni gumi nematatu asi gwaro reWorld Bank rakabudiswa muna 2016 rinoti nyika ine vanhu mamiriyoni gumi nematanhatu .
Hapana mafigiri akajeka ehurumende anoratidza kuti zvizvarwa zvingani zvemuZimbabwe zviri kune dzimwe nyika asi zvinofungidzirwa kuti vanhu vanopfuura mamiriyoni mana vari kugara kune dzimwe nyika .
Vakawanda vevanhu ava vanorarama nekuita mabasa ose ose kuti vakwanise kuriritira mhuri dzavo nehama dzavakasiya kumusha .
VaMaphosa vanoti vakabatsirwa zvikuru kuti vasvike pavari munyika yeSweden nekuti vanhu vakawanda vemunyika umu havana rusarura rudzi uye vanotambira pfungwa dzevamwe vane mafungiro akasiyana .
VaMaphosa vanoti maonero avo ndeekuti vanhu munyika vanofanirwa kuve nemafungiro matsva mune zvematongerwo enyika kuitira kuti vatambire pfungwa dzevamwe vane mafungiro akasiyana vachiti izvi zvinobatsira kudzivirira mhirizhonga mune zvematongerwo enyika uyewo kuti nyika ibudirire .
Vanotiwo vanofunga kuti Zimbabwe inogona kugadzirisa matambudziko ayakatarisana nawo pari zvino kana vanhu vakaita muonera pamwe .
Vanoti vakazvarirwa kuBulilima kuchamhembe kwakadziva kumavirira kwenyika yeZimbabwe mumhuri ine vamwe vana vana , kusanganisira vasikana vaviri .
Vakaita zvidzidzo zveprimary nesecondary muzvikoro zviri muHarare vakazonopedzisira zvidzidzo zve """" A """" Level muguta reMasvingo .
VaMaphosa vanogara vachishanya munyika yavo yechizvarwa uye vaive munyika munguva shoma yapfuura vaine vamwe vakuru vakuru vesangano reSwedish Development Agency , SIDA , iro rinopa rubatsiro kune vanoshaya kunyanya madzimai nevana .
Pakaitika mafashamu emvura nedutumupengo remhepo kana kuti Cyclone Idai pakutanga kwegore munyika , VaMaphosa nevamwe vavanoshanda navo kuSweden vakakwanisa kuunza rubatsiro munyika .
Kunze kwekuve kanzura VaMaphosa vari mukomiti inoona nezvedzidzo uye mubato ravo reSwedish Social Democratic Party vari muchikwata chavana chipangamazano munyaya dzine chekuita nenyika dzekuchamhembe kweAfrica .
Pari zvino VaMaphosa vari kuita zvidzidzo zvepamusoro zvine chekuita nezvematongerwo enyika munyika dzemuEurope vachiti vari kuita izvi seznira yekuwedzera ruzivo rwavo rwenzvimbo .
Vanoti kana mukana ukavepo vangade chose kuwana chinzvimbo chepamusoro mune zvematongerwo enyika kusanganisira kuve nhengo yeparamende yeEuropean Union .
VaMaphosa vane mudzimai nemwana mumwe chete .
Vanorwira kodzero dzevanorarama nechirwere cheshuga vacherechedza zuva re World Diabetes Day neMugovera muZimbabwe kunyange hazvo zuva iri rakacherechedzwa pasi rose nemusi weChina .
Musangano wanga wakarongwa nesangano re Blue Circle Voices Network rakabanatana nesangano re Zimbabwe Diabetes Association .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa kusangano reZimbabwe Diabetes Association kuti tinzwe pamire sangano iri panyaya yechirwere cheshuga .
Asi imwe nhengo ye Blue Circle Voices Network mu Zimbabwe , Amai Heather Koga , vanoti musangano wafamba zvakanaka chose , uye vatora mukana uyu kucherechedza zuva reWorld Diabetes Day .
Amai Koga vanotiwo musangano wavo wapindwa nenyanzvi munyaya dzechirwere cheshuga , uye dzataura pamusoro pezvingaitwe nevanonetsekana nechirwere cheshuga ichi .
Kunyange hazvo huwandu hwevanhu vanonetsekana nechirwere cheshuga husiri kunyatsozivikanwa sezvo pachine vanhu vakawanda vane chirwere ichi asi vasingazivi kuti vanacho , Amai Koga vanoti ongororo yakamboitwa inoratidza kuti zvikamu zvinosvika gumi kubva muzana zvevanmhu vemuZimbabwe vane chirwere cheshuga .
Amai Koga vanoti zvakakosha kuti veruzhinji vaongororwe kana vaine chirwere ichi kuitira kuti vapihwe rubatsiro rwunokodzera kana vainacho .
Zimbabwe iyo yakabudirira nezuro kupinda muchikamu chechipiri chemutambo wemaoko cheNetball World Cup yakundwa nhasi neNew Zealand 79 kwa 36 .
New Zealand yakambotora mukombe weWorld Cup uyu kaviri .
Asi izvi hazvisi kumisa ruzhinji rweZimbabwe kupemberera kutamba kwechikwata chavo chinozivikanwa nekuti maGems ichi kupinda muchikamu chechipiri chine zvikwata gumi nezviviri .
Zimbabwe iri kutamba iri muGroup F nezvikwata zvinoti Australia , Northern Ireland , New Zealand , Malawi ne Barbados .
Kunyangwe Zimbabwe yakundwa , Malawi yakunda Northen Ireland 47 kwa 43 .
Rimwe gungano remakwikwi aya i Group G rine zvikwata zvinoti Jamaica , South Africa , Trinidad and Tobago , England , Uganda ne Scotland .
Zvikwata zviviri zvinenge zviri pamusoro mumagroup maviri aya ndizvo zvichaenda kumasemi finals emakwikwi aya .
Zimbabwe yakunda kaviri ikakundwawo kaviri kusvika parizvino kubva zvatanga makwikwi aya .
Asi zvichitevera kurohwa kwechikwata chenhabvu chemaWarriors kuEgypt , vanhu vakawanda munyika neavo vanga vasingazive kana kutevera mitambo yeNetball vave kuziva kuti kune chikwata chemitambo chinonzi maGems mushure mekunge chikwata ichi chaita mbiri mumakundano avo ekutanga eWorld Cup .
Vatambi vechikwata ichi vakaita saUrsula Ndlovu , Perpetua Sachikonye , Mercy Mukwadi , Joice Takaidza , Sharon Bwanali , Patricia Maoladi vaita mbiri munyika .
VaOliver Musongoro avo vanotsigira chikwata cheDynamos munhabvu vanoti vanga vachingonzwa kuti Gems , Gems vasingazive kuti chii chacho .
Muteveri wezvemitambo VaTatenda Makazhu vanoti vafadzwa zvikuru nezvakaitwa nemaGems vachiti ivo vane tarisiro yekuti vasikana ava vanouya nemukombe uyu .
Mutsigiri wechikwata ichi Muzvare Rebecca Mushunje vanoti vanga vasingatarisire kuti maGems angaiite mashiripiti akadai vachiti ikozvino vave kutotarisira zvakawanda .
Zvaitwa nemaGems izvi zvichataurwa nezvazvo kwemakore nemakore achatevera uyezve kuvatambi ava hazvikanwike muhupenyu hwavo .
Chirikunyanyofadza ndechekuti mbiri iyi yauya kubva mumaoko evanhukadzi avo vanga vachingosimudzira zita renyika mumitambo pasi rese kubvira muna 1980 .
Mugore iroro chikwata chenyika chevanhukadzi chemutambo wehockey chakatora menduru yegoridhe mumakundano eZimbabwe ekutanga emaOlympic Games ayo akaitirwa kuMoscow .
Izvi zvakateverwa nemenduru nomwe dzakatorwa nemutuhwini Kirsty Coventry kumakwikwi e2004 ne 2008 Olympic Games .
Vasikana vemutambo wenhabvu vemaMighty Warriors havana kuda kusaririra ndokubudirirawo kuenda kumaOlympic Games a 2012 , izvo zvatadzwa kuitwa nezvimwe zvikwata .
Mumwe muteveri wemutambo wenhabvu VaLawrence Hwekwete vanoti zvaitwa ikozvino nemaGems zvinoratidza husiyano hwebudiriro hurikuitika mumitambo munyika .
Muongorori wezvemitambo VaTinashe Museti vanoti vanhukadzi varikudadisa munyaya dzemitambo uye vanoti vatambi ava ngavapihwe mari .
Asi mitambo yevanhukadzi haisi kuwana rutsigiro rwakasimba zvekuti maGems akazowana rubatsirwo rwemari vachema chema uyezve vatove pedyo nekuda kusimuka kubva muZimbabwe .
Asi hurumende yakatora nguva imwecheteyo kuumba komiti yekuunganidzira mari chikwata chenyika chenhabvu chemaWarriors icho chaienda kumakundano e 2019 Africa Cup of Nations .
Zvichiburikidza zvekare nekuti maMighty Warriors akatendwa nemadhora mashanu chete apo vakadzoka kubva kuma 2012 Olympic Games , mari yaive isingakwane kuti vamwe vavo vadzokere kudzimba dzavo .
Izvakauya mushure mekunge vaimbove gurukota rezvemitambo VaMakhosini Hlongwane vavimbisa vatambi ava kuti vachatendwa zvakasimba nehurumende izvo zvisina kuzoitika .
Vakawanda vanotevera mitambo vanoti panofanira kuve neshanduko mumabatirwo arikuitwa zvikwata zvenyika zvevanhukadzi VaMuseti vachiti vatambi vemaGems vanofanira kutendwa zvakasimba .
Parizvino , hapana shoko rati rabva kuhurumende nezvaitwa nechikwata ichi kunyange hazvo kune makurukota matatu evanhukadzi akaperekedza maGems kuLiverpool .
Asi vatambi ava vangangowana kutendwa kwakasimba nekuwana mabasa kuzvikwata zvekunze kwenyika izvo zvirikumakundano aya kuraura vatambi .
Mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , vanonzi vaudza bazi rezvezviwanikwa uye bazi rezvemamiriro ekunze reEnvironmental Management Agency kuti vaone kuti kucherwa kwematombo kuDomboshava kotanga here kana kuti kwete .
Kambani yekuChina yeAihua Jianye Company iri kumirirwa muZimbabwe ne GeoGlobal Environmental Solutions ndiyo iri kufanirwa kuita mugodhi uyu .
Nyaya yekuti mugodhi wematombo utange kuchera yakonzera mutauro wakanyanya munharaunda iyi .
Vamwe vanoti vanhu vakawanda vachatamiswa misha yavo asi vanomiririra GeoGlobal Environmental Solutions , VaPercy Mudzidzwa , varamba mashoko ekuti vanhu zviuru makumi maviri vachatamiswa .
Mutevedzeri wegurukota rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko uye vari mumiriri weGoromonzi East mudare reparamende , VaEnergy Mutodi , vanoti dombo iri harifanire kuputswa sezvo rakachengetedzwa senzvimbo yekushanyira .
Sezvo tichitema tisina divi ratinorerekera , tabatawao kanzura wekwaZimbiru vari nhengo yeMDC VaTapiwa Marima varamba kuti vakapihwa mari yechiokomuhomwe .
Mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa vanosvika kuChina murwendo rwavo rwemazuva mashanu , uko vari kutarisirwawo kukwezva vemabhizimusi , pamwe nekusimbaradza hukama hwenyika mbiri idzi .
Vadzidzi vezvemitemo paGreat Zimbabwe University , kuMasvingo , vomiririra nyika mumakwikwi ekutongwa kwedzimhosva e Philip C . Jessup International Law Moot Court Competition , ari kuitwa nevadzidzi vanobva kunyika dzakasiyanasiyana muWashington D . C .

Muchikamu chedu chatinotarisa nezvehutano , nhasi tiri kutarisa nezvezuva rekuyeuchidzana pamusoro pedambudziko rinobata vana vakawanda pasi rose reAutism , takanangaga nezuva re World Autism Awareness Day , anove nhasi .
