Zimbabwe ichiri nemukana wekuwana menduru kubva kuma 2016 Olympic Games kunayngwe vakawanda vave kuti zvegore rino zvinenge zvakaona n'anga murapwa achida .
Kuchiri nevamhanyi venzendo refu Wirimai Juwao , Cuthbert Nyasango , naPartson Ndlovu avo varikupinda munzira ye 42 kilometre marathon nesvondo mangwanani .
Makundano e marathon ndiwo anovhara mabiko emaOlympic Games zvekuti vatatu ava vanofanira kushura mare kana kuti vanongobatana neavo vakadzokera kumba kare mushure mekutatarika .
Mugore ra 2012 , Juwao akapedza ari pachinhanho chechinomwe , icho chaingove zvinhanho zvina chete kubva pamenduru .
Juwao anoti akagadzirira zvakakwana asi kana pane chingangomukanganisa kunyanyopisa kwemu Rio de Janeriro .
Nyasango akapedza aripa chinhanho chechipfumbamwe kumakwikwi ekuLondon zvekuti anofanira kungowedzera mwando zvishoma pamwe vemuZimbabwe vanga farawo
Ndlovu arikukwikwidza mumaOlympic Games ake ekutanga .
Nhasi mangwanani kuBrazil ainge ari makuwerere chaiwo apo mumhanyi ane mukurumbira pasi rose Usain Bolt wekuJamaica akatora menduru yegoridhe mumakwikwi e 200 meters sezvange zvakatarisirwa .
Toenda munyaya dzenhabvu .
Vanotungamira nhabvu vayambira vachakonzera mhirizhonga mumitambo yekupera kwesvondo rino neichatevera kuti vachasungwa nekumiswa pamberi pematare edzimhosva pamwe nekukandwa kujere .
Munyori mukuru wePremier Soccer League VaKennedy Ndebele vanoti vazivisa zvikwata zvese kuti zvive nemapurisa akakwana kuitira avo vanouya kwete kuzoona nhabvu asi kuzokonzera mhirizhonga kumitambo .
Yambiro iyi yauya mushure memhirizhonga yakaitika svondo rapera pamutambo waive pakati peHighlanders neChicken Inn .
Vatsigiri veHighlanders vakakanda zvinokuvadza munhandare pamwe nekurwisana nemapurisa vachipokana nemabatirwo aiitwa pembe .
VePremier Soccer League vati vachamisa Highlanders pamberi pedare kuti vatsanangudze zvakaitika pamwe nekupihwa mutongo wavo
Vachibva munyaya dzakadai , Highlanders yacho ine mutambo wakaoma mangwana neZPC Kariba kuNyamhunga Stadium .
ZPC Kariba inotamba zvine mutsindo nezvikwata zvine mukurumbira kunyanya kana iri pamusha .
Tichitarisa matambiro ari kuita Highlanders parizvino , zvakaoma kufunga kuti Bosso inonodzoka kana nepoindi imwechete kubva kuKariba .
Chikwata chiri kutungamira makundano aya cheFC Platinum chiri kufamba nzendo pfupi apo chirikuenda kuGibbo Stadium kunotamba neTriangle .
Mazuva ano , Kugona Kunenge Kudada irikuwanza mangange zvekuti vakaita izvi Caps United ikakunda Bulawayo City kuBabourfields Stadium zvinhu pamusoro zvinosanduka .
Asi Muteveri weFC Platinum vaTerence Kuhuni vanoti havasi kutya Triangle sezvo vakatokunda kare vachiti ivo varikuda mukombe uyo wavatsvedza kwemakore maviri apfuura .
Mutsigiri weMakepekepe VaMisheck Chisaga vayambira chikwata chavo kuti chisadherere Bulawayo City sezvo kusisina zvikwata zvidiki munhabvu mazuva ano .
Mumusha weDynamos hamuna mufaro mushure mekunge chikwata ichi chakaita mangange acho echishanu mumitambo mitanhatu .
Murairidzi wechikwata ichi Lloyd Mutasa akaedza kusandura vatambi akambomisa Steven Alimenda , Roderick Mutuma , Charles Muroyiwa , na Denver Mukmba asi zvikakona .
Asi varikuona chikwata ichi chichitamba vakaita samuzvare Judith Nyatsanza vanoti chikwata chavo chingadai chiri kukunda asi havana vanwisi nezvibodzwa .
Dynamos yatarisana nemumwe mutambo wakaoma apo iri kusangana neHarare City iyo inorairidzwa naMoses Chunga uyo akamborairidza nekutambira Dembare .

Bato rinopikisa reMDC inotungamirirwa naVaNelson Chamisa rinoti musangano wakarongwa nemutungamiri webato VaChamisa wekuti vataure kumhuri yeZimbabwe weHope of the Nation Address , wave kuzoitirwa kumuzinda webato iri weMorgan Tsvangirai House neChitatu .
Musangano uyu wakambenge wanzi uchaitirwa muAfrica Unity Square muHarare asi mapurisa anonzi akaurambidza kuti uenderere mberi panzvimbo iyi achinzi akati aityira kuti veruzhinji vanogona kuzotora mukana iwoyo kuratidzira nekukonzera mhirizhonga sezvo vanhu vasina kugadzikana munyika .
Mutauriri wemutungamiri weMDC , Doctor Nkululeko Sibanda , vanoti vakaedza kuudza mapurisa kuti vachange vaine vanyarikani vanosanganisira vamiriri vemizinda yenyika dzekunze pamwe nevemabhizimusi , nekudaro hapana mhirizhonga inozoitika , asi mapurisa akaisa zvimiti munzeve .
Doctor Sibanda vanoti havana kushamiswa nemhinduro yemapurisa iyi sezvo agara ari kurambidza bato reMDC kuita misangano yaro nyika yose .
Panyaya yekuti mapurisa haasi kuwirirana nenzvimbo yavari kuda kuitira musangano wavo , Doctor Sibanda vanoti harisi basa remapurisa rekuvatsvagira kwekuitira misangano yavo sezvo vari bato riri pamutemo muZimbabwe .
Mutauriri wemapurisa , Assistant Commissioner Paul Nyathi , varamba kuti mapurisa akarambidza VaChamisa kuita musangano wavo , asi kuti mapurisa haana kuwirirana nepfungwa yekuti musangano uyu uitirwe muAfrica Unity Square .
Assistant Commissioner Nyathi vanoti mutemo mutsva weMaintenance of Peace and Order Act , MOPA , unopa masimba kumukuru wemapurisa mudunhu rinenge richida kuitirwa musangano kuti aone kana zvakakodzera kuti mudunhu rake muitirwe musangano uyu pasina mhirizhonga .
Vanoti nekuda kweizvozvo , mukuru wemapurisa muguta reHarare akaona zvakakodzera kuti musangano uyu usaitirwa muAfrica Unity Square .
Apo pasi rose riri kucherechedza mazuva gumi nematanhatu ekuremekedzwa kwekodzero dzemadzimai nevanasikana , vaimbi vechidzimai vashanu vachange vachiimba pamutambo unozivikanwa nerekuti Pangu Pangu ku German Society muHarare neChipiri manheru .
Mumwe weavo vakaronga mutambo uyu , Muzvare Rudo Chigudu , vanoti zvakakosha kuti madzimai awane nguva yekupemberera hudzimai hwavo zvisineyi nekuti vanoita mabasa api .
Vaimbi vachange vachiridza vanosanganisira Selmor Mtukudzi , Tariro Negitare , Cindy Munyavi , Kessia Magosha , na Rumbi Wengoma .

Vachitaura kuvanhu ava mutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa vati zvirango zvakafanana negomarara riri kudya hupfumi hwenyika .
VaMnangagwa vati zvirango izvi zviri kunze kwemutemo uye zvinofanira kubviswa nechimbi chimbi vachitiwo sehurumende vari kuvandudza zvinhu zvakawanda zvinosanganisira nyaya dzehupfumi , zvematongerwo enyika pamwe nekuti munyika mugare muine runyararo uye kodzero dzevanhu dzichichengetedzwa .
Vati vari kufara kuti zvirango zvavanoti vakatemerwa neEU zvatanga kubviswa kuburikidza nenhaurirano dzavari kuita .

Sezvo Dyanoms yakakundwa , iri kuendawo kubhanga ichinyemwerera sezvo iri kuwana zviuru makumi mashanu zvemadhora , ukuwo Triangle ichiwana zviuru makumi masere zvemadhora .

kuti TIP Report , musi wa 25 Chikumi .
Vachitaura pakuparurwa kwegwaro iri , gurukota rezvekudyidzana nedzimwe nyika , VaMike Pompeo , vakati kumbunyikidzwa kwevanhu vachiendeswa kune dzimwe nyika , kunosanganisira kuitiswa mabasa epabonde pamwe nekushanda mamwe mabasa munhu achimanikidzwa , uye izvi zviri kuramba zvichiitika pasi rose .
"""" Pane zvanhu vanodarika mamiriyoni makumi maviri nemashanu vari kumanikidzwa kuita mabasa avasingade uye kuitiswa mabasa epabonde pasi rose .
Kudzikisira hunhu hwevanhu zvakadaro hazvitambirwe , tose takasikwa tiri mufananidzo yaMwari .
Mabasa akadai ndeehutsinye . """"
Gore rapera , mutungamiri weAmerica , VaDonald Trump , vakamisa rumwe rubatsiro kudzihurumende gumi neshanu idzo dziri mugwaro re 2019 Tip Report .
Muna Ndira gore rino , VaTrump vakati America yakanga yadira mari inoita mazana mashanu emamiriyoni emadhora mukurwisa kumanikidzwa kwevanhu kuita mabasa epabonde pamwe nemamwe mabasa avanenge vasingadi kuita .
VaPompeo vakataura pamusoro pemabasa akaitwa neAmerica mukurwisa maitiro akaipa aya sezviri mugwaro re 2020 TIP Report .
"""" Nyika makumi maviri nembiri dzakasimudzirwa gore rino , gumi nenhatu dziri nyika dzemu Sub - Saharan Africa . """"
Gwaro reTIP Report rinoburitswawo pachena nyika dzinotsigira kumbunyikidzwa kwevanhu vachinoitiswa mabasa avasingadi idzo dziri pachinhambo yechitatu .
Nyika idzi dzinosanganisira China , uko bato re Chinese Communist Party pamwe nemakambani ehurumende izvo zvinomanikidza zvizvarwa zvenyika iyi kushanda munzvimbo dzakashata muhurongwa hwenyika iyi hweBelt and Road , uko verudzi vechi Uighurs nemamwe marudzi madiki echiMuslim vari kumanikidzwa kuita mabasa avasingadi kuita muXinjiang nedzimwe nzvimbo .
Mu Cuba , hupfumi hwehurumende yaVaCastro hunobva muhurongwa hwezvehutano .
Pane vanhu vekuCuba vanodarika zviuru makumi mashanu vanoshanda munyaya dzehutano munyika makumi matanhatu pasi rose .
Madhokotera mazhinji ekuCuba ari munyika idzi anoti ari kumanikidzwa kushanda muhurongwa uhu .
Nyika dzakawanda dzinotambira madhokotera aya kuti ashande munyika idzi , kunyange hazvo zviri pachena kuti vashandi vezvehutano ava vanenge vamanikidzwa kunoshanda kunyika idzi , vachibatirwa magwaro avo ekufambisa , kusajekeswa kwezvibvumirano zvavo zvekushanda kunze kwenyika , uye kubhadharwa kwehurumende yeCuba nenyika idzi
, madhokotera aya asingabhadharwe .
"""" Tinotora zvakadzama nyaya dzekumbunyikidzwa kwevanhu nedzihurumende dzavo , """" vakadaro VaPompeo .
"""" Ibasa redzihurumende kuchengetedza kodzero dzezvizvarwa zvenyika , kwete kumbunyikidza kodzero idzi .
America haife yakabatana nenyika dzinomanikidza zvizvarwa zvadzo kuita zvisingadiwe nezvizvarwa izvi . """"
Mumiriri weAmerica muZimbabwe , Ambassador Harry Thomas Junior , vashanyira dunhu reTsholotsho vachiona zvirongwa zviri kutsigirwa nehurumende yavo munzvimbo iyi .
Vachitaura kuvatori venhau mushure mekushanyira zvimwe zvirongwa zviri kutsigirwa nesangano reUSAID kuNkunzi kuTsholotsho , Ambassador Thomas vati vanofara kuti nyika yavo ndiyo inopa rubatsiro rwakakura kuZimbabwe kudarika dzimwe nyika dzose pasi rose .
Vati izvi zvinoratidza kuzvipira kwakaita vanhu vemuAmerica mukubatsira vanhu vemuZimbabwe vakati muzinda wavo unoshuvirawo kuti kudyidzana pakati peAmerica neZimbabwe mune zvemabhizimisi nezvekutengeserana kukure .
Vachipindura mubvunzo wekuti sei muzinda wavo wakabvuma kupa magwaro ekufambisa kuvanhu vakawanda vakaperekedza mutungamiri wenyika , VaRobert Mugabe , kumusangano weUnited Nations General Assembly kuNew York , VaThomas vati pasi pemiteno yekudyidzana pakati penyika , havakwanise kupindira panyaya dzehuwandu hwevanhu vanenge vanzi nehurumende vari kuenda kumusangano
wakadaro .
Ambassador Thomas , avo vange vachiperekedzwa nevamwe vakuru vakuru vesangano reUSAID pamwe nereCreating New Frontiers in Agriculture , vashanyira chirongwa chekupa chikafu kumadzimai akazvitakura pamwe nevana vari pakati pemwedzi mitanhatu nemakore maviri paNkunzi Clinic kuTsholotsho .
Vashanyirawo madzimai pamwe nevarume vari kuita chirongwa cheThuthukani Village Savings and Lending Group chekuchengeta nekukweretesana mari pamwe nekudzidza nekuchengeta zvipfuyo uye chimwe chekudzidzisa zvehutsanana pasi pezvikwata zvinonzi Community Health Clubs
Zvirongwa izvi zviri kuitwa pasi pechirongwa chinoziikanwa kunzi Amalima chinotsigirwa neUSAID neCreating New Frontiers in Agriculture .
Muzvare Ntombiyenhle Ncube , avo vane mwana ane gore nemwedzi mina , ndemumwe wemadzimai vane mwana ari muchirongwa chekupiwa chikafu , uye vaipiwavo chikafu pavaive vane pamuviri .
Vati chirongwa ichi chakakosha zvikuru nekuti chinobatsira kuti vanamai pamwe nevana vave nehutano hwakanaka .
Mukuru wezvehutano nekudya kwakanaka musangano reAmalima , Amai Pamela Ncube , vati zvirongwa zvavo zvinokurudzirawo vagari kuti vachengetedze hutano nekuita zvinhu zvakasiyana siyana kusanganisira kuvaka zvimbuzi pamisha yavo .
Chirongwa cheAmalima chiri kuitwa kuTsholotsho , muMatabeleland North pamwe nekuBulilima , Gwanda neMangwe kuMatabeleland South uye chinotarisirwa kupedzwa gore rinouya .
Murairidzi wechikwata cheCaps United Darlington Dodo anoti havasati vatora mukombe we Castle Lager Premier Soccer League kusvikira vaisa maoko avo ese maviri pamukombe wacho vachiusimudza .

Izvi zvauya mushure mekunge Makepekepe yarova Hwange 3 - 1 muNational Sports Stadium nemusi weSvondo ndokuramba yakatungamira gungano rePremier Soccer League ichiteverwa neFC Platinum iyo yakarovawo Yadah 3 - 1 neMugovera .
Dodo ari kufara nekurova kwavakaita Hwange achiti chikwata chake chiri munzira inofadza achiwedzerawo kuti vatambi vake var ikuziva chinangwa chavo chemwaka uno .

Asi murairidzi weHwange Nation Dube haasi kufara nemabatirwo akaitwa pembe pamutambo wavo neCaps United .

Sangano revarairidzi reProgressive Teachers' Union of Zimbabwe , PTUZ , rinoti riri kunyunyuta zvikuru nekwarinoti kusarongeka kwechirongwa chehurumende chekuunganidza ruzivo pamusoro pevashandi vayo kana kuti biometric exercise , icho chiri kuitwa senzira yekuburitsa nayo pachena vanhu vangadai vari kutambira mari asi vasiri vashandi vehurumende , kana kuti ghost workers .
Mutungamiri wePTUZ , Doctor Takavafira Zhou , vanoti varairidzi vakawanda vakaedza kunonyoresa pasi pechirongwa ichi asi vari kusangana nezvimhingamipinyi zvakasiyanasiyana zviri kuvatadzisa kuti vange vachipa zvese zviri kudiwa nehurumende pamusoro pavo .
Doctor Zhou vanoti dambudziko guru riri kusangana nenhengo dzavo , nderekuti vanoenda kumahofisi kwacho vosvikoudzwa kuti hapana zvimwe zvinodiwa kuti vabatsirwe .
Vanoti chimwe chiri kunyanyovanetsa ndechekuti chirongwa ichi chiri kuita kusarudza varairidzi , zvikuru vaya vanenge vaine zvitupa zvesimbi vasina zvitsva zvemazuvano .
Vanotiwo vakanyorera hurumende tsamba semasangano evashandi vachida kuti vaite musangano wekutsanangurirwa pamusoro pemafambisirwo ari kuitwa chirongwa ichi , asi vanoti kusvika nanhasi havasati vapindurwa .
Chirongwa ichi chinonzi chiri kutarisirwa kupera neMuvhuro 30 Gunyana , hurumende ichiti mushandi anenge asina kunyoresa patsva zita rake haaizokwanisa kuwana muhoro wake wemwedzi waGumiguru .
Studio 7 yakundikana kunzwa divi rehurumende panyaya iyi .
Asi Doctor Zhou vanoti kusarongeka kwazvo kwave kukanganisa mashandiro evarairidzi uyewo kuvatorera twumari twushoma twavanenge vatambira , zvinozovasiya vasina mari yekutenga zvekudya zvinovakwanira .
Chikwata cheFC Platinum chatarisana nekuwedzera hutungamiri hwacho chiri pamusoro pegungano reCastle Lager Premier Soccer League panguva iyo murairidzi mutsva weDynamos Tonderai Ndiraya ari kuyedza kubvisa chikwata chake mumadhaka machiri .
Murairidzi weDynamos Tonderai Ndiraya ari kuedzwa masimba zvakasimba apo chikwata chake chiri muRufaro Stadium nesvondo kusangana neZPC Kariba iyo irikubvira moto unotyisa kubvira makundamo enhabvu emwaka uno atanga .
Ndiraya akatambidzwa basa iri svondo rapera kwadzingwa basa Lloyd Chigove ndokunoita mangange 1 - 1 neTelOne asi vanoongorora mutambo wenhabvu vanoti iri raive raki reachangotanga basa zvekuti mutambo neZPC Kariba ndiwo chaiwo ucharatidza kuti Ndiraya achagara pabasa kwenguva refu here .
Aka kave kechipiri Ndiraya achirairidza Dembare sezvo akambova nebasa iri muna 2015 ndokudzingwa zvakashamisa veruzhinji mushure mekunge chikwata chake chapedza chiri pachinzvimbo chechipiri , pasi peChicken Inn .
Asi muongorori wemutambo wenhabvu VaEmmanuel Matshinya vanoti Ndiraya ari panguva yakaoma sezvo vatsigiri veDembare vachida kukunda mumitambo yese inotamba chikwata chavo .
Ndiraya pachake anoti acharamba achishanda nesimba kusimudzira Dembare kubva pairi parizvino apo pasingafadze .
Sachigaro weDynamos Supporters Club yemuHarare VaBenjamin Muzira vanoti Ndiraya atanga zvakanaka nekutora poindi kunze kwemusha kuTelOne vachiti ivo vave kutarisira zvekusimudza mukombe .
Asi chikwata chiri kutungamira makwikwi aya cheFC Platinum hachisi kunyanyoremerwa apo chiri pamusha muMandava Stadium mangwana neHerentals iyo iri kutatarika .
Parizvino , FC Platinum iri pamusoro nemapoinzi matatu zvekuti mumwe mutsigiri wavo VaTatenda Makazhu vari kuona vachiwedzera hutungamiri hwavo vari pamusoro pePSL .
Asi zvikwata zvinoteverwa nechaunga Caps United neHighlanders hazvina mitambo iri nyore seFC Platinum sezvo Highlanders iine Chipangano cheHwange muBarboufields Stadium , Caps United ichidzoka kumusha muNational Sports Stadium kusangana neHarare City .

Va Zvemhare , avo vanonyanyozivikanwa nezita remadunhururirwa rekuti Baba vaTennsen kuburikidza nenyambo dzavanoita , vakanowana basa rekushanda sagadheni bhoyi pane mumwe muchena pavakabatwa zvakanaka chose
Kubuda kwevamwe vakawanda munyika vachinotsvaga mafuro manyoro kunze kuri kuvavhurira mikana yakasiyanasiyana , mimwe yakanaka mimwe inochemedza .
Asi kuna VaPepukai Zvemhare , avo vakaberekerwa kuChibi , Maringire , mudunhu reMidlands , makore makumi matatu nemasere apfuura , kubuda kwavo munyika vachienda kuSouth Africa kwakavavhurira mukana mukuru kwazvo , wekuripwa kugara .
VaZvemhare , avo vanonyanyozivikanwa nezita remadunhururirwa rekuti Baba vaTennsen kuburikidza nenyambo dzavanoita , vakanowana basa rekushanda sagadheni bhoyi pane mumwe muchena pavakabatwa zvakanaka chose .
"""" Ndakanga ndiine zvose , mvura inodziya , cheya inotenderera , imba ine mhepo inodziya kana kutonhorera , chikafu ndichipiwa mahara , apa ndichiripwa ndakagara zvangu , """" Va Zvemhare vanodaro .
Vanoti izvi zvakaita kuti vatore kavhidhiyo kadukuku vachiudza hama dzavo kusha nekugarika kwavakanga vaita pabasa ravo rekutanga muhupenyu hwavo , semunhu akanga asati amboshanda kunyange hazvo vaive vaine magwaro edzidzo ye Form 4 .
Va Zvemhare , avo vane vana vaviri , Tennsen , ane makore gumi nemana , naTensley ane makore gumi ekuberekwa , vanoti kunyange hazvo pari zvino vasati vave kukwanisa kuita zvavanoshuvira kuita kumusha kwavo nekuda kwekushaiwa mari , vane hurongwa hwekuti remangwana vashande nezvikoro .
Asi pari zvino vanoti mavhidhiyo avari kuita ari kuita kuti vakwanise kuriritira mhuri yavo , zvekuti vakatosiya basa ravaiita vachingorarama nekuita nyambo dzavo kumichato nekumabhavhadhe kwavanokokiwa .
Gurukota rezvemari Muzvinafundo Mthuli Ncube vakazivisa nezuro kuti mutengo wehupfu hwave kuwedzerwa zvekare kubva pamadhora makumi mashanu kusvika pamadhora makumi manomwe pamakirogiramu gumi .
Mutsamba kuvatori venhau , bazi rezvemari rakazivisa kuti hupfu hunofanira kunge huchitengeswa hwakaderera mutengo sezvo hurumende iri kubatsira hwave kutengeswa pamukoto zvopa kuti vade kuona kuti vagadzirise dambudziko iri sei .
Asi dzimwe nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfumi dzinoti hurumende haina mari yekuramba ichipa vanogaya hupfumi ava kuti vatengese nemutegno wakaderera .
Mutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa vainge vatiwo hupfu hausi kuzokwidzwa asi aya anenge aiva manyautsa mukanwa chembere kurota ichiyamwa .
Zimbabwe yakatarisana nenzara inotyisa gore rino sezvo vanhu vanosvika mamiriyoni masere vachida rubatsiro rwechikafu .
United Nations inoti izvi zvakonzerwa nekusanaya zvakanaka kwemvura uye kutadza kutungamirwa kwenyika .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfumi Muzvinafundo Gift Mugano vanodzidzisa paNelson Mandela Metropolitan University vanoti mitemo yehurumende ndiyo iri kupa kuti zvinhu zvinyanyoite mhidigari .
Vati hurumende haifanire kutara mutengo wechibage sezvo zvichipa kuti vanhu vashoma vade kuchirima .
Hurumende inoti yabhadhara chikwereti chayo chemagetsi kumbani yemagetsi yeZESA uyewo yabhadharwa chikwereti cheZESA kukambani yemagetsi yeESKOM yekuSouth Africa .
Vachitaura mushure memusangano wedare remakurukota , gurukota rinoona nezvemamhando dzemoto , VaFortune Chasi , vati hurumende yabhadhara chikwereti chayo chemamiriyoni makumi maviri emadhora kuZESA uyewo yapa kambani iyi mamwe mamiriyoni makuma maviri emadhora ekuti kambani iyi ivandudze basa rekugaya magetsi .
Vatiwo vabhadhara chikwereti cheZESA kuESKOM chemamiriyoni gumi emadhora ekuAmerica .
Vati izvi zvichabatsira kuti nyika ideredze dambudziko rekushomeka kwemagetsi munyika iro raita kuti nyika igove magetsi kana kuti loadshedding .
VaChasi vatiwo veruzhinji , makambani nemakanzuru vanofanira kubhadhara magetsi .
Vatiwo nyaya yemagetsi inofanira kubatanidza vanhu munyika kuona kuti vogadzirisa sei dambudziko rekushomeka kwemagetsi .
Vachitaurawo mushure medare remakurukota , gurukota rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , Amai Monica Mutsvangwa , vati dare remakurukota ratambira danho rakatorwa nebazi rezvemari svondo rino rekudzora dhora remuno rikati danho iri richaunza kugadzikana munyika munyaya dzehupfumi .
Pavabvunzwa nezvekuti vanhu vane maNostro Foreign Currency Account nevaya vanotumirwa mari nemakambani akaita Western Union nemamwe , vachawana mari yavo here kana kuti vachamanikidzwa kuitengesa kumabhanga , Amai Mutsvangwa vati vanhu ava vacharamba vachiwana mari dzavo ari madhora ekuAmerica , mapaunzi nedzimwe mari dzekunze .
Asi kunyange hazvo Amai Mutsvangwa vati dare remakurukota ratambira gwaro reStatutory Instrument 142 , masangano evashandi pamwe nevemabhizimisi audza hurumende kuti mutemo uyu unofanira kubviswa sezvo wakaitwa pasina kuwirirana sezvinodiwa pasi pemutemo weTNF .
Masangano aya atuma gurukota rezvevashandi , Doctor Sekai Nzenza , kuti vaendese nyaya iyi kudare remakurukota svondo rinouya kuti mutemo uyu ubviswe .
Zimbabwe Congress of Trade Unions inoti vashandi vacharamwa mabasa kana izvi zvikasaitika .
Mutemo uyu , uyo wakaburitswa nemusi weMuvhuro wave pamberi pekomiti yeparamende yeParliamentary Legal Committee iyo inoongorora kuti mitemo haipikisane nebumbiro remutemo here kana kuti kwete .
Rimwe gweta risina kuda kudomwa nezita raudza Studio7 kuti rinoona nesekuti mutemo uyo hauna kunyorwa zvakajeka uye zviri pachena kuti hurumende ine vanhu kana makambani ainoda kubata pachishandiswa mutemo uyu .
Zvichakadai nhengo dzeparamende nhasi dzati nyaya yekuzvidza paramende kuri kuitwa nemakurukota ehurumende iri kuenderera mberi yave kunganganisa mashandiro eparamende .
Sachigaro wekomiti yeparamende inoona nezvedzidzo , Amai Priscillar Misihairambwi Mushonga , vaudza mutauriri weNational Assembly , Advocate VaJacob Mudenda , kuti makomiti ave kutadza kuita basa rawo nekuti makurukota ehurumende pamwe nevanyori vemapazi ehurumende havawanike , sezvo vanenge vasipo nguva dzese .
Amai Mushonga vati zviri pachena kuti zvose zvinotaurwa nemutungamiriri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , hazvisi kuitwa nekuti makurukota avo nevanyori vawo havana basa ravari kuita .
Vati nekuda kwazvovo vave kuda kuita musangano wemasachigaro emakomiti eparamende nemutungamiriri wenyika .
Advocate Mudenda vatambira chikumbiro chaAmai Mushonga uye vaudza mukuru webasa rehurumende muparamende zvakare vari gurukota rezvemitemo neparamende , VaZiyambi Ziyambi , kuti varonge musangano nemutungamiri wenyika .
Chitatu chega chega vatevedzeri vemutungamiriri wenyika , makurukota ehurumende nevatevedzeri vavo vanosungirwa kuenda kuparamende kunopindura mibvunzo kubva kunhengo dzeparamende asi vazhinji vavo havaendi .
Bazi rezvehutano rinoti huwandu hwevanhu vabatwa nechirwere checoronavirus munyika hwakakwirazve zvakanyanya kusvika pachiuru chimwe chete nemazana matanhatu ane gumi nemumwe chete kana kuti 1 , 611 mushure mekunge vamwe vanhu zana nemakumi matatu nevatatu kana kuti 133 vabatwa nechirwere ichi nezuro .
Pavanhu ava zana negumi nevanhatu kana kuti 116 vakatapurirwa chirwere ichi munyika vamwe gumi nevanomwe vakabva kuSouth Africa .
Vanhu vapora kubva kuchirwere ichi vakawedzera nemakumi matatu kusvika pamazana manomwe nemakumi manomwe nevaviri kana kuti 472 .
Vafa vachiri makumi maviri nevashanu .
Vanhu vavhenekwa chirwere ichi vanodarika zviuru zana kana kuti 100 000 .
Nyaya yedkuwedzera kwehuwandu hwevanhu vari kubatwa nechirwere ichi yave kupa kuti dzidzo munyika idzokerewo kumashure .
Nekukwira kuri kuita vanhu vabatwa nechirwere ichi , sachigaro weZIMSEC Muzvinafundo Eddie Mwenje vakazivisa bepanhau reSunday Mail kuti bvunzo idzi dzinogona kunyorwa gore rinouya vana vanyatsopedza zvidzidzo zvavo .
Mutungamiri wesangano revarairidzi reZIMTA VaRichard Gundani vanoti sangano ravo rinotambira hurongwa hwekuti bvunzo dzeO Level ne A Level dzirege kunyorwa gore rino nekuda kwechirwere checoronavirus .
Zvichakadaro , mashoko atumirwa studio 7 neAfrican Union achibva kuAfrica Centers for Disease Control and Prevention anoratidza kuti vanhu vanodarika zviuru mazana manomwe nemaviri kana kuti 702 , 000 vabatwa nechirwere checoronavirus muAfrica .
Vanhu vafa vanosvika zviuru gumi nezvina zvine mazana mapfumbamwe ane makumi mashanu nematanhatu kana kuti 14 , 956 .
Vapora vadarika zviuru mazana matatu zvine makumi matanhatu nemanomwe kana kuti 367 , 000 .
South Africa ine vanhu vanodarika zviuru mazana matatu zvine makumi mashanu kana kuti 350 , 000 ndiyo ine vanhu vakawandisa vabatwa nechirwere ichi muafrica .
Huwandu hwevanhu vabatwa nechirwere checoronavirus pasi rose hwadarika mamiriyoni gumi nezvina ane zviuru mazana matatu kana kuti 14 , 3 million .
Johns Hopkins University yemuAmerica iyo iri kuongorora kupararira kwechirwere ichi pasi rose inoti muamerica ndimo mune vanhu vakawandisa vabatwa nekufa nechirwere ichi ichiteverwa neBrazil .
Vanhu vafa muamerica vadarika zviuru zana zvine makumi mana kana kuti 140 , 000 .
Pasi rose vanhu vafa nechirwere ichi vadarika zviuru mazana matanhatu nematatu kana kuti 603 , 000 .
Vapora vachidarika mamiriyoni masere kana kuti 8 million .

Vepakati : Marlon Mushonga , Moses Muchenje , Devon Chafa , Trevor Mavhunga , Kelvin Madzongwe , Phineas Bamusi , Juan Mutudza , King Nadolo , Wellington Taderera , Ishmael Wadi , Valentine Kadonzvo , William Manondo , Kelvin Chibunyu na Stanley Ngala .
Mumwe mugari wemuBulawayo , VaEmmerson Madzana , vanoti sevamwe vatungamiri vose vane nhoroondo yekutonga nedemo , hazvivashamise kuti VaMugabe vakaratidza kuti vanoda kuramba vari pachigaro .
Asi vanoti vanoona VaMugabe vachisiya chigaro chavo munguva pfupi iri kutevera .
Izvi zvatsinhirwawo naVaElliot Sithole avo vati vanhu havafanirwe kuwora moyo vachienzanisa nhoroondo yenyika nenhoroondo yekufamba kwevana veIziraeri vachibva muhunhapwa kuenda munyika yehuchi nemukaka yeCanaan yavaive vavimbiswa naMwari .
Mukuru wesangano re # This Constitution , Our Constitution , Muzvare Abigale Mupambi , vati kunyange zvikadii vanoona hutongi hwaVaMugabe huchipera nekukasika .
Vatiwo masangano anoshanda akazvimirira pamwe nemapato anopikisa vanofanirwa kungwarira kuti vasakoshiwa kuti hondo yekugadzirisa bumbiro remitemo yenyika haina kupera .
Mutauriri webato reZapu , VaIphithule Maphosa , vatsinhirawo izvi vachiti nekuda kwekuti zviri kuitika pari zvino zvinhu zvakakosha zvikuru munhoroondo yenyika , vanhu vanogona kufarisa zvekuzopererwa nemazano ekutii voenda sei mberi .
Pari zvino veruzhinji vari kukwenya mhino dzavo nekasiyanwa vakamirira kunzwa kuti VaMugabe vasiya basa uye kuti chii chichatevera mumashure .
Sangano rinomiririra vanhukadzi nekurwira kodzero dzavo , re Women's Academy for Leadership and Political Excellence ( WALPE ) rinoti raendesa zvichemo zvaro kunhengo dzeparamende richiti rinoda kuona bumbiro remutemo richishandiswa zvakanaka uye zvesarudzo zvichipindudzwa nenzira inoita kuti vechidzimai vapiwe mukana wekukwanisavo kuti vaite zvematongerwo enyika pasina rusarura
.
Mukuru wesangano iri , Muzvare Sitabile Dewa , vaudza Studio 7 kuti zvimwe zvavanoda zviri mugwaro ravasvitsa kuparamende zvinosanganisa kugadziriswa nekukurumidza kwebumbiro remutemo kuti rishande pamwe chete nemitemo yemunyika , zvikuru sei munyaya dzesarudzo , vachiti sangano ravo rinoda kuti paramende idzike mutemo wekuti vanhukadzi
vapiwe zvigaro zvakaenzana nezvevanhurume , kuita 50 / 50 , kwete zve'proportional representation' zviri kushandiswa ikozvino .
Mushure mekunetsana kwemakore akawanda uye kukandirana makobvu nematate pakati pehurumende nebazi rezvevashandi reZimbabwe Congress of Trade Unions , ZCTU , nezvekuti sangano revashandi rive nemumiriri mubhodhi reNational Social Security Authority kana kuti NSSA , nyaya iyi yazogadziriswa .
Mutevedzeri wemunyori mukuru weZCTU , VaThomas Masvinge , ndivo vakasarudzwa kupinda mubhodhi iri .
Gurukota rezvevashandi , Doctor Sekai Nzenza , vanoti vave kushanda zvakanaka nevashandi .
Vaimiririra ZCTU mubhodhi reNSSA vari mutungamiri wesangano iri , VaPeter Mutasa , vakadzingwa mubhodhi reNSSA muna 2017 vachipomerwa mhosva yekusvibisa zita rekambani iyi .
ZCTU yakaedza kuti vadzokere zvekare asi hurumende yakatsika madziro .
Asi VaMutasa vanoti havasi havo kufara nematanho avanofanira kutora kana vachisarudza mumiriri wavo .
VaMutasa vanotiwo mamwe makurukota ehurumende ange achitora mukana wekushaikwa kwenhengo yavo mubhodhi kuita zvehuori zvakaona vaimbova gurukota rezvekushanyirwa kwenyika , Amai Prisca Mupfumira , vachisungwa vachipomerwa mhosva yekuita zvehuori .
Mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , vari kuNamibia uko vari kushanya kwemazuva matatu .
VaMnangagwa , avo vari kuperekedzwa negurukota rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , Amai Monica Mutsvangwa , vari kutarisirwa kuvhura zviri pamutemo chiteshe cheZimbabwe chiri kuWalvis Bay , icho chichashandiswa mukupinda kana kubuda kwezvinhu zvinenge zvauya nengarava .
Rwendo rwaVaMnangagwa urwu rwakananganawo nemusangano wechipfumbamwe wekudyidzana kwenyika mbiri idzi mune zveupfumi , we Zimbabwe - Namibia Joint Permanent Commission .
Nyika mbiri idzi dzanyorerawo zvibvumirano zvakasiyanasiyana zvakanangana nekudyidzana mune mapoka akasiyanasiyana , anosanganisira kufambiswa kwemashoko , zvehumhizha , zvemabhizimusi maduku , pamwe nezvekutengeserana .
Chimwe chibvumirano chanyoreranwa chinosanganisirawo chekudyidzana kwematunhu anoti reOkavango East rekuNamibia nereMashonaland West remuZimbabwe .
Urwu rwendo rwemutungamiri wenyika rwepiri kubva pavakatora chigaro muna 2017 .
Vanoongorora zvematongerwo enyika , vari mudzidzisa mukuru paTswane University of Technology iri muPretoria , muSouth Africa , Doctor Ricky Munyaradzi Mukonza , vanoti rwendo rwaVaMnangagwa rwakanaka chose sezvo rwuchisimbisa hukama gwara huripo pakati penyika mbiri idzi .
Asi VaMukonza vanoti pazvibvumirano zvanyorerana pasi , havaone havaone zvose zvichibereka michero , sezvimwe zvakawanda zvakanyoreranwa pasi nenyika dzakasiyanasiyana kubva pakapinda VaMnangagwa pachigaro .
Mutungamiri wenyika , VaRobert Mugabe , vasvitsa makore makumi mapfumbamwe nematatu .
VaMugabe vakaberekwa musi 21 Kukadzi mugore ra 1924 .
Bhavhudhe raVaMugabe rinosvika panguva iyo zvinhu zvisina kumira zvakanaka munyika , uye vanhu vakawanda vasina mabasa .
Vachitaura neZBC pamberi pezuva rekuzvarwa kwavo , VaMugabe vakataura pamusoro pezviri kuitika mubato ravo , umo mune kurwisana pamusoro pekuti ndiyani achavatsviva kana vabva pachigaro .
VaMugabe vakataurawo pamusoro pevanhu vari kuti vakwekugura , nokudaro vanofanirwa kusiya basa .
Asi VaMugabe vanoti vachiri njanji chaiyo pakusimba .
VaMugabe vakatorawo mukana uyu kutaura pamusoro pezvirango zvakatemerwa nyika ne America , vakati vanovimba kuti mutungamiri mutsva we America , Va Donald Trump , vachabvisa zvirango izvi nekupindana kwenguva .
Gurukota rinoona nezvehumhizha mukufambiswa kwemashoko , VaSupa Mandiwanzira , vanoti VaMugabe vanofanira kukorokotedzwa nekutungamira zvine hungwaru pazuva ravo rebhavhudhe ravo .
Asi vanopikisa munyika vari kuti VaMugabe vave kuchifanira kuenda pamudyandigere .
Mabiko ebhavhudhe raVaMugabe achaitwa paRhodes Estate Preparatory School kuMatopos , mudunhu reMatabeleland .
Nzvimbo iyi iri chinhanho makumi maviri emakiromita kumadokero kwakadziva kuchemhembe kweguta reBulawayo .
Mambo Seke , VaStanley Chimanikire , vanoti Zimbabwe haisisina tsika nehunhu zvinotarisirwa kunyika yakaita seZimbabwe .
Vachitaura vari pamuzinda wavo kwaSeke mazuva mashoma mitambo yemazuva maviri yeKumusha Fringe Festival isati yatanga kuDema Growth Point , Mambo Seke vati vanhu havachaziva tsika dzavo , izvo zvakapa hurumende kuti ipe madzishe basa rekudzidzisa veruzhinji pamusoro petsika dzavo .
Mambo Seke , avo vane nzvimbo iri kuitirwa Kumusha Fringe Festival , vakurudzirawo vanoita mitambo yechinyakare yakaita seJerusarema , kuti vazive zvinoreva mitambo iyi sezvo mimwe yacho iri mitambo inofanirwa kuonekwa nevanhu vakuru chete , kwete zviri kuitwa mazuva ano zvokuti vana vadiki vari kusiyiwa vachiona mitambo yakadai .
Vatiwo veruzhinji muZimbabwe havacharemekedzi mabasa emadzimambo , izvo vati zvinovaodza moyo zvikuru .
Vari kuronga mitambo iyi , uye vari mutambiwo pachavo , Sabhuku Eddie Kandava , vati vakaronga mutambo weKumusha Fringe Festival mushure mekuona kuti vagari vekumaruwa vari kushaya zvinovavaraidza , uye kusimudzira mabasa avanoita akaita sekuimba nekuveza nezvimwe zvakadaro .
VaKandava vati mutambo weKumusha Fringe Festival , uyo uri kutanga neChishanu uchipera neMugovera , uchaitwa gore rega rega kwaSeke , uye shuviro yavo ndeyekubatana nemamwe matunhu kuti aitewo mitambo iyi senzira yekusimudzira mabasa evatambi vari mumatunhu gumi ari muZimbabwe .
Aimbove mushamarari wenhepfenyuro yeZimbabwe Broadcasting Corporation , ZBC , Caleb Tondhlana , uyo akashaya kuSouth Africa nemusi weMuvhuro wapfuura , aradzikwa kumarinda eWarren Hills muHarare .
Tondhlana , kana kuti Mr . CT , akaita mukurumbira apo aishandira nhepfenyuro yeRadio 3 kumakoe ekuma 1980 .
Akazosiya basa kuZBC kuma 1990 achienda kuBotswana , achizobva zvakare onanga kuSouth uko akazvikoenderera mberi nebasa rake rekushamarara pamwe nekusimudzira vaimbi .
Mukoma wemushakabvu , VaMartin Tondhlana , vaudza Studio 7 kuti mhuri yavo yarasikirwa zvikuru sezvo Mr . CT aive munhu aifarira basa rake , kudzidzisa vamwe pamwe nekuriritira mhuri yake .
Mumwe akashanda semutori wenhau panguva iyo aTondhlana aive kuZBC , Ray Moyo , anoti aifarira zvirongwa zvaiitwa naTondhlana uye aive munhu aigona basa rake .
Tondhlana , uyo aive mukoma wemupepeti webepanhau reThe Observer , Banarbas Tondhlana , akazosiya basa rekushamarara ndokutanga mabhizimisi ake izvo akazoshaya achiita muJohannesburg , South Africa .
Tondlana akshaya mushure mekunetsekana nechirwere cheshuga , uye asiya vana vapfumbamwe .
Makundano eCastle Lager Premier Soccer League ave kupinda musvondo repiri maziso ese ari pamurairidzi weDynamos , Paulo Jorge Silva , uyo akonzera mutauro wakanyanya munyika .
Kochii chiri kuitika kuDenamo Dembare ?
Vamwe vatsigiri veDynamos vatove kusheedzera kuti Silva ngaasiiswe basa mushure mekuzvamburwa kwakaitwa chikwata ichi neChicken Inn svondo rapera .
Kunyunyuta uku kunogona kuwedzera kana chikwata ichi chikakundwa nemusi weMugovera apo chiri kusangana neTriangle iyo iri kurairidzwa naDavid Mandigora uyo akadzingwa basa kuDynamos mwaka wapera .
Triangle yakakunda Harare City 1 - 0 mumutambo wayo wekutanga .
Vatungamiri veDynamos vakapa Silva mitambo mina kuti akunde vachiti ivo akatadza anosiiswa basa .
Sachigaro weDynamos , VaKennny Mubaiwa , vanoti ivo zviri mugwara reDynamos kuti murairidzi akatadza basa anodzingwa .
Asi mumwe mutsigiri wechikwata ichi , VaSmart Nyaguse , vanoti Dembare inofanira kupa Silva nguva yekuita basa rake sezvo pari zvino mitambo ichangotanga .
VaNyaguse vanoti sezvo uyu uri mutambo wechipiri mwaka uno havasi kutarisira zvakawanda asi kungotora mapoinzi chete kunyange hazvo zvikasave nemutsindo .
Asi mutambo uri kunyanyotaurwa nezvawo ndeuyo uri kuBarbourfields Stadium pakati pezvikwata zviri kubhebha moto cheHighlanders neche FC Platinum .
Zvikwata zviviri izvi zvakakunda mumitambo yazvo yekutanga , Highlanders yakarakasha Hwange 3 - 0 panguva imwe cheteyo FC Platinum yakadambura Tsholotsho Pirates 2 - 1 .
Mutsigiri weHighlanders , VaProsper Musiyazviriyo , vanoti Highlanders iri kutora mapoinzi matatu mumutambo uyu .
Chikwata chemaGreen Machine cheCaps United chakananga kuNgezi Platinum Stars uko chinemutoro wakaoma .
Zvikwata zviviri izvi zvakakunda nezvibodzwa 3 - 0 svondo rapera , Ngezi Platinum Stars ichi dambura Mutare City ukuwo Caps United ichirova Chapungu .
Zvikwata zvakarohwawo nema 3 - 0 svondo rapera cheHwange neche Chapungu zvirikusanganawo zvekare muAscot Stadium neMugovera .
Zvikwata zvemuBulawayo zviviri cheBulawayo City chirikudamburana nechikwa cheTsholotsho Pirates .
Bulawayo City yakatora poindi imwechete mumutambo wavo wesvondo rapera apo Tsholotsho Pirates yakakunndwa neFC Platinum .
Totarisa mumutambo weRugby .
Chikwata chenyika chemaSevens chemaCheetahs chiri kuHong Kong uko chiri kurwira kupinda mugungano rakakosha neHSBC World Series umo mune zvikwata zviviri chete zvemuAfrica , South Africa neKenya .
Chikwata chemaCheetahs chirimugungano rimwechete neGermany , Hong Kong pamwe nemaCayman Islands , gungano iro murairidzi wechikwa ichiBrighton Chivandire anoti harina kunyanyooma .
Chikwata chichapedza chiripamusoro mugungano iri ndicho chinoenderera mberi mumakundano aya .
Chikwata chimwe chete pazvikwata zvisere zvirikukwidza ndicho chinopinda muHSBC World Series .
Vanhu makumi mana nevashanu pavanhu makumi mapfumbamwe nevasere vakafa mutsaona yemvura yakakonzerwa nedutumupengo Cyclone Idai , vanonzi vavigwa kusvika pari zvino kuChimanimani , mudunhu reManicaland .
Mumiriri wedunhu reManicaland muparamende pasi pehurongwa hweProportional Representation , Amai Lynnette Karenyi veMDC , vanoti vanhu makumi mana vakavigwa neMuvhuro mumusha unogara veruzhinji weNgangu muChimanimani , uye vamwe vehukama vachiri kuedza kutakura mitumbi yehama dzavo kunoichengetedza kumisha yavo .
Amai Karenyi vanoti dunhu reChimanimani East ndiro rakanyanya kurasikirwa nevanhu , sezvo vakawanda vevakashaya vaive vagari vemo .
Vanoti huwandu hwevanhu vakashaya mutsaona iyi hunogona kudarika huri kuziviswa nehurumende sezvo mimwe mitumbi iri kunzi iri kuonekwa ichieredzwa nemvura munzizi .
Amai Karenyi vanotiwo vakaziviswawo nemumwe ishe wekuMozambique kuti kune mimwe mitumbi yakawanikwako inofungidzirwa kuti ndeye zvizvarwa zveZimbabwe .
Vanoti dunhu ravo riri kukumbira rubatsiro rwekuti vakwanise kuviga vakashaya vose , uye mishonga yekurapa vakakuwara , pamwe chete nechikafu chekupa vakaparadzirwa misha yavo .
Mutungamiri weMDC , VaMorgan Tsvangirai , vashaya kuSouth Africa neChitatu mushure mekurwara kwenguva yakareba nechirwere chegomarara .
Mutevedzeri waVaTsvangirai , VaElias Mudzuri , vabvuma kuStudio7 kuti ichokwadi kuti mutangamiri webato ashaya .
VaMudzuri ndivo vakanzi vanotaura nezvehurwere hwaVaTsvangirai vakamirira bato .
Izvi zvatsinhirwawo nehama yepedyo yaVaTsvangirai iyo yati haikwanisi kutaura zvakawanda panguva ino .
VaMudzuri vati bato ravo rarasikirwa zvikuru nekushaya kwaVaTsvangirai .
VaTsvangirai , avo vakamboita mutungamiri wehurumende munguva yehurumende yemubatanidzwa pamwe nebato reZanu PF , vange vave nemakore makumi matanhatu nematanhatu ekuberekwa .
VaTsvangirai vashaya panguva iyi mubato ravo muine makakatanwa ekuti ndiyani akafanobata chigaro chemutungamiri webato iri pakati paVaNelson Chamisa naVaElias Mudzuri .
MDC iri kuita musangano wechimbi chimbi neChina muHarare wekuzeya makakatanwa ari mubato iri .
Vachinyora munganonyorwa yehupenyu hwaVaTsvangirai inonzi """" Morgan Tsvangirai : At the Deep End , vaimbova mutauriri wavo , muchakabvu William Bango vakati VaTsvangirai vakaberekwa musi wa 10 Kurume 1952 kuGutu .
Baba vavo , VaDzingirai Chibwe Tsvangirai , vainge vari mugari wekumaruwa uye vachiveza uye mai wavo vainzi Lydia Tsvangirai .
VaTsvangirai ndivo vainge vari dangwe pavana vapfumbamwe .
Kunyangwe hazvo vanhu vakawanda vasingadi kutaura nezvehurwere hwavo zvikuru zvirwere zvakaita segomarara , VaTsvangirai vakaudza Studio7 kuti vakabuda pachena nekuti vaida kuti mhuri yeZimbabwe inzwisise nezvechirwere chegomarara .
VaTsvangirai vakatanga nyaya dzekumirira vashandi kumugodhi weTrojan Nickel Mine uko vakaenda kunoshanda pamichina kana kuti plant operator mushure mekumboshanda pafekitari imwe vachiita basa rekutsvaira .
Panguva yavo kuTrojan Mine , Vatsvangirai vakatanga kufarira kodzero dzevashandi vakasarudzwa kuita mutevedzeri wemutungamiri weZimbabwe Associated Mine Workers Union .
Mushure memakore matatu vakabva vasarudzwa kuita munyori mukuru weZimbabwe Congress of Trade Unions .
Mumakore anosvika gumi akatevera , VaTsvangirai nevamwe vakaita samuchakabvu Gibson Sibanda vakazoshanda zvakasimba kuti ZCTU iite mutsindo munyika yose ichipikisa zvimwe zvaiitwa nehurumende yaVaMugabe zvaitsikirira kodzero dzemushandi .
Vakatungamira kuratidzirwa kwakaitwa mumakore a1997 kusvika muna 1998 , vakatungamira kuratidzira kunotyisa kwakaitwa nevashandi nyika yose vachiratidza kusafara nemamiriro ehupfumi munyika .
VaTsvangirai vakazosiya chigaro chekuva munyori mukuru muZCTU muna 1999 vopinda munyaya dzezvematongerwo enyika .
Kuumbwa kweMDC muna 1999
Vakabatanawo nemamwe masangano munyika kuti varwire kodzero dzevanhu zvakapa kuti vazoguma vaumba bato rinopikisa reMovement for Democratic Change muna 1999 vachitsigirwa neZCTU nesangano revadzidzi reZINASU nemamwe akawanda munyika .
VaTsvangirai ndivo vange vachitungamira bato reMDC kubva zvarakaumbwa .
Vakakwikwidza musarudzo dzemuna
VaTsvangirai vakamboitawo sachigaro weNational Constitutional Assembly sasachigaro weTaskforce yesangano iri .
Vakashanda nevamwe musangano iri vakaita saMuzvinafundo Lovemore Madhuku , Welshman Ncube , Everjoice Win , Brian Kagoro , Tendai Biti and Priscilla Misihairabwi .
NCA yakakunda hurumende yaVaMugabe musarudzo dzereferendum yebumbiro remutemo yakaitwa muna 2000 .
VaTsvangirai vaigarawo vachisungwa nekupomerwa mhosva huru dzaigona kuti vatongerwe rufu kana kuti treason .
Muna 2001 vakasungwa vakapomerwa mhosva iyi pasi pemutemo weLaw and order Maitaninace Act vachinzi vaida kukurudzira vanhu kuti vapandukire nekupidigura hurumende yaVaMugabe nechisimba .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzezvematongerwo enyika dzinoti vaipomerwa mhosva iyi nehurumende yaVaMugabe kuti vasakwikwidze musarudzo dzemuna 2002 .
VaTsvangirai vakapinda musarudzo idzi asi havana kutambira zvakabuda vachiti dzakabirirwa uye dzaive nemhirizhonga inotyisa .
Nyika dzakaita seAmerica neBritain dzakabva dzatemera VaMugabe nevamwe vavo zvirango .
VaTsvangirai vakasungwawo kakawanda vachipomerwa mhosva yekuda kupidigura VaMugabe iyi asi vachingochenurwa nedare .
Muna 2005 mushure mekunetsana nevaive munyori mukuru webato ravo VaWelshman Ncube , bato reMDC rakapatsanuka kekutanga .
Muhurukuro dzakawanda VaTsvangirai vakati kupatsanuka kwebato uku kwakavarwadza zvikuru .
Musi wa11 Kurume muna 2007 , Vatsvangirai nevamwe vatungamiri vebato ravo vakaita saVatendai Biti nasachigaro weNCA VaLovemore Madhuku vakarohwa zvakaipisisa vari muhusungwa apo vaienda kuhurongwa hwekunonamatira nyika kuHighfield .
Muna 2008 Zimbabwe yakaita sarudzo dzakaonekwa sedzakachena nenyika dzakawanda zvakapa kuti bato reMDC rikunde Zanu - PF musarudzo dzenhengo dzedare reparamende .
Asi musarudzo yemutungamiri wenyika VaTsvangirai vakanzi vainge vatadza kusvika mavhoti aidiwa kunyange vainge vakunda VaMugabe .
Nekudaro pakanzi paitwe sarudzo yepiri yemutungamiri wenyika kana kuti election run - off .
Sarudzo yepiri iri haina kuzoitwa nenyaya yemhirizhonga yakaona vatsigiri vakawanda vaVaTsvangirai vachirasikirwa nehupenyu zvakapa kuti vabude mukukwikwidza sarudzo yacho .
Hurumende yemubatanidzwa
Vaimbova mutungamiri weSouth Africa , VaThabo Mbeki , ndivo vakave mutongi gava weSADC pagakava reZimbabwe kukazoguma kwaumbwa hurumende yemubatanidzwa muna 2009 VaTsvangirai vari mutungamiri wehurumende , VaMugabe vachiramba vari mutungamiri wenyika .
Hurumende yemubatanidzwa yakasvika kwamvura yacheka makumbo muna 2013 .
VaTsvangirai vakashanyirawo nyika dzakawanda panguva iyi vachitambirwa segamba .
Vakapihwawo mibayiro yakawanda kusanganisira kudomwa mumakwikwi eNobel Peace Prize .
MaUniversity maviri ekuSouth Korea akavapawo ruremekedzo rwedoctorate .
VaTsvangirai vasiya vana vanomwe uye mudzimai , Elizabeth Macheka Tsvangirai , mudzimai wavo wekutanga , Amai Susan Tsvangirai kwemakore aidarika makumi matatu nerimwe , akashaya munjodzi yemumugwagwa muna 2009 .
VaTsvangirai vakasara vakuvara mutsaona iyi .
Vagari vemumaguta nemadhorobha , pamwe nenyanzvi vanoti nyaya yekuti vanhu vanoramba vachibatwa nezvirwere zvemanyoka zvakaita setyphoid nekorera zvinoratidza kuti hurumende nemakunzuru hazvisi kushandisa mari zvine mwero kwenguva yakareba .
Hurumende ine mutemo unoti makanzuru anofanirwa kushandisa zvikamu makumi manomwe kubva muzana zvemabhajeti awo kuita mabasa akaita sekuwanisa vanhu mvura yakachena nekutakura marara uye zvikamu makumi matatu kubva muzana semari yemihoro .
Asi izvi handizvo zviri kuitika sezvo makanzuru mazhinji munyika ave kutotambirisa mari yakakwira kudarika makambani anoshanda akazvimirira .
Semuenzaniso , mukoti wemukanzuru yeHarare anotambira zviuru zviviri nemazana mashanu emadhora asi mukoti anoshandira hurumebde achitambira mazana mashanu emadhora .
Vaimbove meya VeHarare , VaBenard Manyenyeni , vanoti nyaya yemihoro yevashandi ndiyo yauraya kanzuru yeHarare .
VaManyenyeni vanoti kanzuru iyi haigoni kuita basa rayo nekuda kwenyaya iyi .
Mukuru werimwe remasangano anomirira vagari vemuHarare , reHarare Resident Trust , VaPrecious Shumba , vaudza Studio7 kuti hurumende inofanira kumisa zvese izvi yowona kuti mari yemvura yashandiswa mabasa emvura .
Vanotiwo nyaya yehuwori mukanzuru ndiyo iri kuita makanzuru aya atadze kutakura marara nekupa vanhu mvura yakachena izvo zvinokonzera kuwanda kwetsvina nezvirwere zvemudumbu .
VaManyenyeni vanotiwo nyaya yekuti hurumende , vagari nemakambani havasi kubhadhara mitero inoomeserawo kunzuru nekuitadzisa kuita mabasa ayo zvinozopedzisira zvakonzera zvirwere zvakaita sekorera .
Mutauriri wekanzuru , VaMichael Chideme , vanoti havadi kuti vagari vabatwe nezvirwere , uye zvakakosha kuti vanhu vabhadhare mitero kuitira kuti kanzuru ikwanise kuivaitira zvese zvakaita sekuvapa mvura yakachena .
MuHarare nemamwe madhorobha vanhu vanogara vakabatwa nezvirwere zvinokonzerwa netsvina nekushaikwa kwemvura yakachena nekusatakurwa kwemarara .
Iko zvino pane vanhu makumi mana nemapfumbabwe vafana nechirwere korera uye hurumende yave kuita chipata pata chekutsvaga rubatsiro kuti ikwanise kurapa nekumisa kupararira kwechirwere .
Mukuru wezvirwere zvekutapurirana mubazi rezvehutano , Dr Portia Manangazira , vanoti zvirwere zvekorera netyphoid zvave kunetsa kurapika zvopa kuti vape vanhu nhomba kuti vasatapurirwe chirwere ichi .
VaManyenyeni nenyanzvi munyaya dzehupfumi , VaMasimba Manyanya , vanoti mafambisirwe ari kuitwa hurumende handiwo vachiti nyika haingararame nekupemha .
Vanoti hurumende nemakanzuru vanofanira kugara vaine mari parutivi yekubatsira kana pachange paita dambudziko rakaita sekorera .
Tsvagiridzo ichangobva mukuitwa neUniversity of Zimbabwe , inoratidzawo kuti zvirango zvakatemerwa Zimbabwe zvakakanganisawo zvikuru mabasa ezvehutano munyika .
Zvakabuda mutsvakiridzo iyi , iyo yakaitirwa bazi rezvedzidzo yepamusoro neUniversity of Zimbabwe , zvinoratidza kuti mari yerubatsiro kunyika nemakanzuru munyika yakadzikira nekuda kwezvirango uye kuti mitengo yezvinhu nemabasa yakakwirawo zvakanyanya .
Tsvagiridzo iyi inotiwo hurumende nemakanzuru vanofanira kutsvaga nzira dzekukunganidza mari muno kwete kumirira vekunze .
Nyika dzakawanda nemasangano ekunze nemakambani akazvimira ndivo vari kubatsira zvakanyanya mukurwisana nekokera pamwe nekubatsira makanzuru kuita mabasa ekuwanisa vanhu mvura pamwe nekutakura marara .
Bazi rezvedzidzo rinoti pane zvikoro zvakawanda zvehurumende nezvimwe zvakazvimirira zvoga zvaisa zvikumbiro zvekuti zvikwidze mari dzinobhadharwa nevana muzvikoro kutanga gore rinouya .
Zvikoro zvizhinji zvehurumende zviri kuda kuwedzera mari dzedzidzo nemitero nemadhora ari pakati pemakumi matatu nemakumi mashanu pamari iri kubvisa kare .
Gurukota rezvedzidzo , Va David Coltart , vanoti bazi ravo riri kutarisisa nyaya idzi .
Vatiwo panyaya yemari yechikoro , vanotarisira kuti zvikoro zvitange zvawirirana nevabereki vasati vakwidza zvikumbiro zvavo kubazi ravo .
Vakafanobata chinzvimbo chemunyori webazi redzidzo , Amai Elizabeth Marunda , vanoti bazi ravo richiri kuongorora kuti zvikumbiro izvi zvotambirwa here kana kuti kwete .
Bazi redzidzo riri kutizve zvikoro hazvifaniri kuti vana vari kutsvaga nzvimbo dze form one vabhadhriswe mari yakawanda yekunyora bvunzo yekutsvaga nzvimbo nekuti vari kubira vabereki .
Pfungwa yekuda kukwidza mari idzi inonzi iri kutsamwisa vabereki vazhinji .
Mumwe mubereki ava muHarare , Va Friday Tendai , vanoti havasi kufara nenyaya yekukwidzwa kwemari idzi nokuti vanhu havasi kutambiriswa mari dzakawanda .
Kunyange hazvo ndege yeEthiopian Airlines yakadonha neSvondo mangwanani ikauraya vanhu vose vaive mundege iyi , vamwe vanoshandisa ndege idzi pavanenge vachishanya kuAfrica vachibva kuAmerica vanoti vacharamba havo vachishandisa ndege dzeEthiopian Airlines sezvo iri nani pane dzimwe ndege dzavanomboshandisa .
Chizvarwa cheZimbabwe chiri muCalifornia , Doctor Angela Gapa , vanoti mubasa ravo ravanoita vanoona Ethiopian Airlines iri nyore kushandisa .
Doctor Gapa vanoti ndege zhinji dzinobva kuLos Angeles , muCalifornia dzichienda kuAfrica dzinoshandisa nzira refu dzinoita kuti munhu upedze munguva yakareba usati wasvika kwauri kuenda .
Semuenzaniso , Doctor Gapa vanoti kana vachienda kuZimbabwe vanogona kutora ndege yeEthiopian Airlines inovasvitsa muAddis Ababa , vozotora imwe ndege inoenda kuHarare mushure mekumira muEthiopia kwenguva pfupi .
Doctor Gapa vanoti kana vakashandisa dzimwe ndege , vanotanga vaenda kuEurope uko vanosvika mangwanani vopedza zuva rese vakamirira ndege yemanheru kuti vaende kuZimbabwe .
Ndege yeEthiopian Airlines Flight 302 yakaita tsaona mangwanani eSvondo maminetsi mashoma ichangosimuka muEthiopia ichienda kuNairobi , kuKenya , vanhu vose vaive mundege iyi vakafa .
Tsaona iyi ndeye chipiri kuitika kumhando yeBoing 737 Max 8 , zvichitevera imwe tsaona yakaitika mwedzi mitanhatu yapfuura pedyo neIndonesia , vanhu vose vaive mundege iyi zana nemakumi masere nevapfumbamwe vakafa .
Mhando yeBoing 737 Max 8 inonzi ndiyo iri kufarirwa zvakanyanya nemambani endege , zvekuti pane dzimwe ndege itsva zviuru zvishanu dzakatomirirwa nemakambani endege kuti vadzishandise .
Ndege yemhando iyi yakatanga kushandiswa muna 2017 .
Zvichitevera tsaona iyi , makambani endege emuAmerica anoti Southwest Airlines , Air Canada neUnited Airlines , anoti acharamba achishandisa ngege dzemhando iyi , asi China inonzi yambomisa kushandisa ndege dzayo makumi mapfumbamwe nenhanhatu dzemhando iyi .
Dembare yaunganidza vatambi vakawanda vechidiki vasina mukurumbira avo murairidzi wavo , Lloyd Chigove , ane chivimbo chakasimba kuti vachamubatsira mwaka uno wenhabvu .
Chigove anoti ari kuda kurasa tsika yekuti vatambi vamwe chetevo ndivo vanenge vachingofamba kubva kune chimwe chikwata vachienda kune chimwe panguva yezororo yemitambo achiti iye ari kuda kuunza vatambi vatsva mudariro .
Dembare ichange zvekare ichiratidza vatambi vaviri vakabva kunze kwenyika , Ngandu Mankala na Diamon Onedika Katako avo vakabva kuDemocratic Republic of Congo .
Asi Chigove atsvagawo vamwe vatambi vane mazita munhabvu yemuZimbabwe kusanganisira Edward Sadomba uyo aitamba kuSudan , Archierford Gutu aive kuSweden , Kudzanai Dhembere uyo Dembare yakatenga kuHarare City , Edward Mhungu kubva kuHerentals , na Kudzai Chideu uyo aitambira Chicken Inn mwaka wapera .
Mumwe muteveri wechikwata ichi , VaBatai Kwayedza , vanoti pavakapedisira kuona chikwata chavo chaitonyadzisa zvekuti vari kuda kuti Chigove agadzirise zvavakaona mwaka wapera .
Asi VaKwayedza vachaona chikwata cheDembare chakasiyana zvikuru nechemwaka wapera sezvo Chigove atsiva vatambi vakaenda kune zvimwe zvikwata nevechidiki vakaita sa Munya Kawadza , Emmanuel Jalayi , Rodwell Mhlanga , Jerome Nyatenge , joseph Mutembedza , Tanaka Chiengeta Munyaradzi Chipo , Tatenda Hapazari , Tafadwa Ngwena , nevamwe vakadaro .
Mwaka wapera Dynamos yakatatarika zvikuru ndokupedza iri pachinhanho chegumi asi mumwe muteveri wechikwata ichi , VaMoses Mukanda , vanoti mukombe ndewavo gore rino .
Chigove pachake ari kutarisira kufadza chaunga chinotevera chikwata ichi icho anoti chave kudarika mamiriyoni manomwe .
Asi Chigove anofanira kuyambirwa kuti pasina zvibodzwa nemikombe , kuDynamos hakugarike .
Nhengo dzeparamende dzashatirwa mushure mekunge sangano reZimbabwe Football Association ( ZIFA ) nekanzuru yeBulawayo vatadza kunopa humbowo kudare mushure mekunge sangano rezvenhabvu muAfrica reConfederation of African Football ( CAF ) rati nhandare dzese dzemuZimbabwe hadzikodzeri kutambirwa nhabvu .
Nhengo dzekomiti inoona nezvevechidiki nemutambo dzaratidza kusafara nekuita kweZIFA dzichiti hazvishamisi kuti mutambo wenhabvu wasvika pauri munyika nekuti ZIFA haikoshesi basa rayo pamwe nedare reparamende .
Imwe nhengo yekomiti iyi , Muzvare Tatenda Mavetera veZanu PF , vati danho reCAF rakabata vakawanda nevatsigiri venhabvu munyika uye kana ZIFA isingakoshesi izvi , zvinoreva kuti haina hany'a nenhabvu .
VaOmega Sibanda veZanu PF varatidzawo kusafara nekuita kweZIFA nekanzuru yeBulawayo vachiti ndivo vanhu vange vakanyanya kukosha kukomiti yeparamende
VaGift Banda veMDC vatiwo zvange zvakakosha kuti ZIFA ive pamusangano wanhasi sezvo iri iyo inotaura neCAF ichizozivisa vamwe vese zvinenge zvabva kuCAF .
Vachipa humbowo pamusoro penyaya iyi , vakafanobata chinzvimbo chemunyori mubazi rezvematunhu , VaJoseph Mhakayaora , vati zvose zvinodiwa neCAF zvingadai zvagadzirwa munhandare yeNational Sports Stadium dai vaipihwa mari nehurumende .
Vati nhandare iyi yakapedzisira kugadziridzwa makore gumi apfuura nemari yakabva kuChina .
Vati gore rapfuura chairo vakaisa bhajeti remamiriyoni mazana maviri nemakumi mana emadhora rekusimudzira National Sports Stadium , asi hapana chakabuda .
Asi vakafanobata chinzvimbo chemunyori mubazi revechidiki nemitambo , VaBenson Martins Dube , vaudza paramende kuti hurumende yakataoudza ZIFA kuti inyorere kuCAF ichiikoka kuti izoongorora zvakare National Sports Stadium neBarbourfields sezvo nhandare idzi dziri kugadziriswa .
Vati hurumende iri kushandisa mamiriyoni makumi matatu nematatu ekugadzirisa nhandare idzi uye vati vanovimba kuti dzichange dzapera kugadziriswa mukati memazuva gumi nemana ari kuetevera .
Zvichakadai , CAF yanyorera ZIFA ichiramba chikumbiro chekuti iongorore zvakare nhandare idzi ikati inoda kuti Zimbabwe idome nhandare iri kunze kweZimbabwe yainoda kutambira mutambo weZimbabwe neAlgeria .
Mutauriri ZIFA , VaXolisani Gwesela , vaudza Studio 7 kuti hongu vatambira gwaro iri kubva kuCAF mushure mekunyorera sangano iri neMuvhuro .
VaGwesela vatiwo vatadza kuenda paramende nhasi sezvo vange vakabatikana uye vakanyorera kuparamende neChitatu vachiti musangano wanhasi uendeswe mberi .
Mutungamiri weSouth Africa , VaCyril Ramaposa , vakumbira ruregerero kuvanhu vanga vari kuNational Sports Stadium pamusoro pemhirizhonga iri kuita kunyika kwavo vachiti vane hurombo nezvakaitika sezvo zvisingaenderane nezvinhu zvaidiwa nevaimbove mutungamiri wenyika , VaRobert Mugabe , pamwe nevamwe vatungamiri vakaita saVaNelson Mandela .
Vachitaura kuNational Sports Stadium mushure mekusveveredzwa nevanhu , VaRamaposa vati zvakaitika kunyika kwavo hazvina kunaka uye hazvisi zvinhu zvakarwirwa nevatungamiriri vakaita saVaMugabe .
VaRamaphosa vati South Africa inyika isingavenge zvizvarwa zvedzimwe nyika dzemuAfrica vachiti nyika idzi dzakabatsira South Africa apo yaive panguva yakaoma .
Veruzhinji vazofarira mashoko aVaRamaphosa mushure mekunge vakumbira ruregerero nekuda kwemhirizhonga iri kuitika kuSouth Africa .
VaCris Mutsvanga ndemumwe weavo vafara chose nekuda kwezvaitwa naVaRamaphosa .
Munyori mubazi rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , VaNick Mangwana , vaudza Studio 7 kuti vanokudza zvikuru zvaitwa naVaRamaposa .
VaRamaphosa , mumwe wevatungamiri venyika dzemuAfrica vanga vari kuNational Sports Stadium .
Mutungamiri weKenya , VaUhuru Kenyatta , varumbidza VaMugabe nebasa guru ravakaita pakusungura Zimbabwe neAfrica .
Vamwe vanga vari pahurongwa uhu vanosanganisira vaimbovc mutungamiri weGhana , VaJerry Rawlings , VaKenneth Kaunda vekuZambia , VaOluseguni Obassanjo vekuNigeria nevamwe .
Mutumbi waVaMugabe unotarisirwa kuenda kumusha kwavo kwaZvimba mangwana uye ndivo gamba rezana nemakumi matatu neshanu richaradzikwa paNational Heroes Acre , asi zuva richaitwa izvi harisati razivikanwa .
Pane magamba gumi nemaviri echidzimai akaradzikwa paHeroes Acre anosanganisira mukadzi waVaMugabe wekutanga , Amai Sally Heyfron Mugabe .
Zvichakadai VaMangwana vati VaMugabe vachavigwa muguva repamusoro soro rinonzi Musoleum iro rave kugadzira nehurumende paHeroes Acre .
VaMangwana vati madzishe nemhuri yaVaMugabe vakatotara guva raVaMugabe , uye mutumbi waVaMugabe uchazovigwa muguva iri kana rapera kugadzirwa .
VaMangwana vati ijana remhuri kuchengeta mutumbi apo guva raVaMugabe rinenge richigadzirwa .
VaMangwana vati hurumende ndiyo ichabhadhara zvese zvichaitwa pakugadzirisa guva raVaMugabe .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzekuchengeta zvitunha dzinoti zvinokosha madhora ekuAmerica makumi mashanu kana kudarika kuchengeta chitunha pazuva .
Imwe nyanzvi yezvehutano hwepfungwa inoti zvakakosha chose kuti vanhu vane dambudziko rehutano hwepfungwa vapiwe rutsigiro nevanhu vari pedyo navo kuitira kuvabatsira kuti vakwanise kurarama munharaunda dzavagere .
Doctor William Guri , avo vanoshanda neboka rezvehutano hwepfungwa kuvana vadiki kuBritain , vanoti basa ravo ndere kupa rutsigiro muzvikoro , kuvana , kuvadzidzisi nekuvabereki , nechinangwa chekuti vana vakwanise kuwana rutsigiro vachiri vadiki kuitira kuti vazokura vakasimba muhutano hwavo hwepfungwa .
Doctor Guri vanoti basa rehutano hwepfungwa rinogona kuonekwa nevamwe sebasa risina kukosha , asi ibasa rakaskosha kwazvo rinofanirwa kutsigirwa nedzihurumende pamwe neveruzhinji .
Vanoti pane zvakawanda zvinokonzera kuti munhu arware nepfungwa , zvinosanganisira kuomerwa nehupenyu , hurwere hweshuramatongo hweHIV / AIDS , kana kushaya basa chaiko .
Doctor Guri vanotiwo ongororo dzavari kusanganawo nadzo dziri kuratidza kuti chirwere chiriko iye zvino ichi che Covid - 19 , chiri kukonzerawo zvakare kuti vanhu vakanganiswe hutano hwepfungwa kuburikidza nekugara vanhu vakavharirwa mudzimba vasingasangane nevamwe kungava kumabasa , kunzvimbo dzekudyira , kana kumitambo .
Vanotiwo murwere weCovid - 19 kana akasashanyirwa kuchipatara nehama neshamwari , anogona kukanganisika pfungwa zvakare .
Zvizvarwa zveku China zvinomwe zvakapihwa mukana wekubvisa mari yechibatiso kuitira kuti zvitongwe zvichibva kumba , zvichiri mu remand prison sezvo magwaro azvo asati apera kugadzirwa .
Vasungwa ava , avo vakasungwa ku Victoria Falls gore rapera mushure mekuwanikwa vaine zvidimbu zvenyanga dzechipemberere dzinorema makirogiramu makumi maviri , vakanzi vabhadhare zviuru zvishanu pamunhu zvemadhora ema RTGS .
Vakanziwo vazvipire kumapurisa epa Victoria Falls katatu pazuva , uye kuisa mapasipoti avo mumaoko amabharani wematare .
Gweta riri kumirira vasungwa ava , Va Givemore Muvhiringi , vati vachiri kugadzirisa magwaro ekuti varume veku China ava vaburitswe muhusungwa neMugovera .
Va Muvhiringi vati vasungwa ava vari kutarisirwa kumira zvakare pamberi pedare nemusi weMuvhuro , sezvinodiwa nemutemo , kunyange hazvo vachange vachibva kudzimba dzavo .
Komiti yakaumbwa negurukota rezvematunhu , Va July Moyo , kuitira kuti iferefeta huori hunonzi huri kuitwa nemakanzura eguta reMarondera , yakatanga kuita basa rayo nemusi weMuvhuro .
Komiti iyi yakatambirwa zviri pamutemo muguta iri nameya weguta reMarondera , VaChengetai Murova .
Komiti iyi iri kutarisirwa kupedza basa rayo rekuferefeta makanzura eMarondera nemusi weChishanu .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kubata VaMoyo kuti tinzwe divi rebazi ravo panyaya iyi , asi mutevedzeri wegurukota rezvekutongwa kwematunhu , Amai Marian Chombo , vakaudza Studio7 pakabuda runyerekupe rwekuti hurumende iri kuronga kuferefeta makanzura eMarondera kuti komiti iyi yakaumbwa mushure mekunge vagari vekuMarondera vanyorera bazi ravo vachigunun'una
nehuori hwavanoti huri kuitwa mukanzuru yeguta guru redunhu reMashonaland East .
Amai Chombo vakatiwo hachisi chokwadi kuti hurumende yeZanu PF yakanangana nekuda kubvisa makanzura eMDC anotonga maguta ose ari munyika .
Asi VaMurova vanoti kunyange hazvo kanzuru yavo isina huori hwairi kuita , chinovanetsa ndechekuti hurumende inongoda kuferefeta chete makanzuru ari pasi peMDC .
VaMurova vanoti vachashanda nekomiti iyi sezvinodiwa nemutemo sezvo kanzuru yavo isina zvairi kuvanza .
Munyori wezvekutongwa kwematunhu muMDC inotungamirwa naVaNelson Chamisa , Engineer Elias Mudzuri , vanoti hurumende haina kuvazivisa nezvekuda kwayo kuferefeta kanzuru iri pasi peMDC .
VaMudzuri vanoti havana chivimbo chekuti hurumende iri kuita izvi mune rakanaka sezvo iri garoziva kuti hurumende yeZanu PF yagara ichibvongodza pamwe nekupindira mumashandiro akanaka anenge achiitwa nebato ravo .
VaMudzuri , avo vakava meya weMDC wekutanga muguta reHarare , vanoti kana hurumende iri kufungidzira kuti makanzuru eMDC ari kuita zvehuori , inofanirwa kusiya Zimbabwe Anti Corruption Commission , Zaac , ichiita basa rayo rekuferefeta huroyi pamwe nekusunga vanenge vabatwa nemhosva .
"""" Zaac ndizvo zvayakaummbirwa kuti isunge vanoita zvehuori , saka handioni chinangwa chekuumbira komiti yekuti iferefete kanzuru iri pasi peMDC .
Hazviratidzi zvakanaka kuti rimwe bato riti riri kuongorora rimwe bato , """" vadaro VaMudzuri .
Sangano rinomirira varairidzi vekumaruwa , reAmalgamated Rural Teachers' Union of Zimbabwe , ARTUZ , rinoti varairidzi vakawanda pamwe nevamwe vashandi vehurumende vachakundikana kunge vaendesa zvinokwanisa kuti vazivikanwe sevashandi vehurumende kana kuti biometrics pachapera nguva yatarwa nehurumende .
ARTUZ inoti izvi zviri kukonzerwa nekushaya kwevashandi vakawanda mari dzekufambisa kuenda kumahofisi ari kunyoresa vanhu .
Mutungamiri weARTUZ VaObert Masaraure vanoti gore rapera , sangano ravo rakanga rakumbira kuhurumende kuti iise vashandi vanopinda muzvikoro ichitora humbowo hwemunhu uhwu , asi hurumende chayakangoita kuwedzera nguva yechirongwa ichi .
Bepanhau reHerald rinoti gwaro rakanyorwa nemunyori mubazi rezvevashandi nemabasa , VaJonathan Wutawunashe richienda kuvashandi vehurumende vese , rakatara musi wa 28 mwedzi uno waKukadzi sezuva rekupedzisira kuti vashandi vese vehurumende vange vanyoresa .
Gwaro iri rinonzi riri kuti anenge asina kunyoresa zvakare pasi pechirongwa ichi haazokwanisa kuramba achitambiriswa muhoro wake .
Hatina kukwanisa kunzwa divi rehurumende pachikumbiro chekuti iise vashandi muzvikoro vanonyora varairidzi .
Kusawirirana pakati pemutambi Christian Ntouba Joel Epoupa nechikwata chake cheDynamos kunonzi nevakawanda kwave kupa kuti chikwata ichi chirambe chichitatarika mumakwikwi eCastle Premier Soccer League .
Asi ikozvino ave kutarisirwa kudzoka kuzotambira chikwata ichi .
Nemusi weSvondo , kambani iri kutsigira Dynamos yeNetOne nevakuru vechikwata ichi vakazivisa kuti Epoupa uyo ange ari kuramba kutambira chikwata ichi achiti haana kupihwa mari dzake ainge apihwa zvekuti vari kushamisika kuti sei asiri kutamba nhabvu .
Asi pamusangano uyu , Epoupa namaneja wake Gilbert Sengwe havana kuuya zvopa kuti zvinetse kunzwisisa kuti chii chiri kunetsa .
Apo kunetsana uku kuri kuenderera , mberi , chikwata cheDynamos chave pachinzvimbo chechipiri kubva pasi pasi mushure mekufamba ndokunoita mangange neZPC Kariba iyo iri pasi pasi pegungano rezvikwata gumi nezvisere reCastle Lager Premier Soccer League .
Dynamos yakaita 0 - 0 neZPC izvo zvavasiya vaine mapoindi maviri chete kubva mumitambo mishanu uyezve vanwisa zvibodzwa zvitatu chete ivo vakakandwa zvibodzwa zvitanhatu .
Mumwe mutsigiri wechikwata ichi VaMichael Bundo vanoti vari kurwadzikana zvikuru nekutadza kurova ZPC Kariba iyo ine poindi imwe chete chete mugungano rePremier Soccer League iri .
VaBundo vanoti murairidzi wavo Lloyd Mutasa anofanira kugadzirisa chikwata ichi nechimbi chimbi kana achida kubatana nezvikwata zviri pamusoro soro .
Mumusha weDembare uyu matove nemutauro vamwe vatsigiri vechikwata ichi vachishevedzera kuti Mutasa anofanira kusiiswa basa .
Mutasa wacho anoti kana vatungamiri veDynamos vafunga kuti nguva yake yakwana anozvipira kupa vamwe varairidzi mukana .
Asi mumusha weNgezi Platinum Stars hamuna matambudziko kunge ane Dembare mushure mekunge Madamburo yarova Chicken Inn 1 - 0 ndokuramba iri pamusoro pehurongwa hweCastle Lager Premier Soccer League .
Uyu wave mutambo wechishanu Ngezi Platinum Stars ichikunda mumitambo mishanu yatambwa parizvino mugungano renhabvu yepamusoro iri .
Murairidzi weNgezi Platinum Stars Tonderai Ndiraya anoti chikwata chake chaive chakasimba panzvimbo dzose uye kurova kwavo Chicken Inn iyo yakambotora mukombe weligi uyu muna 2015 munongedzo wekuti chikwata chavo chakasimba .

Musangano weGlobal Initiative for Responsible Mining , uyo uri kutsvaka kubvumirana kwenyika pasi pose mirairo yekubatwa kwevanhu vanoita basa rekuchera zviwanikwa pamwe chete nenzizi dziri kuparadzwa nekuchera uku , uri kuitwa muguta re Vancouver kuCanada .
Musangano uyu waunganidza varidzi vemakambani emigodhi , masangano anomiririra vashandi ne anorwira kodzero dzevanhu , vatengi vezvicherwa nevamwe vanechekuita nezvezvicherwa kuti vakurukure nekubvumirana nzira nemitemo yakanaka , inochengetedza vanhu vanoita basa rekuchera , vana nenzizi dziri padyo nepanocherwa .
Mukuru weHuman Rights Watch kuchamhembe kwe Africa , VaDewa Mavhinga , avo vari kumusangano uyu , vaudza Studio 7 kuti musangano uyu une basa zvikuru kunyika yakaita se Zimbabwe ine migodhi yakawanda uye ine vanhu vazhinji vanorarama nekuchera zviwanikwa .
VaMavhinga vati chimwe chinhu chikuru chiri kukurukurwa pamusangano uyu , inyaya ye kuchengetedzwa kwevana vanomanikidzwa nenhamo kuchera zviwanikwa kuti vararamise mhuri dzavo .
Vati mamwe emakambani ari pamusangano uyu anosanganisa Anglo American , de Beers , Microsoft , Tiffany's , nemamwe .

Vane ruzivo nezvakaitika vanoti vamwe vaviri vanochengetedza mhuka kubva kubazi reZimparks vakaita mahwekwe nevanofungidzirwa vaizvhima zvisiri pamutemo mudhamu reKariba .

Bazi rinoona nezvemitemo muAmerica , reDepartment of Justice ( DOJ ) , rinoti ongororo yarakaita inoratidza kuti chikoro chepamusoro , cheYale University , chinoita rusarura mukutambira kwacho vadzidzi .
DOJ inoti Yale University inonyima nzvimbo dzechikoro vamwe vadzidzi vechichena vemuAmerica nevamwe vadzidzi vemu America vari vechirudzi cheku Asia .
DOJ inoti ongororo yayo yakatora makore maviri .
Gore rapfuura , dare redzimhosva rakawana chimwe chikoro chepamusoro , Harvard University , chisina mhosva yerusarura mushure mekunge DOJ yaiendesa kumatare edzimhosva nenyaya yerusarura , ichiti vamwe vadzidzi vechichena nevechi Asia vemuAmerica vakange vachishaiswa nzvimbo pachikoro ichi kuchitorwa vemamwe marudzi .
Vanodzidzisa paDeVry University , Muzvinafundo Elliot Masocha , vanoti DOJ iri kutambisa nguva sezvo zvikoro zvepamusoro zvizhinji zvichiita izvi .
Vanoti zvikoro zvepamusoro zvinoita izvi senzira yekuti vadzidzi vavo vazive pamusoro pevanhu nezvenyika dzakasiyanasiyana , kwete zverusarura .
Yale University yakaramba mashoko aya ichiti haina kupiwa nguva yakakwana yekupa DOJ ruzivo rwese pamusoro pemashandiro anoita chikoro ichi kana chichisarudza vadzidzi .
Yale inoti haisi kuzochinja maitiro ayo pamusoro pezvainoti mashoko asina chokwadi uye asina maturo anobva kuDOJ .

Sangano rinoona nezvemotokari dzinotakura zvinorema reTransport Operators Association of Zimbabwe , TOAZ , rinoti riri kushushikana zvikuru nevatyairi vari kutakura zvinodhaka , uye rakatosungisa vamwe vatyairi gumi nevashanu pazororo rekisimusi .
Mukuru anoona nezvekufambiswa kwebasa musangano iri , VaJeremiah Maruza , vanoti donzvo ravo nderekuti motokari dzenhengo dzaro dzisashandiswe kutakura zvinodhaka izvo zvinopesana nemitemo yenyika .
VaMaruza , avo vanoti vari kuita chirongwa chekuongorora motokari dzenhengo dzavo kuti hadzisi kutakuriswa zvinodhaka , vanoti vakatobata vatyairi gumi nevashanu kubva musiwa 18 Zvita kusvika 26 Zvita .
VaMaruza vanoti vakawanda vevatyairi vakasungwa vainge vakatakura zvinodhaka zvakaita sembanje , hwahwa nemapiritsi pamwe nemabhero ehembe .
VaMaruza vanoti basa ravo riri kudzoserwa kumashure nemapurisa ayo vanoti havasi kunyatsoshandirana pamwechete navo .
Vanoti mapurisa vari kugarira nyaya dzavanenge vavapa zvinoratidza kuti panenge paitwa huori .
Sangano reTOAZ rinoti rimwe dambudziko guru ravanosangana naro ndere nhengo dzavo dzinosungirwa mhosva inenge yaparwa nevatyairi vavo zvichinzi motokari dzavo ndidzo dzinenge dzakatakura zvisingabvumirwe .
Mumwe anotengesa mbatya dzemumabhero anoda kuzivikanwa nezita rekuti Antony anoti vanoshandisa motokari dzinotakura zvinorema nekuti hadziongororwe zvakanyanya sezvinoitwa mabhazi .
Mutauriri wemapurisa mudunhu reMashonaland West , VaClemence Mabgweazara , vanobvuma kuti pane vatyairi vakasungwa asi havana huwandu hwavo .
VaMaruza vanoti vamwe vatyairi gumi nevaviri vakasungwa kuBeitbridge vamwe vana vakasungwa kwaMutare paForbes .
Masangano ose anomirira varairidzi asangana neMuvhuro nevamiriri vebazi rezvedzidzo pamwe neveboka rinoona nezvebvunzo , reZimbabwe Schools Examination Xouncil , ZIMSEC , kuti vazeye nezvemari dzinofanirwa kubhadharwa varairidzi vachanyoresa kana kumaka bvunzo gore rino .
Izvi zvinotevera yambiro yakanga yapiwa nevarairidzi yekuti vakanga vasiri kuzonyoresa kana kumaka bvunzo dzegore rino kana mari dzavanobhadharwa dzisina kuwedzerwa .
Varairidzi ava vaiti hurumende haisati yavabhadhara mari dzavo dzavakashandira makore adarika .
Munyori wePTUZ , VaRaymond Majongwe vanoti vafadzwa nemafambiro aita musangano wavo , uye vavimbiswa kuti zvichemo zvavo zvichatarisiswa .
VaMajongwe vanoti vaudzwa kuti zvichemo zvavo zvakatosvitswa kuboka rePublic Service Commission , iro riri kutarisirwa kuzvisvitsawo kudare remakurukota .
Zvichakadaro , masangano evarairidzi anoti PTUZ neARTUZ , ari kurambawo zvakare kutambira zvikamu makumi manomwe nezvitanhatu zvakaiswa patafura nehurumende svondo rapera yekuwedzera vashandi vayo mihoro .
Sangano reAPEX Council riri kutarisirwa kusangana nevamiriri vehurumende neChipiri kuti vaedze kupeta nhaurirano dzemihoro yevashandi vehurumende .
Madzima matanhatu anenge akazvitakura ari kufa pazuva muZimbabwe nekusamira zvakanaka kwakaita zvinhu munyaya dzezvehutano .
Mashoko aya akabuditswa nesangano reUnited Nations Population Fund yakabatana nemuzinda weSweden muZimbabwe uye sangano ravananyamukuta reConfederation of Midwives Zimbabwe .
Izvi zvinotevera kubatana nemusi weChina kweZimbabwe nedzimwe nyika mukucherechedza zuva ravananyamukuta kana kuti International Day of the Midwife paine kurudziro yekuti hurumende iite mushandira pamwe nemasangano akazvimirira oga kuti adzikise huwandu hwemadzimai anofa pakusununguka vana .
Sangano reInternational Confederation of Midwives rinoti huwandu uhu hunokwanisa kudzikiswa kusvika nezvikamu makumi mapfumbamwe kubva muzana kana nyaya dzezvehutano dzikagadziriswa .
Sangano reUnited Nations Population Fund kana kuti UNFPA rati vananyamukuta vakakosha zvikuru mukuita basa rekusunungutsa madzimai .
Sangano reNational Health Strategy rinoti muzvipatara zvehurumende , pane mabasa avana nyamukuta anosvika makumi masere kubva muzana anoda vanhu .
Vatiwo pane mabasa makumi matanhatu nemaviri evarairidzi vavananyamukuta .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzezvavananyamukuta muUNFPA amai Agnes Makoni vanoti zvakakosha kuti paitwe mushandirapamwe kugadzirisa nyaya dzehutano hwemadzimai akazvitakura .
Asi vati zvinhu zviri kuita zviri nani .
Vagari vekuMasvingo vanoti havasi kufara nedanho rakatorwa nekanzuru yavo rekutambisa mari dzavanobhadhara apo yakaenda kunoshambdza mabasa ayo kuZimbabbwe International Trade Fair kuBulawayo .
Vagari ava vanoti hazvina musoro kuti kanzuru iende kuZITF kundoshambdza basa rayo ikoko nekuti mari zhinji inobva kuvagari veMasvingo avo vasina kuendako .
Vagari ava vanoti hapana mari inowanikwa nekanzuru kubudikidza nekuzvishambadza kuZITF .
Kanzuru , iyo yakaenda kuZITF kwesvondo rose , inonzi yakabudisa mari yakawanda sezvo kwakaenda vashandi vakawanda pamwe nemakanzura eguta rose avo vari kugarako .
Vazhinji vanoti bhizimusi rekanzuru guru rinobva mukubhadhrwa kwemari dzemitero nevagari nekudaro hapana chainoda chakakura kuBulawayo uko vanoti vakaenda kunodya mari vari kuzororo .
Mugari weku Rhodene , Amai Eashter Nyambiya , vanoti kanzuru iri kutambisa mari kuenda kuBulawayo nekuti hakuna vagari vemuMasvingo vanoda kushambadzirwa basa kuti kanzuru iwane mari .
Kanzuru inonzi yakaendesa vashandi vanopfuura makumi maviri pamwe nemakanzura ose ari gumi kuBuluawayo , uko vanhu ava vanopihwa mari dzekubatsirikana dzinosvika chiuru chemadhora emaRTGS pamunhu mumwe chete , zvichireva kuti kanzuru yakabudisa mari inopfuura zviuru makumi matatu emadhora semari yekubatsirikana
Pamusoro pezvo , kanzuru inozobhadharira vanhu vayo vose mari dzekugara muhotera kwemazuva mashanu inopfuura zana remadhora pazuva roga roga , iyo inozopfuura zviuru makumi maviri zvemadhora , isati yabhadhra mari dzesitendi nekushambadza mu ZITF .
