Vamwe vagari vakaita saVa Hardlife VaMapingure vanoti mari yakashandiswa kuBulawayo yaigonawo kutenga mafuta emotokari dzemarara kwemwedzi mitanhatu .
Asi meya weguta reMasvingo , VaCollen Maboke , vaudza Studio7 parunhare kuti kundoshambadza mabasa avo ku Trade Fair kunobatsira kutsvaga vemabhizimusi vanogona kuzouya kuitira mabasa avo mudhorobha reMasvingo .
Asi vamwe vagari vakaita sa VaNkulumani Mulambo , vanoti Trade Fair haisiyo nzvimbo yekutsvaga vanoinvesita mudhorobha kanzuru ichishandisa mari yakawanda kuti izvi zviitike .
Vamwewo vanoti mari yakashandiswa kuZITF inogona kushandiswa kutenga mishonga yekuchenesa mvura kwemwedzi mitatu kuitira kuti vanhu vanwe mvura yakachena .
Mukuru wemabasa musangano reVagari , reMasvingo United Residents and Rate Payers Alliance ( MURRA ) VaAnoziva Muguti , vanoti uku kutambiswa kwemari inofanira kushandiswaa pazvinhu zvakakosha .
Vagari vanoti Kanzuru inofanira kushambadza mabasa ayo panoitwa showo ye Masvingo muna Nyamvhuvhu sezvo vagari vazhinji vachikwanisa kupinda mushowo iyi vachionawo zvavanoshambadza .
Mutongi wedare repamusoro , Justice Pisirai Kwenda , vati pane zvakavanzika panyaya yechibvumirano cheDrax - SAGL nekambani yehurumende yeNatPharm vachiti zvinoshamisa kuti hurumende iri kunyanyobatikana nenyaya yekuti muzvinabhizimisi amutsa mutauro munyika , VaDelish Nguwaya , vakanyepera hurumende kuti isaine chibvumirano ichi asi isingashushikane
kuti chibvumirano ichi chemamiriyoni makumi maviri emadhora ekuAmerica chakaitwa pasingatevedzwe mutemo wekutengwa kwezvinhu weProcurement Act uye pasina Procurement Regulatory Authority of Zimbabwe iyo inoona nezvekutengwa kwezvinhu muhurumende nekambani ayo .
Justice Kwenda vataura mashoko aya mudare apo vange vari kuongorora nyaya yekuti dare raMagistrate rakapa mutongo kwawo here apo rakanyima VaNguwaya mukana wekubvisa mari yechibatiso kuti vatongwe vachibva kumba panyaya dzavari kupomerwa .
VaNguwaya , avo vanomirira muZimbabwe kambani yekuSwitzerland yeDrax , vane nyaya mbiri dzekuti vakanyepera hurumende kuti kambani yavo yaigadzira mishonga izvo zvakaita kuti hurumende ipinde muzvibvimirano zviviri , zve $ 21 million ne $ 40 million emadhora ekuAmerica zvekuti Natpharm itenge mishonga kubva kuDrax .
Vachuchusi panyaya iyi vanoti dai VaNguwaya vasina kunyepa hurumende ingadai isina kupinda muzvibvumirano izvi sezvo yaida kushanda nekambani inogadzira mishonga kwete inotenga nekutengesa mishonga zvinotwa neDrax .
Vatiwo VaNguwaya , avo vanomira kambani yePapPharma yekuAlbania , vakambotsvaga basa kurumende rekutengesa mishonga vakatadza kuriwana sezvo kambani iyi yainge isingagadzire mishonga .
Vati mushure mekuziva kuti hurumende yaida kushanda nekambani inogadzira mishonga , ndipo pavakadzoka zvekare neDrax ndokunyepa kuti kambani iyi inogadzira mishonga izvo zvakaita kuti vapihwe basa .
Asi Justice Kwenda vati chinoshamisa ndechekuti sei basa iri rinokosha mari yakawanda kudai rakaitwa pasina kutevedzwa mutemo weProcurement Act nebumbiro remutemo wenyika .
Vati zviri pachena kuti zvisinei nekuti VaNguwaya vakanyepa zviri pachena kuti mutemo wekutenga hauna kutevedzwa uye ndiyo nyaya yakakosha apa .
Vati zviri pachena kuti pane zviri kuvanzwa nehurumende panyaya iyi .
Vachuchusi vaudza dare kuti zvekuti izvi zvakaitwa pasina kutevedzwa mutemo ndizvo zvakaita kuti gurukota rezvehutano , Dr Obadiah Moyo , pamwe nevamwe vakuru vakuru vatatu vekambani yeNatPharm vanoti Amai Nancy Sifeku , VaCharles Mwaramba naVaRolland Mlalazi , vasungwe nenyaya iyi .
Rimwe remwagweta aVaNguwaya , VaTafadzwa Hungwe , vaudza dare kuti nyaya yekuti mutemo wekutenga zvinhu hauna kutevedzwa handizvo zvingavanyimise mukana wekubhadhara mari yechibatiso vachiti haraive basa ravo kuita izvi .
Vati samuzvinabhimisi chavo kutsvaga basa uye havashandi muhurumende zvekuti vangazive kuti chinofanira kuitwa chii pakutenga zvinhu .
Rimwe gweta ravo , VaAshely Mugiya , vati hapana chingaite kuti VaNguwaya vatize munyika kuti vasatongwa nekuti hapana mhosva yavakapara .
Asi mumwe wevachuchusi panyaya iyi , VaLancelot Mutsokoti , vaudza dare kuti kana vakabatwa nemhosva VaNguwaya vanogona kukandwa mujeri kwenguva yakareba nekudaro pane mukana mukuru wekuti vanogona kutiza munyika .
Vatiwo vavari kupomerwa mhosva navo vakaita saLlir Deja ari kunze kwenyika uye vanogona kuchengeta VaNguwaya kunze kwenyika sezvo vakatobhadharwa mamiriyoni maviri emadhora ekuAmerica nehurumende .
Asi magweta avo anoti vakazvipira kuti vabatise gwaro ravo rekufambisa kunamabharani wedare .
Justice Kwenda vati vanoda nguva yekumbozeya nyaya iyi vasati vapa mutongo wavo uye vati vachaita izvi musi weChitatu chinouya usati wadarika .
Nyaya yaVaNguwaya yakaputika nguva pfupi yapfuura mushure nekunge sangano remapurisa pasirose reInterpol ranyorera kuZimbabwe Republic Police richida kuziva hukama weDrax neNatPharm .
Huori uhu pakati peDrax neNatpham pamwe nebazi rehutano hwakatanga kuburitswa nebepanhau repaindaneti , reZim Morning Post .
Nyaya yaVaNguwaya yamutsa mutauro mukuru munyika sezvo vachifambidzana nevana vemutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , Collins naShaun uye vachionekwa pamadandemutande vaina VaMnangagwa pamwe nemudzimai wavo , Amai Auxillia .
VaMoyo vari kutongwa vachibva kumba kwavo mushure mekubhadhara zviuru makumi mashanu zvemadhora semari yechibatiso .
Amai Sifeku , VaMlalazi naVaMwaramba vari kutongwawo vachibva kunze mushure mekubhadhara mari yechibatiso zviuru gumi zvamdhora pamunhu .
Hurumende iri kuenderera mberi ichiratidza kusarongeka kwemhando yepamusoro apo vanhu vakabva kuZambia vachipinda munyika , vakagariswa panzvimbo isina kukodzera panguva iyo vanenge vachiongororwa chirwere cheCovid - 19 sezvinokurudzirwa nesangano reWorld Health Organization .
Nzvimbo inosvikira vanhu iyi haina kumira zvakanaka sezvo ichiisa hupenyu hwevanhu padanho rakaomarara .
Pari zvino paVhuti pane vanhu gumi vakachengetedzwa zvichitevera kupinda munyika kwavakaita vachibva kuZambia .
Dzimba dzinogara vanhu hadzina magonhi , hapana magumbeze , hapanawo mvura yakachenam magetsi , chikafu nezvimwe zvakakosha kuitira kuti munhu ararame zvakanaka , uye kuti asabatwe nechirwere .
Chikoro cheVhuti chinonzi chaifanirwa kunge chakagadziriswa nekuvakiridzwa nebazi rezvekuvakwa kwezvinhu , vanhu vasati vagariswa panzvimbo iyi , asi izvi hazvina kuitika .
Kusamira zvakanaka kwezvinhu pachikoro ichi kwakabudawo pamusangano wakaitwa neChina pakati pegurukota redunhu reMashonaland West , Amai Mliswa - Chikoka , namasachigaro emakomiti ari kuona nezvekupararira kwechirwere cheCovid - 19 .
Mukuru wezvehutano mudunhu reMashonaland , West Dr Wensilus Nyamayaro , vakati pari kuchengeterwa vanhu ava hapana mvura , magetsi , zvekudya uye pamwe nemagonhi mudzimba dzavari kugara .
Dr Nyamayaro vakati pagere vanhu ava hapanawo hutsanana zvekuti mararamiro avari kuita anotyora kodzero dzavo zvakanyanya .
Mukuru webazi reSocial Welfare muMashonaland West , Amai Agnes Mutowo , vakati vanovaka zvivakwa zvehurumende vakaudzwa kuti vagadzirise nzvimbo iyi asi hapana zvavati vaita kusvika pari zvino .
Asi mukuru wePublic Works mudunhu iri , VaTrymore Mutizwa , vakatiwo havasati vatengerwa zvinodiwa kuti vagadzirise midhuri iri kugara vanhu ava pachikoro cheVhuti .
Vachitaurawo pamusangano wanezuro Amai Mliswa - Chikoka vakati havasati vawana rubatsiro kubva kuhurumende kuburikidza nekomiti yeNational Taskforce , kunyange komiti iyi yakavaudza kuti vanyore zvose zvavari kuda mudunhu ravo .
Kusarongeka kwehurumende kuri kubudawo munzvimbo dzakawanda dzakachengeterwa vanhu vakamirira kuongororwa Covid - 19 vasati vabvumidzwa kuenda kudzimba dzavo sezvinodiwa nesangano reWorld Health Organization sedanho guru rekudzivirira kupararira kwechirwere ichi .
Zimbabwe ine nzvimbo nomwe dzakachengeterwa vanhu vakabva kune dzimwe nyika vari kuongororwa Covid - 19 vasati vabvumidzwa kuenda kumisha yavo .
Mune imwewo nyaya , kanzuru yeChinhoyi yatanga kupaza zvivakwa zvanga zvichitengeserwa zvinhu nevanhu sezvavakataurirwa nehurumende .
Mutauriri wekanzuru , VaTichaona Mlauzi , vati vanhu pachavo ndivo vari kupaza zvivakwa zvavo sezvo vakavaonesa kuti vakaita zviri kunze kwemutemo .
Asi vanomirira vagarii muChinhoyi , VaKliford Khlupeko , vati havasi kufara kuti vanhu vari kumanikidzwa kupaza zvivakwa zvavo zvavanga vachitengesera kuitira kuti vararame sezvo vanhu vakawanda vasina mabasa munyika .
Hurumende yakazivisa makanzuru ose munyika kuti achenese maguta munguva ino yekuvharwa kwenyika .
Kunyange hazvo mutauriri wemutungamiri weMDC Alliance VaNelson Chamisa , Doctor Nkululeko sibanda vakanga vapika kuti mubatanidzwa wavo uchaenderera mberi nemusangano wekutenda vanhu kuKwekwe , bato iri harina kuzoita musangano uyu mushure mekunge warambidzwa nemapurisa .
Mapurisa akarambidza musangano uyu achiti paityirwa kuti vanhu vakaungana vaizogona kuparadzira chirwere chemanyoka che Typhoid , icho chinonzi chiri kufungidzirwa kuti chiri mudunhu iri .
Vanofungidzirwa kuti vasori , mapurisa ange asina kupfeka nhumbi dzavo dzebasa pamwe nemasoja vaonekwa vachitendereratenderera panzvimbo yange ichifanirwa kuitirwa musangano nemubatanidzwa uyu kubvira panguva dzemangwanani , vamwe vevatsigiri vebato iri vachiti havasi kufara nekurambidzwa kwemusangano uyu nemapurisa .
Pasvika Studio 7 panzvimbo yeMbizo 4 Shopping Centre panguva dzekuma 10 mangwanai veruzhinji vange vachiita mabasa avo semazuva ose .
Asi pane motokari yemasoja yange yakamiswa mukati me durawall yechimwe chitoro uye masoja vasori pamwe nampurisa ange asina nhumbi dzebasa vane chitsama vange vachitenderera panzvimbo iyi .
Mutungamiri weMDC Alliance VaNelson Chamisa vange vachifanirwa kutaura pamusangano uyu uyo wange uchifanirwa kuve musangano wavo wekutanga mushure mekugadzwa kwaVaEmmerson Mnangagwa semutungamiri wenyika .
Asi nemusi weChina mapurisa akati musangano uyu waisafanirwa kuenderera mberi nekuda kwekuti paityirwa kuti kuungana kwevanhu kwaizobatsira kuwedzera kupararira kwechirwere cheTyphoid .
VaAmos Chibaya , murongi wemisangano mumubatanidzwa weMDC Alliance , avo vambosvika panzvimbo yange ichifanirwa kuitirwa musangano uyu , vati vaita izvi kuti vaone kuti vatsigiri vavo vatevedzera kurudziro yemapurisa yekuti vanhu vasaungane .
VaChibaya vati nemusi weChishanu bato ravo rakakwidza chikumbiro chechimbi - chimbi kudare reHigh Court chekuti musangano wavo uyenderere mberi asi dare rakati raizonzwa chikumbiro ichi mangwana Muvhuro .
Vamwe vatsigiri vebato reMDC Alliance vataura neStudio 7 vati vatsamwisa zvikuru nekurambidzwa kwakaitwa nemapurisa musangano uyu vachitiwo havazi kufara nekwavati kuve pachena kwekupindira kwevechiuto kuri kuramba kuchiitika mune zvematongero enyika .
Mumwe wevanhu ava ndiVaTawanda Mukurazita , avo vati vange vakatarisira kuona VaChamisa kuti vanzwe kuti vanoti chii neramangwana rebato nenyika .
Mumwewo mutsigiri , uyo angozvidoma nezita rekuti Tanyaradzwa , ati kunyange hazvo ange akanzwa nezvekurambidzwa kwemusangano uyu , nekuda kwechidokwa - dokwa chekuda kunzwa kubva kumutungamiri webato rake ange auya achifunga kuti pamwe musangano uyu waizoenderera mberi .
VaJeremiah Nyika vanove sachigaro weWard 5 muMbizo vati vatsigiri vakawanda vebato reMDC vachiri kurwadziwa nemabatirwo akaitwa nyaya yesarudzo nedare re Constitutional Court , vakati zvakakosha kuti hurumende isarambe ichivashungurudza nekurambidza kuti bato ravo risaite misangano .
VaChibaya vati kana dare rikati musangano wange uchifanirwa kuitwa nhasi uenderere mberi vachaona kuti vouita riinhi sezvo bato ravo rakaronga kuita mimwe misangano munzvimbo dzakasiyana - siyana munyika mumazuva ari kutevera .
Mamwe madzimai akazvitakura anoti ari kumanikidzwa kubatsirwa naana nyamukuta sezvo asina mari dzinodiwa kuti atange abhadhara kumakiriniki .
Madzimai akawanda anogara mumakomboni emapurazi ari pedyo neTynwald North , anoti kana achinge aita pamuviri , ari kubatsirwa naana nyamukuta pakusununguka sezvo asina mari dzinodiwa kumakiriniki ari pedyo .
Mumwe wemadzimai aya , Amai Nyarai Mugava , vanoti makiriniki ave kuvadhurira uye mari yeamburenzi yakakwira zvakare zvokuti vazhinji vavo vanopedzisira vabatsirwa vari kudzimba dzavo .
Amai Mugava vanoti vakasunungukira mwana wavo pamusika wemuTynwald North , uko vakabatsirwa nemamwe madzimai emunharaunda mwedzi miviri yapfuura .
Asi vanoti vakazovaendesa kukiriniki yekuDziresekwa kuti vanonyoresa gwaro rokuti vazokwanisa kupiwa gwaro rekuberekwa kwemwana wavo .
Gogo Tenesi Mauzhenti , avo vanogara papurazi riri pedyo nekuDzivaresekwa Extension , vanotiwo kunyange hazvo hurumende iri kukurudzira kuti madzimai abatsirwe kumakiriniki , madzimai mazhinji , vanhu vanotambura vasingakwanise kubhadhara mari dzinenge dzichidiwa .
Mbuya Elizabeth Zisengwe , avo vanogara kuCaledonia Farm , vanoti vari kusunungutsa madzimai akawanda anenge asina mari yokbhadhara kumakiriniki .
Mbuya Zisengwe vanoti vanosangana nemadzimai akawanda anongoerekana ave kurwadziwa nenhumbu zvokuti vanotozoshandisa mapepa echingwa chaiwo nokuti vanenge vasina kutakura zvishandiso zvekusunungutsa vakazvitakura .
Mutevedzeri wemukuru noona nezvezvirwere zvisingatapuriranwe mubazi rehutano , Dr Justice Mudavanhu , vanoti zvakakosha kuti vana nyamukuta vanyorese zviri pamutemo , kuitira kuti vashande basa ravo zvakanaka , pamwe nekupihwawo zvidzidzo nebazi rezvehutano .
Dr Mudavanhu vanoti ichokwadi kuti vanhu vakawanda havachakwanisi kubhadhara mari kumakiriniki nekuzvipatara zvisiri zvehurumende nepamusana pekuoma kwaita zvinhu munyaya dzehupfumi .
Kanzuru yeHarare yakakwidza mibhadharo yokurapwa kumakiriki ayo zvokuti vana amai vakazvitakura vanofanira kubhadhara mari yekunyoresa inoita zana nemakumi maviri emadhora emunyika , inova mari yakawanda kumadzimai akawanda anotambura .
Mumiriri wekomiti yehutano muparamende , Dr Ruth Labode , vanoti mamiriro ezvehupfumi hwenyika ari kuvhiringidza zvinhu zvakawanda , kusanganisirawo madzimai anenge akazvitakura .
Sangano reWorld Health Organisation rinoti madzimai anodarika zviuru zvitatu vanofa pagore munyika nokuti vazhinji vavo havaende kunoongororwa hutano hwavo kana vakazvitakura .
Mumiriri weAmerica muZimbabwe , Ambassador Brian Nichols , vanoti nyika yavo iri kuedza nepaigona napo kubatsira Zimbabwe munyaya dzehutano .
Vachitaura nevatori venhau veStudio7 muWashington neChishanu , Ambassador Nichols vakati vakashanyira bazi rinoona nezvezvirwere muAmerica , re Centers for Disease Control , CDC , mu Atlanta , vachiedza kuona kuti Zimbabwe ingabatsirwa seyi mudambudziko rekorera .
VaNichols vakati vakawana mukana wekutaura nenyanzvi dzehutano idzo dziri kushanda zvakanaka neZimbabwe munyaya dzehutano .
"""" Tine hukama hwakanaka chose neZimbabwe munyaya dzehutano uye ndakanzwa kufara nemushandira pamwe uri kuitwa nehurumende yeZimbabwe neCenters for Disease Control , """" Ambassador Nichols vakaudza Studio7 .
Vakati chirwere chekorera chirwere chinodzivirirwa , vachiti chinhu chakakosha ndechekuti vanhu vawane mvura yakachena .
"""" Tinoda chaizvo kushanda nevanhu vemuZimbabwe mukusumidzira kuwanikwa kwemvura yakachena , """" vakadaro VaNichols .
Vakati pane mushonga wekunwa unogona kudzivirira korera .
Asi vakati kunyange hazvo usina simba rakanyanisa , mushonga uyu unobatsira zvikuru kudzivirira korera .
"""" Munhu anogona kupora nekuchimbidza kana aching abatwa nechirwere ichi , uye tiri kushanda nehurumende yeZimbabwe mukuwanira vanhu mushonga uyu .
Tinovimba kuti vanhu vanodarika mazana matatu ezviuru vachawana mushonga , """" vakadaro .
Kunze kwenyaya dzehutano , Ambassador Nichols vakatora mukana wekutsanangura zvinoreva zvisungo zvakatemerwa vamwe vanhu muhurumende pamwe nemakambani anodyidzana nevakuru .
Vakati Zimbabwe ine mukana wekuti zvirangano izvi zvibviswe , ndokana ichinge zadzisa zvinodiwa nebumbiro rayo remitemo iro rakatambirwa muna 2013 .
Vakati pane mitemo yakaita sePublic Order and Security Act nemimwe inodzvanyirira kodzero dzevanhu .
Ambassador Nichols vakati Zimbabwe inofanirwa kuremekedza kodzero dzevanhu pamwe nemitemo yayo kuitira kuti zvirango zvibviswe .
Vakati America inoda kuona zvinhu zvichivandudzwa kwete vimbiso chete .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa divi rehurumende kuburikidza nebazi rezvekudyidzana nedzimwe nyika muZimbabwe .
Asi mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , vanogara vakataura kuti hurumende yavo yakazvipira kugadzirisa hukama hwayo nedzimwe nyika .
Hurumende , nevemasangano ekunze kusanganisa United Nations , iri kusimbaradza zvirongwa zvehutano kuti zvirwere zvakaita semalaria necholera zvisapararire kuChimanimani neChipinge kwakawirwa nedambudziko recyclone Idai .
Cyclone Idai yakauraya vanhu , kuparadza dzimba uye kupwanya zvinhu zvakaita semadhamu , zvibhorani nezvimwe .
KuMozambique kune vanhu vakatobatwa nechirewre checholera mushure medutumupengo iri .
Hurumende ichishanda neWorld Health Organisation kana kuti WHO iri kupa vanhu mushonga wekunwa kudziviira cholera uye inoti ichaparura chimwe chirongwa chechipiri kubatsira vanhu kudzivirira cholera .
Dr Maxwell Rupfutse vanoshanda neWHO vari kukurudzira vanhu kuti vatambire mushonga wavari kupihwa kuti vasatapurirwe chirwere checholera .
Vanhu vanosvika zviuru mazana mashanu vari kutarisirwa kupihwa mushonga uyu kuManicaland .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzekurwisana nehuwori inoti mashoko akataurwa nevakafanobata chigaro chemutauriri weZanu PF , VaPatrick Chinamasa , ekuti kufumura mazita evemabhizimusi vemunyika vakabudirira vanenge vachinzi vari kuita zvehuwori kunokanganisa kukura kwehupfumi hwenyika , anopa mufananidzo wekuti Zimbabwe inotambira huwori .
Vanoona nezvemabasa musangano reAnti - Corruption Trust of Southern Africa , VaMunyaradzi Alouis Chaumba vanoti mashoko akadaro haafanirwe kunge achibva kumunhu mukuru akaita saVaChinamasa , avo vanofanirwa kunge vari ivo vari pamberi mukurwisana nehuwori mubato ravo reZanu PF pamwe nemuhurumende umo vakambove gurukota pamwe nemunyika yose .
VaChinamasa vakaudza bepanhau reHerald kuti kufumura mazita evanenge vachipomerwa kuita zvehuwori kunoita kuti vemabhizimusi vanenge vafumurwa vatize munyika vachienda muhupoteri izvo zvisingazobatsire kukura kwehupfumi , uhwo hunofanirwa kukudzwa nevemabhizimusi vemunyika .
Vanonzi vakatiwo zvakare izvi zvinogona kuitawo zvakare kuti vekunze vanenge vachida kuzodyara mari dzavo munyika vatye kupinda munyika .
Studio 7 yakundikana kubata VaChinamasa kuti tizvinzwire tega pamusoro pemashoko avo aya .
Hurumende yeZimbabwe yakawana mari inosvika mamiriyoni mazana mashanu nemaviri kubva kuhomwe yeGlobal Fund yekubatsira kurwisa zvirwere zvitatu zvinoti HIV / Aids , Tuberculosis neMalaria .
Hurumende inoti mari iyi ichabatsira zvikuru mukurwisa zvirwere izvi nekusimudzira hutano .
Gurukota rezveutano , Doctor David Parirenyatwa vakati kubva muna 2002 zvatanga Zimbabwe kuwana mari kubva kuGlobal Fund , yashandisa mari inosvika bhiriyoni imwechete .
Doctor Parirenyatwa vakati mari yakawanikwa neZimbabwe ichasimbisa zvikuru kurwiswa kwezvirwere zvitatu izvi .
Asiwo Doctor Parirenyatwa vakati kunyangwe zvazvo vari kuwana mari kumasangano akazvimiririra , shuviro yavo ndeyekuti hurumende ikwanise kupa bazi rezveutano mari yakawanda kuti rikwanise kufambisa mabasa .
Mukuru wekomiti yeParamende inoona nezveutano Doctor Ruth Labode vakati mari yakapiwa kubazi rezveutano mubhajeti ishoma zvakanyanya nekudaro vanotarisira kuti mari iyi icharerutsa mukufambiswa kwemabasa , zvikuru mukupedza HIV / AIDS , Malaria neTB .
Dr Labode vakaudzawo Studio 7 kuti vane chivimbo chekuti mari iyi ichashandiswa sezvinotarisirwa nesangano reGlobal Fund sezvo mari iyi ine mitemo inoita kuti isashandiswe nenzira dzisidzo .
Pamari yakapiwa Zimbabwe iyi , madhora mamiriyoni mazana mana nemakumi maviri ane nhanhatu emari iyi achashandiswa mukuderedza HIV / AIDS .
Mukuru weGlobal Fund muZimbabwe VaMark Eddington vakatiwo sangano ravo rakazvipira kushanda pamwechete neZimbabwe munyaya dzekusimudzira hutano .
Sangano reCancer Association Of Zimbabwe riri kukurudzira veruzhinji kuti vaende kunoongororwa kuti vane chirwere chegomarara here kana kuti kwete sezvo chirwere ichi chikaera chakomba zvinonetsa kuchirapa .
Mashoko aya ari kuuya apo sangano iri riri kuita gadziriro yekucherechedza zuva regomarara inoitwa musi wa 4 Kukadzi gore rega rega .
Mutungamiri wesangano iri amai Juniour Mavhu vaudza Studio7 kuti sangano ravo richabatana nebazi rezvehutano muchirongwa chekucheredza zuva iri chichaitirwa kwaMutare svondo rinouya .
"""" Tinokukurudzirai kuti veruzhinji vaende kunowongorwa magomarara akasiyana siyina kamwe pagore kuitira kuti kana vakabatwa vanawo vabva vawana rubatsiro nechimbi chimbi , """" amai Mavhu vakaudza Studio7 .
Bazr reUnited Nations rinoona nezvehutano reWhorld Health Organization kana kuti WHO rinoti ongororo yakaitwa mugore ra 2012 inoratidza kuti chirwere chegomarara chakauraya vanhu vanodarika mamiriyoni masere kana kuti 8 . 2 million pasi rose .
Dingidira remabiko egore rino rinoti , """" Not Beyond Us . """"
Vechidiki vebato reZanu PF muHarare vari kugadzira mishonga inouraya hutachiwana kana kuti sanitizers , pamwe nezvekuvharisa miromo , kana kuti masks , mukubatsira kwavo hurumende mukudzivirira kupararira kwehutachiwana hunokonzeresa COVID - 19 .
Mukuru anoona nezvekuburitswa kwemashoko muZanu PF , VaTafadzwa Mugwadi , vanoti chirongwa ichi chakabudirira kuburikidza nemari yakawanikwa nevechidiki ava kubva kuEmpower Bank .
VaMugwadi vanoti zvinhu izvi zvichapiwa kune mwana weZimbabwe wese zvisineyi nekuti ndewebato rezvematongerwo enyika ripi .
VaMugwadi vanoti vechidiki vebato ravo ava vakasimudzirwa zvikuru nezviri kuitwa nebato rinopikisa muSouth Africa , reEFF , iro riri kuitawo zvimwechetezvo .
Vanoti sebato reveruzhinji , rinokoshesa veruzhinji , zvisineyi nekuti munhu ndewebato ripi .
"""" Hazvisi zvinhu zvingakatyamadza zvekuti vechidiki veZanu PF vari kuita basa iri nekuti musangano weZanu PF kuburikidza kunyanyanyanya neChitepo School of Ideology vanodzidziswa yatinoti patriotism , kuda nyika yako zvisineyi kuti iri mumatambudziko , munhu unongofanirwa kuda nyika yako .
"""" Ndosaka tiri ku supporter donzvo ratorwa nevechidiki tichiti iro richabatsira hurumende , richabatsira vana veZimbabwe , richabatsira zvakare zvakare munhu wese ari muZimbabwe nenhau yekuti ma sanitizer mazhinji tanga tichiawana kubva kune dzimwe nyika , """" VaMugwadi vanodaro .
Zvichakadaro , vechidiki vebato guru rinopikisa reMDC inotungamirirwa naVaNelson Chamisa , vanotiwo vari kuita zvakasiyanasiyana mukubatsira kushambadza nezvedzidziso pamusoro pechirwere che Coronavirus .
Munyori muboka revechidiki mudunhu reHarare , uye vari kanzura vewadhi 16 , VaDenford Ngadziore vanoti vechidiki vavo vari kushandawo nevezvitoro , vemakereke pamwe nemamwe mapoka mukuona kuti vanhu vari kutevera here kurudziro yekuti vavhare miromo yavo uye kugeza maoko .
Vanotiwo vari kukurudzira veruzhinji kuti vasaswederane munguva dzavanopinda mizvotoro kana kunge vari munzvimbo dzinoungana vanhu .
Bazi rezvehutano rakazivisa nemusi weChina kuti huwandu hwevanhu vabatwa neCovid - 19 munyika hwakanga hwakwira kusvika pazviuru zviviri nezana rine makumi maviri nevana kana kuti 2 124 , zvichitevera kuwanikwa kwevamwe vanhu makumi mapfumbamwe kana kuti 90 vaine chirwere ichi .
Vanhu zviuru zviviri nemazana manomwe ane makumi manomwe nevatatu kana kuti 2 773 ndivo vakavhenekwa nyika yose nemusi weChina .
Vanhu vakanga vapora vakanga vave mazana mashanu ane gumi kana kuti 510 , uye huwandu hwevanhu vashaya hwakakwirawo kusvika pamakumi maviri nevasere kana kuti 28 zvichitevera kushaya kwevamwe vaviri .
Pavanhu vakawanikwa vaine chirwere ichi , vanomwe kana kuti 7 vakabva kuSouth Africa kuchitiwo makumi masere nevatatu kana kuti 83 vari vanhu vagara vari munyika .
Kukwira kwehuwandu hwevanhu vari kuwanikwa vaine chirwere vari vanhu vagara vari munyika kunonzi nedzimwe nyanzvi mune zvehutano kunofanirwa kuongororwa zvakadzama nekuti vanhu ava vanogona kunge vakatosangana nevanhu vakawanda kwazvo vasati vaziva kuti vane chirwere ichi .
Imwe nyanzvi mune zvehutano vachidzidzisa zvehutano paNottingham Trent University kuBritain , Doctor Mathew Nyashanu , vari kukurudzirawo veruzhinji kuti vasimbe kutevera mitemo yekudzivirira kupararira kwechirwere cheCovid - 19 yakatarwa nebazi rezvehiutano pamwe nemitemo yeWorld Health Organisation , W - H - O .
Mimwe yemitemo iyi inosanganisira kusabatana maoko , kusiya mikaha pakati pevanhu , kugeza maoko nesipo , kusaungaana pamwe nekuvhara miromo nemhino nemamasiki .
Johns Hopkins University yekuAmerica , iyo iri kutevera kupararira kwechirwere ichi inoti pasi rose vanhu vabatwa nechirwere ichi vadarika mamiriyoni gumi namashanu nezviuru mazana mashanu kana kuti 15.5 million , kuchitiwo vafa vadarika zviuru mazana matanhatu nemakumi matatu ane zvina kana kuti 634 000 .
America , iyo iri pamusoro pasi rose , yave nevanhu vanodarika mamiriyoni mana kana kuti 4 million vabatwa nechirwere ichi uye vanhu vafa vadarikawo zviuru zana nemakumi mana nezvina kana kuti 144 000 .
Doctor Nyashanu , vanoti kuti dambudziko rekukwira kwehuwandu hwevanhu vave kuwanikwa vaine chirwere ichi munyika rideredzwe , hurumende inofanirwa kusimbisa zvakare nyaya yekuteverwa kwevanhu vakasangana nevanenge vawanikwa vaine chirwere , kana kuti contact tracing , uye kuti vanhu vagare kwavo voga , kana kuti self - isolation .
Magweta ari kumiririra mutevedzeri wasachigaro wemusangano weMDC , VaJob Sikhala , aisa chikumbiro chekuti mhosva yavari kupomerwa yekuda kupidigura hurumende nechisimba iraswe achiti VaSikhala havana mhosva yavakapara , apo kutongwa kwenyaya iyi kwatanga nhasi mudare repamusoro reHigh Court muMasvingo .
Amai Beatrice Mtetwa , avo vange vachitungamirira magweta aVaSikhala , vaisa chikumbiro ichi kune mutongi wedare VaGarainesu Mawadze , vachiti vachuchisi vakadoma mhosva isiriyo panyaya iyi yekuti vanoda kubvisa hurumende nechisimba ivo vakati vanoda kubvisa mutungamiriri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa gore ra2023 risati rasvika .
Mai Mtetwa vati mhosva iyi haisiriyo nekuti kubvisa VaMnangagwa pachigaro hakusi kubvisa hurumende , sezvo VaMnangagwa vari voga vasiri hurumende .
Munyori wezvemutemo muMDC uye vari gweta , VaInnocent Gonese , vati chikumbiro chaiswa chichapuwa mutongo nemutongi wedare musi wa 14 Kukadzi gore rino .

Nematambiro avakaita neSvondo , zviri kuratidza kuti kumberi kwavo kwakajeka .
Sangano reZimbabwe National Network of People Living with HIV , kana kuti ZNNP + , rinoti riri kushushikana zvikuru kuti nhengo dzaro dzakawanda hadzisati dzava kushandisa mushonga unonzi unodzikisa hukasha pamwe nekupararira kweHIV / AIDS mumuviri wemunhu anorarama neHIV / AIDS .
Mumwe mukuru mukuru musangano reZNNP + , VaClarence Mademutsa , vanoti mushonga mutsva weDolutegravir , kana kuti DTG , uyo wakaparurwa muZimbabwe gore rakapfuura , hausati wava kupihwa vanhu vakawanda vanorarama neHIV / AIDS munyika .
VaMademutsa vanoti vanhu vanorarama neHIV / Aids vakawanda vaifanirwa kunge vakatanga kunwa mushonga weDTG gore ra 2019 risati rapera .
VaMademutsa vanoti vanhu havafanirwi kuramba vakamirira mushonga weDTG , sezvo wakanakira kuvanhu vanorarama neHIV / AIDS .
VaMademutsa vanoti dzimwe nhengo dzesangano ravo dzanga dzichinetseka pakushandisa mushonga we Efavirenz , nokudaro chinhu chinenge chakanaka kuti vanhu vakawanda vashandise DTG sezvo mushonga uyu usina hukasha hunovhiringa hutano hwevanhu vanorarama neHIV / AIDS . .
VaMademutsa vanoti havasati vave neruzivo rwekuti vanhu vangani vanofanirwa kunge vachipihwa DTG .
Asi mumwe mudzimai asina kuda kudomwa nezita rake anoti vanhu havafanire kumanikidzwa kuti vapinde muchirongwa cheDTG , sezvo vamwe vanhu , vakaita saivo , vasina dambudziko nemishonga yavari kunwa pari zvino .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa kugurukota rezvehutano , Dr Obadiah Moyo , kuti zvii zvakanakira mushonga mutsva uyu , uye kuti seyi vanhu vakawanda vasati vava pahurongwa hweDTG sezviri kutaurwa naVaMademutsa .
Asi imwe nyanzvi munyaya dzezvirwere mubazi rezvehutano , Dr Clorata Gwanzura , vanoti mushonga weDTG mushonga mutsva unobatsira kudzikisa hukasha hweHIV .
Dr Gwanzura vanoti bazi rehutano rinogara richiita ongororo dzekuona kuti ndeupi mushonga ungave nani pakubatsira vanorarama neHIV / AIDS .
Dr Gwanzura vanoti ongororo yakaitwa inoratidza kuti DTG inobatsira zvikuru mukudzikisa hukasha hweHIV munguva pfupi mushure mekunge munhu atanga kunwa mushonga uyu .
Zimbabwe imwe yenyika shoma dzemuAfrica dzava kushandisa mushonga weDTG uyo wakatambirwa zviri pamutemo muAmerica mugore ra 2013 , mushure mokunge nyanzvi dzehutano dzaona kuti mushonga uyu waibatsira zvikuru kudzikisa hukasha hweHIV / Aids .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzechikafu chinovaka muviri dzinoti dziri kufara nedanho rakatorwa nehurumende rekuti zvinhu zvekudya zvakaita sehupfu nemafuta zviwedzerwe chikafu chinovaka muviri senzira yekurwisa dambudziko rekushaikwa kwechikafu chinovaka muviri .
Zvichitevera dambudziko rekushaikwa kwechikafu chinovaka muviri muvanhu vakawanda , bazi rezveutano rakaisa chiga chekuti kutanga musi wa 1 Chikunguru gore rino , vanogadzira zvekudya zvakaita sehupfu , mafuta ekubikisa , shuga neflour , vachange vachisungirwa kuwedzera zvinovaka muviri muchikafu ichi .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzechikafu chinovaka muviri , Muzvare Ollin Rukweza Chimhau , vanoti danho iri rakanaka chose mukurwisa dambudziko rekushaikwa kwekudya kwakakwana .
Mumwe chiremba musangano reZimbabwe Association of Doctors for Human Rights , Dr Nicholas Wazadza , vanoti izvi zvichadzivirira zvirwere , kunyanya zvinobata vana vadiki nemadzimai .
Dr Wazadza vanoti chikafu chizhinji chiri kudyiwa munyika hachina kudya kunovaka muviri .
Kunyange hazvo vamwe vari kutyira kuti kuwedzerwa kwezvinovaka muviri uku kunogona kuzokanganisa hutano hwavo , Dr Wazadza vanoti vanhu havafanire kutyira hutano hwavo , sezvo zvose zviri kuitwa , zviri kuitwa nenzira dzakatambirwa nenyanzvi .
Mumwe mugari wemuHarare , VaAndrew Tsiga , vanoti nyaya yehurombo ndoinokonzera kuti mhuri zhinji dzinoshaya dziite dambudziko rekushaya kudya kwakakwana uku .
Mutemo wehurumende unoti ma Vitamin A achawedzerwa pamafuta neshuga kuitira kuti zvivake hutano hwakanaka hwevanhu .
Muhupfu neflour muchawedzerwa neFolate , Zinc , Vitamin B6 neB12 , iron nezvimwewo zvinobatsira mukuvaka hutano hwakanaka hwemuviri .
Gwaro reongororo yakaburitswa neZimbabwe Health Demographic Survey muna 2015 rinoti muZimbabwe pavana vari pasi pemakore mashanu , zvikamu zvevana ava makumi maviri nezvinomwe kubva muzana , havasi kuwana kudya kwakanaka , pamwe nekunovaka muviri yavo .

Vagari vemumusha weNyamhunga vakaita saMuzvare Cleopatra Rusere vanoti havana kumbosangana nedambudziko rakadai mumakore akawanda zvekuti vari kutoshamisika kuti chii chave kuitika .
Vanoti kunyangwe kanzuru iri kuvapa mvura nemabhauza haisikuvakwanira .
Muzvare Rusere vanoti zvinoshamisa kuti vari kushaya mvura ivo vari kumahombekombe kwayo .
Amai Mavis Makombe vanoti vave kumanikdzwa kunochera mvura isina kuchena kudhamu .
Mwana wechikoro uyo asingabvumirwe kuti tiburitse zita rake pamhepo anoti vana vechikoro vave kumanikidzwa kutakura mvura yekunwa muzvigubhu .
Meya weguta reKariba VaGeorge Masendu vanobvuma kuti guta ravo raita dambudziko remvura vachiti riri kukonzerwa nemvura yadzikira mudhamu .
Meya Masendu avo vanoti havasati vapihwa mari nehurumende iyo yakapihwa mamwe makanzura kuti vape vagari mvura yakachena nekutakurwa kwemabhini vanoti panofanirwa kuwedzera mapombi emvura sezvo vagari vawandisa kudarika nguva yakare .
Kushaikwa kwemvura kuKariba kunouya apo nyika yatarisana nekupisa kwezuva munzvimbo dzakawanda dzenyika vanhu vachikurudzirwa kuti vanwe mvura yakawanda kuti vasarasikirwe nehupenyu .
Mune imwewo nyaya , zvinonzi paita ropa rakaipa pakati penhengo dzeZanu PF mudunhu reMashonaland West zvichitevera kushoropodzwa kunonzi kwakaitwa mutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa nemwana weimwe nhengo yeZanu PF yekuHurungwe , VaRueben Marumahoko .
Mwana waVaMarumahoko , Simbarashe ari kupomerwa mhosva yekutuka VaMnangagwa achiti vari kuuraya bato reZanu PF nenyaya yehuori .
Hatina kukwanisa kubata Simbarashe kuti tinzwe divi rake .
Mutevedzeri wasachigaro webato iri mudunhu reMashonaland West , VaDexter Nduna vaudza Studio 7 kuti nyaya iyi yakazeyiwa pamusangano webato iri paChinhoyi Training Centre nemusi weSvondo asi hapana zvavakaita sezvo iri nyaya inofanirwa kunomhan'arwa kumapurisa .
VaNduna vanoti sasachigaro webazi rinoranga vose vanenge vakanganisa mudunhu vanozeya nyaya dzavanenge vasumwa zviri pamutemo .
Asi baba VaSimbarashe , VaMarumahoko vanoti havadi kubvunzwa nezvenyaya iyi .
Pamusangano uyu pakabuda nyaya yekuti VaMnangagwa vari kushoropodzwa zvikuru nenhengo dzebato ravo pamadandemutande asi pasina matanho akasimba ari kutorwa .
Mapurisa arambidza MDC inotungamirwa naVaNelson Chamisa kuparura hurongwa hwayo hwekutsvaira kuChitungwiza .
Mapurisa aya , ayo anga akatakura zvombo , afumira panzvimbo yemabhizimusi paUnit L muChitungwiza akatakura tsamba yanga ichirambidza MDC kuenderera mberi nehurongwa hwayo hwekuparura kutsvairwa kwenzvimbo dzakasiyana - siyana munyika kuitira kuti nyika igare yakachena .
Pasvika Studio 7 pamabhizimusi epa Unit L panga pasara mapurisa mashomanana anga achingotenderera uye vanhu vanga vauya kuzoona VaChamisa vachiparura chirongwa ichi vanga vadzokera mudzimba dzavo .
Mumwe wevanhu ava , Amai Viola Taderera , vaudza Studio7 kuti veruzhinji vanga vabuda chaizvo kuti vanotsvaira pamwe chete naVaChamisa , asi izvi zvatadziswa nemapurisa .
Mutevedzeri wemutauriri weMDC , VaLuke Tamborinyoka , vati zvaitwa nemapurisa izvi zvinoratidza kuti hurumende yaVaEmmerson Mnangagwa inotya veruzhinji nepamusana pekutadza kutungamira zvakanaka kwavanoti kuri kuitwa naVaMnangagwa .
VaTamborinyoka vaenderera mberi vachiti sebato iye zvino vatarirana mutsetse nehurumende yaVaMnangagwa zvichitevera kuramba vongorambidzwa nemapurisa kuenderera mberi nezvavanenge vakaronga .
Asi hurumende , kuburikidza negurukota rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , Amai Monica Mutsvangwa , vati VaChamisa vanofanirwa kuteerera zvinotaurwa nemapurisa , uye kana vari pachokwadi chekuda kuchenesa nzvimbo vanofanirwa kubatana nemutungamiri wenyika muchirongwa chake chekutsvaira munzvimbo dzinogara veruzhinji .
Tsamba yemapurisa yekurambidza hurongwa hwaVaChamisa hwanhasi iyo yanyorwa nemukuru wemapurisa munharaunda yeChitungwiza , Chief Superintendent S . Mujiwa , iyo iri mumaoko eStudio 7 , yakurudzira MDC kuti ibatane nemutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , pavanenge vachiita hurongwa hwavo hwekutsvaira uhwo hunoitwa kutanga
kwemwedzi wegawega .
Mutauriri wemapurisa , VaPaul Nyathi , vati tigovabata zvakare patavafonera asi pataenda pamhepo nharembozha yavo yanga isiri kudairwa .
Chikwata chema Warriors chatarisana nemukana mukuru wekubudirira kuenda kumafainari e 2020 Africa Nations Championships , Chan , apo chiri kutamba neLesotho nemusi weSvondo .
Chikwata ichi chine gumbo rimwechete mumafainari aya mushure mekurova Lesotho 3 - 1 muNational Sports Stadium asi vanoziva kuti kukundwa 2 - 0 muMaseru neSvondo , kunosvitsa rwendo rwavo kumagumo mumakwikwi aya .
Zimbabwe inofanira kukunda , kana kuita mangange , kana kurohwa zvayo 1 - 0 , kana 2 - 1 , kuitira kuti ikwanise kuenda kumafainari emakundano aya kuCameroon mushure mekutadza kuita izvi muna 2018 .
Pamitambo makumi maviri nemiviri yasangana zvikwata zviviri izvi kubva muna 1980 , Zimbabwe yakunda mumitambo gumi neminomwe , Lesotho ichikunda mumutambo mumwe chete , mimwe mitambo mina ichiita mangange .
Nhengo yeZimbabwe National Soccer Supporters Association , VaProsper Chimusoro , vanoti havasi kuona Lesotho ichikwanisa kurova maWarriors ikozvino mushure mekutadza kuita izvi kwemakore makumi matatu nemapfumbamwe .
Nhengo yerimwe sangano revatsigiri vemaWarriors , reWarriors Fan Club , VaMarcabee Makamure , vanoti Lesotho ichazvindikitwa zvokuti Zimbabwe ichakunda 3 - 1 sezvayakamboita mumutambo wekutanga .
Asi murairidzi wemaWarriors , Joey Antipas , anoti kunyange hazvo vakakunda mumutambo wekutanga , hakusisina zvikwata zvidiki munhabvu muAfrica zvekuti havasi kutarisira Lesotho iyi pasi mumutambo uyu .
Antipas atakura chikwata chake chakasimbisa chinosanganisira Prince Dube , uyo ari kukanda zvibodzwa pamadiro kuHighlanders , Joel Ngodzo na Phineas Bhamusi avo vari kupisa kuCaps United , Evans Katema we Dynamos , Wellington Takaendesa weBlack Rhinos , Edward Madzongwe weFC Platinum , pamwe na Ian Nekati uyo ari kuvhara zvibodzwa kuZPC Kariba .
Zvichakadaro , makundano eCastle Lager Premier Soccer League ari kuenderera mberi kunyange hazvo chikwata chenyika chichange chiri munhandare .
Asi mitambo yezvikwata zviri kutungamira makwikwi aya , Caps United neFC Platinum , yambomiswa kusvika neChitatu apo maWarriors anenge adzoka .
Asi hondo yezvikwata zviri kurwira kuramba zviri muPremier Soccer League iri kuenderera mberi , chikwata chiri pasi pasi mugungano iri Yadah , chiri pamusha neManica Diamonds .
MuGweru muchange musingadaidzwe anonzwa apo zvikwata zvemuguta iri , TelOne neChapungu , zviri kusangana muAscot Stadium neMugovera .
Asi mutambo mukuru muPremier League ndeuyo uri kuColliery apo Chipangano cheHwange chiri kusangana nemaSunshine City Boys eHarare City .
Murairidzi weHwange , Nation Dube , ari kuramba kuti chikwata chake chichange chiri muDivision One mwaka unouya achiti iye varipo svondo rino kunyaradza avo vari kuparidzirira mashoko akadai .

Misika yefodya yavhurwa muHarare mitengo yefodya iri pasi asi hurumende ichiti inotarisira kuti mitengo ichakwira nekufamba kwenguva .
Gurukota rinoona nezvekurima , VaPerence Shiri , ndivo vaparura mwaka wekutengesa fodya zviri pamutemo pamusika weTobacco Sales Floor muHarare , uye vati vafara nemutengo kunyange hazvo wange uri pasi .
VaShiri vati izvi ndizvo zvinogaroitika mwaka yese sezvo varimi vachitanga kuitengesa foya yemhando yepasi .
Bhero rekutanga ratengwa nemadhora mana eku America pakirogiramu kozotiwo bhero repasi ratengwa nemasendi makumi mapfumbabweeku America pakirogiramu rimwe chete .
VaShiri vaudza Studio7 kuti zvinofadza kuti misika yefodya yavhura kunyange hazvo paine dambudziko rechirwere cheCoronavirus .
Asi mutungamiri werimwe remasangano anomirira varimi vefodya munyika reTobacco Association of Zimbabwe , VaGeorge Seremwe , vaudza Studio7 kuti kunyange hazvo misika yavhurwa , havasi kufara nemitengo iripo .
VaShiri vatiwo kunyange hazvo paine dzimwe nyika dzakawanda dzinorima fodya pasi rese , Zimbabwe ine mbiri yekurima fodya yemhando yepamusoro uye inokwikwidzana neBrazil chete pasi rese .
VaShiri vati kurimwa kwefodya kuri kusimukira zvakanyanya munyika uye ishuviro yavo kuti dai vanorima zvimwe zvirimwa vadzidza kubva kuvarimi vefodya .
Vatiwo kunyange hazvo Coronavirus yakavhiringa hupfumi hwenyika dzinotenga fodya kubva kuZimbabwe dzakaita seChina , hazvisati zvave pachena kuti , izvi zvichakakanganisa kutengwa kwefodya yeZimbabwe here
VaShiri vatiwo vati hurumende inoda kuti varimi vatevedze marimirwo anoitwa kufodya pakurimwa zvimwe zvirimwa zvakaita sechibage , nembanje dzinioshandiswa kurapa dzakaita seHemp neCannabis .
Sachigaro vebhodi remakambani yehurumende inoona nezvekutengeswa kwefodya , yeTobacco Industries Marketing Board , TIMB , VaPat Devenish , vati misika yefodya ingadai yakavhurwa mwedzi wapfuura asi izvi zvakatadziswa nekuda kweCoronavirus .
Vatiwo mwaka uno zvinhu hazvisi kufambiswa semamazuva ose nekuda kwechirwere cheCovid - 19 uye mwaka uno varimi havasi kubvumidzwa kupinda mumisika uye vachange vaine vanhu vanovamiririra .
Mumisika mange muine vatengi chete nevanhu vashomanana uye vanhu vese vange vari pamusika vange vakapfeka maMask , vachigeza maoko nekuita zvese zvinofanirwa kuitwa pakudzivirira Coronavirus .
VaDevenish vazivisawo kuti huwandu hwevarimi vefodya hwakadzikira gore rino nezvikamu guni nezvinomwe kubva muzana .
Vatiwo varimi vachange vachibhadharwa mari yavo nezvikamu makumi mashanu kubva muzana ari madhora ekuAmerica , uye imwe yacho iri mari yemuno .
Nyaya yedare remakurukota yekuchinja mazita emigwagwa yakonzera mutauro wakanyanya vamwe vachiti mutemo wakatyorwa uye kupedza mguva kuzeya nyaya dzakadai mudarenyika yakatarisana nenzara .
Vamwe vanoti zviri pamutemo uye hapana chakaipa kuchinja mazita munyika .
Migwagwa inokwana misere mumadhorobha akasiyana siyana akapihwa zita remutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa kusanganisa Enterprise Road muHarare , Road , Sixth Avenue muBulawayo , A5 Road mu Kwekwe , Main Street mu Gweru , Chipinge Main Street , Etherton Road ku Bindura , Edgar Peacock Road kwa Mutare , Henry Hartley Road mu Chegutu uye Hughes Street kuMasvingo .
Ko zvekuchinja mazita izvi zviri pamutemo here ?
Muzvinafundo Lovemore Madhuku nyanzvi munyaya dzezvemitemo vachitungamirawo bato reNCA vanoti mutemo weNames Alteration Act Chapter 14 : 10 unopa hurumende simba rekuvandudza mazita emigwagwa .
Meya weguta reHarare vari nhengo yeMDC VaHerbert Gomba vati havana kunge vasumwa here nezvedanho iri uye vachatanga vanzwa kubva kumagweta avo kuti zvakaitwa zviri pamutemo here .
Vanachiremba navana mukoti munyika vatanga kuramwa mabasa kunyangwe nyika yatarisana nechirwere chouraya vanhu vakawanda pasi rose cheCoronavirus .
Vanachiremba navanamukoti ava vanoti hurumende iri kukundikana kuvapa zvekushandisa kuti vazvidzivire kutapurirwa zvirwere zvakaita seCoronavirus .
Mutsamba kubazi rezvehutano , iri mumaoko eStudio 7 , vanamukoti kuburikidza nesangano reZimbabwe Nurses Association vati vakasuma bazi rezvehutano mazuva maviri apfuura kut vanoda zvekuzvidzivirira kubva kuchirwere cheCoronavirus , mvura muzvipatara uye mari yekushanda kwavachaita nguva yakareba vachirapa vane chirwere cheCoronavirus .
Mutsamba kubazi rezvehutano nevakuru vezvipatara zvehurumende munyika , mutungamiri wesangano rinomirira vanachiremba reZimbabwe Hospital Doctors Association , Dr Tawanda Zvakada , vatiwo nhengo dzavo hadzichakwanise kuramba dzichishanda kutanga nhasi sezvo dzisina zvekuzvidzivirira .
Vati vakaita musangano nehurumende neMuvhuro nezvenyaya iyi asi kusvika pari zvino hapana chabuda .
Hatina kukwanisa kubata gurukota rezvehutano , Dr Obadiah Moyo , kana munyori mubazi ravo , Dr Agnes Mahomva , sezvo vose vange vasiri kudaira nharembozha dzavo .
Kusvika pari zvino hurumende inoti vanhu vatatu vabatwa nechirwere cheCoronavirus munyika uye mumwe chete , mutori wenhau , Zororo Makamba , akashaya vakavigwa neChipiri .
Mutungamiri weZimbabwe Nurses Association , VaEnock Dongo , vatenda kuti vanoda zvikwanisiro muzvipatara nechimbi chimbi uye vakanda mapadza pasi . .
Banga guru renyika , reReserve Bank of Zimbabwe , RBZ , raparura musika wekutenga nekutengesa mari yekunze kwenyika kana kuti foreign currency auction nechinangwa chekuyedza kumisa vanhu kuenda kunotenga mari pamukoto zvinonzi nehurumende zvapa kuti dhora remunyika rishaye simba .
Pakuparurwa kwemusika uyu , patengeswa mari inosvika mamiriyoni gumi nerimwe nezviuru mazana mana emadhora ekuAmerica kana kuti US $ 11 , 4 million .
Dhora rekuAmerica ratengwa nemari yemuZimbabwe inoita mabhora makumi mashanu nemamonwe nemasendi makumi matatu nematanhatu .
Asi hapana kuwirirana kuti danho iri richanyukuru nyika mukanwa mamupere .
Hurongwa hweRBZ uhu hunoreva kuti hakuchina zvainge zvoitwa nebhanga iri zvekutara mari inofanira kutengwa kana kutengeswa kwedhora rekuAmerica .
Gavhuna weRBZ , Doctor John Mangudya , vanoti munhu kana kambani inoda kutenga mari pamusika uyu inofanira kunge ichitangira pamadhora zviuru makumi mashanu zvekuAmerica kana kuti US $50 000 kusvika pazviuru mazana mashanu kana kuti US $500 000 .
Mari yepamusoro soro inenge yatengeswa nayo mari pamusika uyu ndiyo inenge yoshandiswa vhiki rose semari yekuchinja nayo madhora kana kuti exchange rate .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzezvemabhanga , VaGilbert Muponda , vanoti danho iri rakanaka uye rinoratidza kuti RBZ iri kuteerera zviri kutaurwa nevanhu zvekuti isatare mutengo wemari .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfum , i Muzvinafundo Gift Mugano , avo vanodzidzisa paDurban University of Technology , vanoti zviri kuitwa neRBZ hazvina zvakanyanya zvazvinobatsira uye zviri pachena kuti akaroya Zimbabwe akazunza negona rose nekuti matambudziko acho rufuse rusingapore .
Mashoko aya atsinhirwa nemutungamiri wesangano revashandirwi reEmployers Confederayion of Zimbawe kana kuti EMOCOZ , Dr Israel Murefu .
VaMurefu vanoti zvimwe zviri kuitwa naVaMangudya zvinonetsa kusadzikisa nekuti vari kutengesa zvinhu zvisipo .
Kunyange vachitenderana nemaonero aya , VaMuponda vanoti zvinhu zviyedzwa chembere yekwaChivi yakabika mabwe ikanwa muto .
VaMugano vanoti kuita musika uyu kunge svondo inopindwa kamwe pavhiki , kukanganisa zvikuru .
Kuti danho ratorwa neRBZ iri richamisa musika mutema ?
Vamwe vanoti uku kupedzera tsvimbo kumakunguwo idzo njiva dzichitevera .
Asi veRBZ vanoti vari kushora danho iri vari kuita shungu dzomutana waswera padare kuramba nemhandire seane meno .
Veruzhinji muZimbabwe havasi kufara nemabatirwo akaitwa chikwata chemaWarriors apo chaive mukamba chichigadzirira makwikwi e2017 Africa Cup of Nations .
Vakawanda vanoti mabatirwo akaitwa chikwata ichi anokwanisa kuvatadzisa kutamba zvakanaka kumakundano e 2017 Africa Cup of Nations ayo ari kutanga neMugovera .
Chekutanga , maWarriors akatanga achigariswa kuZifa Village uko vatambi vanoti vaisangana nemakonzo ayo aivatadzisa kurara .
Chechipiri , chikwata ichi chaiita gadziriro yacho munhandare yeGateway Primary School mushure mekunge veZifa vatadza kubhadhara mari yekuti vashandise National Sports Stadium .
Chechitatu , maWarriors ayo aifanira kuve akasimuka neMugovera akazosimuka nezuro mushure megakava nenyaya dzemari yavanofanira kupihwa mukukwikwidza kwavo mumakundano ezvikwata gumi nezvitanhatu aya .
Muongorori wemutambo wenhabvu , VaProsper Muzanharwo , vanoti vatambi vanofanira kupihwa mari kuti vatambe neshungu .
Muteveri wenhabvu , VaShingirai Kadiyo , vanoti havasi kufara nemabatirwo anga achiitwa maWarriors vachiti ivo izvi zvinokonzera kuti chikwata chikundwe mumitambo iyo chaifanira kukunda .
VaKadiyo vanoti vari kuona maWarriors achidyiwa mumitambo yavo yese iyo vari kusanga neAlgeria , Senegal pamwe neTunisia .
Mutsigiri wechikwata cheDynamos , VaShephed Saizi , vanoti vatambi vanofanirwa kubatwa zvakanaka vachiwedzera ivo kuti nemabatirwo anga achiitwa maWarriors , vari kuona pasina chimuko kuGabon .
Zvikwata zviviri kubva mugungano reZimbabwe ndizvo zvinoendera mberi nemakundano aya .
MaWarriors ari kutarisirwa kutamba mutambo wekuedzana masimba neCameroon muYaounde mangwana .
Mutambo wavo wekutanga mumaAfrica Cup of Nations uriko neSvondo apo vari kusangana nemaDesert Foxes ekuAlgeria .
Mvura yakawanda yakanaya muBindura nemusi weMuvhuro inonzi yakaita mafashamu akazopinda mudzimba achiparadza midzyo yakasiyanasiyana .
Kanzura wewadhi 10 uye vari mutevedzeri wameya weBindura , VaNorbert Dhokotera , vanoti kuvhara kwemigero inofanirwa kunge ichirasa mvura ndiko kwakakonzera kuti mvura iyi ijenge ichizopinda mudzimba .
VaDhokotera vanoti kanzuru yavo ichishanda pamwechete nemapurisa neCivil Protection Unit vachiri kuongorora kuti zvinhu zvakakanganiswa nemvura iyi zvakawanda zvakadii , uye kuti vanhu vangani vakawirwa nedambudziko iri .
Kanzuru iri kupomerwawo mhosva yekubvumidza vanhu kuvakira mumadafanha nemunzvimbo dzekurasa nadzo mvura .
Asi VaDhokotera varamba kuti kanzuru yavo yakapa vanhu mvumo vachiti vari mushishi kuti vapiwe mvumo nematare yekuti vaputse dzimba dzakavakwa zviri kunze kwemutemo idzi .
Vashandi vehurumende varamba kutambira mari yanga yavimbiswa nehurumende mumusangano wavaita nehurumende pasi peNational Joint Negotiating Council .
Vachitaura neStudio7 mushure memusangano uyu , uyo watora maawa mashanu , sachigaro wesangano rinomirira vashandi vehurumende reApex Council , Amai Cecillia Alexander , vati hapana chine musoro chabuda mumusangano uyu .
Amai Alexander vati varamba mari yavanga vapihwa nehurumende yanga ichiita kuti mushandi wepasipasi awedzerwe nezvikamu makumi mapfumbamwe nezvinomwe kubva muzana .
Amai Alexander vati vashandi vehurumende vari kuda kuti vabhadharwe mari yakaringana neinenge iri pamusika webhanga kana kuti interbank rate .
Vanga vachitungamira nhaurirano idzi vakamirira divi rehurumende , VaMoses Mhike , varamba kutaura nezvenyaya iyi vachiti titaure negurukota rinoona nezvevashandi , VaPaul Mavhima , avo vanga vasiri kudaira nharembozha yavo .
Amai Alexander vati vachaita musangano nenhengo dzavo neMuvhuro kuti vaone kuti votora danho ripi zvichitevera kutadza kuwirirana kwavaita nehurumende .
Nekune rumwe rutivi , mamwe masangano anomirira vadzidzisi asiri muApex Council akaita seAmalgamated Rural Teachers Union of Zimbabwe akatozivisa kare kuti nhengo dzawo hadzisi kuzoenda kubasa pachavhurwa zvikoro svondo rinouya sezvo achiti mari dzavari kutambiriswa nehurumende hadzisisina chadzinokwana .
Apex Council inotiwo dzimwe nhengo dzayo hadzisati dzadzoka kumabasa kubva zvadzakaenda kuzororo rekisimusi kubudikidza nekushaiwa mari dzemabhazi .
Hurumende inoti haikwanise kubhadhara vashandi vayo mari dzavari kuda sezvo ichiti homwe yayo yakabooka .
Mutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa vasvika kuBotswana kumusangano wekudyidzana unoitwa mukati memakore maviri nenyika iyi kana kuti Bi - National Commission .
VaMnangagwa vaenda nemakurukota anosanganisira rezvemari Muzvinafundo Mthuli Ncube , rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko amai monica mutsvangwa uye rezvehutano dr obadiah moyo .
Munyori mukuru mubazi rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , VaNick Mangwana vati nhaurirano dzakatanga nemusi weChipiri uye mangwana VaMnangagwa nemumwe wavo VaMokgweetsi Masisi vachava zvapupu pakunyoreranwa kwezvibvumirano zvatenderanwa .
Zvibvumirano zviri munyaya dzezvekutengeserana , dzidzo uye nyaya dzezvehutano .
Paramende iri kutarisirwa kuzeya zvakabuda muongororo yemhirizhonga yakaita mushure mesarudzo zviri mugwaro rekomisheni yaitungamirwa nevaimbove mutungamiri weSouth Africa , VaKgalema Motlanthe .
Izvi zvinotevera chikumbiro chaitwa nenhengo yeMDC muparamende .
Gwaro iri rakaburitswa neChipiri kune veruzhinji nemutungamiriri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , zvichitevera ongororo yakaitwa nekomisheni yaVaMotlanthe .
Mumiriri weMbizo muNational Assembly , VaSettlement Chikwinya , veMDC vaudza mutauriri wedare iri , Advocate Jacob Mudenda , kuti zvakakosha kuti zvakabuda muongororo iyi zvizeyiwe nedare iri sezvo zvine chekuita nedare iri pamwe nekushandurwa kwemimwe mitemo yakaita sewesarudzo .
Gurukota rezvemitemo neparamende , VaZiyambi Ziyambi , vati hapana chakaipa panyaya yaVaChikwinya uye vachapinza gwaro iri mudariro pachabva dare iri kuzororo pakati paNdira gore rinouuya .
Vanokokera nhengo dzeMDC muparamende , VaProsper Mutseyami , vaudza Studio7 vati zvakakosha kuti nhengo dzeparamende dzizeye gwaro iri nekuti pane zvimwe zvisina kujekeswa mukati maro .
Mukuru weZimbabwe Democracy Institute , Doctor Pedzisayi Ruhanya , vati kunyange paramende ikazeya gwaro iri , hazvina zvazvinobatsira nekuti mabhiri ese anobva kumutungamiriri wenyika .
Vati zviri kuna VaMnangagwa kutevedza zvakataura naVaMotlanthe nekomisheni yavo .
Asi mutauriri weCrisis In Zimbabwe Coalition , VaTabani Moyo , vati zvakakosha kuti paramende iongorore gwaro iri pamwe nekuona mutungamiriri wenyika atevedza zviri mugwaro iri .
Zvichakadai , nhengo dzeparamende dzeMDC dzaramba kutambira mifaninidzo yemutungamiriri wenyika adzapihwa neparamende pamwe nemakhadi anonzi abva kumahofisi emutungamiriri wenyika .
VaMutseyami vaudza Studio 7 kuti havana chikonzero chekutora mifanidzo iyi nekuti bato ravo haritori VaMnangagwa semutungamiriri wenyika yeZimbabwe .
VaChikwinya vatiwo kunyange dai vaida kutora mifananidzo iyi , havana kwekuisa mifanidzo iyi nekuti ivo senhengo dzeparamende dzese , havana mahofisi kana kuti maConstituency Office munzvimbo dzavanomirira .
Sangano re Cancer Association Of Zimbabwe ririkukurudzira vanhu vane makore makumi mana zvichikwira kuti vaende kunovhenekwa zvirwere zvegomarara .
Izvi zvinotevera mashoko ekuti mutungamiri webato rinopikisa reMDC - T VaMorgan Tsvangirai ari kurapwa chirwere chegomarara rematumbu .
Amai Lyne Mupunzwana mukuru kana kuti Health Services manager vesangano re Cancer Association Of Zimbabwe vanoti vanhu vazhinji vanouya kunotsvaga rubatsiro chirwere chakomba izvo zvinoita kuti zvinhu zvisavafambe zvakanaka dzimwe nguva .

Doctor Chipo Dendere , avo vanodzidzisa pachikoro chepamusorosoro cheGettysburg College , chiri mudunhu rePennyslvania muAmerica , vanoti imwe nzira huru inoita kuti vanhu vari kunze kwenyika vazive zviri kuitika kumusha , kuverenga nhau zuva roga roga .
Vanotiwo izvi ndizvo zviri kubatsira zvikuru dzimwe nyika dzemuAfrica dzine zvizvarwa zviri kunze , dzakaita seNigeria , Ghana nedzimwe , kuburikidza nezvizvarwa zvasdzo zviri kupinda mune zvematongerwo enyika kana kutanga mabhizimusi .
Zvizvarwa zveZimbabwe zvinodarika mamiriyoni matatu zvinofungidzirwa kuti zviri kunze kwenyika , uye mari dzinotumirwa nevanhu ivava ndidzo dziri kubatsira zvikuru mukufambisa hupfumi hwenyika .
Vazhinji vevari kunze kwenyika ava vanonzi vari kuitawo zvirongwa zvakasiyanasiyana zvinosanganisira zvekuvaka , kubatsira vanoshaya uye kusimudzira matunhu avanobva .
Rimwe sangano rinomirira vabereki vane vana vasinganzwe , reDeaf Zimbabwe Trust , raudza paramende neChitatu kuti vana vazhinji vasinganzwi havasi kuenda kuchikoro munyika sezvo zvikoro zvisina varairidzi vane ruzivo rwekudzidzisa vana ava pamwe nemabhuku .
Vachipa humbowo maererano nematambudziko anotarisana nevana ava kukomiti yeparamende inoona nezvedzidzo , imwe nhengo yesangano iri , Amai Barbra Nyangairi , vati zvinosuwisa kuti vana vanodarika zvikamu makumi mapfumbamwe nezvina kubva muzana havasi kuenda kuchikoro .
Vati kunyange zvikamu zvitanhatu nechidimbu kubva muzana zvevari kuenda kuchikoro , vana ava havasi kudzidza zvakanaka , uye zvikoro zvizhinji hazvisina varairidzi vane ruzizvo rwekudzidzisa vana ava .
Amai Nyangairi vati kunyange hazvo pane Maduramanzwi evana vasinganzwe akanyorwa , haasati ave kushandiswa muzvikoro uyewo varaidzi vazhinji havakwanisi kutaura nevana ava sezvo vasingazive mutauro wavo kana kuti Sign Language .
Vati chikumbiro chavo kubazi rezvedzidzo ndechekuti mutauro wemaoko ushandiswe muzvikoro zvese uyewo kuti zvikoro zvevarairidzi zvidzidzise varairidzi kuti vakwanise kudzidzisa vana vasinganzwe .

Kudzai Madzivire anoti akaongororwa pamwechete nenhengo dzekomiti yeparamende pakiriniki yemuGweru , akazoshamiswa achiona zita rake rakanyorwa padandemutande achinzi aiva atapurirwa Covid 19 .
Madzivire anoti pakatanga veruzhinji kuziva kuti aive neCovid - 19 , vanhu vakawanda vakabva vatanga kumusema .
Madzivire anoti musikana wake waaida kuroora mukupera kwegore , akamuramba netsambambozha yaakatumira parunhare mbozha achiti aiva asisakwanise kuenderera mberi nezvehurongwa rwokuti varoorane .
Madzivire anoti pakabuda nyaya iyi iye aiva asati ava kuratidza kurwara , asi akazotanga kurwara achirwadziwa muchipfuva akatomboedza kutsvaga rubatsiro kumakiriniki emuBudiriro asi hapana akauya kuzomuona .

Madzivire anoti akaona vanhu vaifa zuva nezuva zvinova zvimwe zvakakonzera kuti asapore nekukurumidza nokuti aifunga kuti haabude muchipatara ari mupenyu .

Mugwaro rakaburitswa neChishanu nesangano iri , Senior Hospital Doctors Association inoti rubatsiro rweHigher Life Foundation rwakanaka chose , asi arwugadzirise matambudziko ari muzvipatara zvehurumende , izvo zvsina mishonga , michina pamwe nezvimwe zvinetswa .
Munyori mukuru we Senior Hospital Doctors Association , Dr . Aaron Musara , vanoti haisi mari chete iri kudiwa navana chiremba , asi kuti vari kuda kuti muzvipatara munge muine mishonga yakakwana nezvimwe zvikwanisiro kuitira kuti varwere varapwe nemazvo .
Dr . Musara vanoti vanotambira nemufaro chido chiri kuratidzwa nesangano reHigher Life Foundation , asi chavanopokanqa nacho chete inyaya yekuti sangano iri rava kuti haridi kutaura navana chiremba , asi iro rakambotanga raenda kwavari richida kunzwa zvichemo zvavo .

Asi Dr . Musara vanoti muzvipatara mukava nezvose zvinodiwa , uye vana chiremba vachipihwa mihoro inokodzera , vana chiremba vose vasiri kuenda kubasa vanodzokera kumabasa avo .

Amai Mutsvangwa vakurudzira vechidiki kuti varege zvekukanganisa hutano hwavo nekufurirwa kumwa nekuputa zvinodhaka .

Mubatanidzwa wemapato ari munhaurirano nemutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , Political Actors Dialogue , Polad , unonzi wakasunga kuti uite nhaurirano nemasangano eUnited Nations , International Monetary Fund , World Bank , pamwe nevamwe vane chekuita nezvirango zvinonzi zvakatemerwa vamwe vakuru muhurumende nevekumadokera .
Polad yakabuda nechisungo ichi kumusangano wayo wemazuva maviri wakapera neChitatu waiitirwa kuNyanga , apo vatungamiri vemamwe mapato anopikisa vakakwikwidza musarudzo dzegore rapera vari mumubatanidzwa uyu vakazivisa kuti vanoda kuti zvirango izvi zvibviswe vachiti zviri kurwadzisa vana veZimbabwe .
Mapato aya anoti zvirango izvi zviri kutadzisa kuti nyika iende mberi nekuda kwekunyimwa zvikwereti nemasangano akaita seIMF neWorld Bank .
POLAD ine mapato gumi nemanomwe , ayo ari kutsigirana neZanu PF panyaya yezvirango iyi .
Mutauriri werimwe remapato ari muPolad , reNational Constitutional Assembly , NCA , VaMadock Chivasa , vanoti kunyange hazvo vasingataure vakamirira Polad , bato ravo riri kuti zvirango izvi zvibviswe , kana Zanu PF iri kutadza basa yosara isina chekuhwanda nacho .
Asi vanoona nezvekufambiswa kwezvirongwa musangano reZimbabwe Network for Social Justice , uye vachiongorora zvematongerwo enyika , VaTendai Ruben Mbofana , vanoti havaoni zvirango izvi pazviri kubata nyika , sezvo zvakatemerwa vanhu zana nemakumi mana nevaviri chete .
VaMbofana vanoti hurumende yeZanu PF pamwe nemapato ari muPolad vanogona kunge vaine zvimwe zvavari kuwana kubva mukunyepera vanhu kuti zvirango zvauraya nyika .
Asi VaChivasa vanoti hapana munhu ari kugara muZimbabwe pari zvino asingazive kuti zvirango zvakasunga sei nyika , sezvo iri kutadza kukwereteswa mari nemasangano akaita seIMF neWorld Bank nekuda kwezvirango izvi .
Munyori anoona nezvekuenzaniswa kwemikana pakati pevanhurume nevanhukadzi uye kugara kwakanaka musangano revarairidzi vekumaruwa , reAmalgamated Rural Teachers Union of Zimbabwe , ARTUZ , mudunhu reMasvingo , Amai Sheila Chirisamhuru , vasungwa nemapurisa kuMasvingo kwakare .
Izvi zvinotevera kuratidzira kwaitwa nevarairidzi mudunhu iri vachiti vanoda kuti hurumende ivape mihoro yavo nemari yekuAmerica .
Gweta riri kumirira Amai Chirisamhuru , VaMartin Mureri vekambani yemagweta yeMatutu and Mureri Legal Practitioners , vanoti Amai Chirisamhuru vave kupomerwa mosva yetyora mutemo weMOPA nekuungana vasina mvumo yemapurisa mushure mekumbenge vapomerwa mhosva yekuita zvemhirizhonga .
VaMureri vanoti Amai Chirisamhuru vambochengetedzwa pakamba yemapurisa yeChikato vasati vaiswa mumaoko ematikitivha edivi reLaw and Order uko vacharara usiku hwanhasi paine tarisiro yekuti vamiswe pamberi pedare neChipiri .
Varairidzi vanodarika zana nemakumi mashanu varatidzira pamahofisi edzidzo muMasvingo vachiti vanoda kuti hurumende ivape mihoro yavo nemari yekuAmerica inoita madhora mazana mashanu nemakumi maviri pamwedzi .
Studio 7 yakundikana kubata mutauriri wemapurisa , Assistant Commissioner Paul Nyathi kuti tinzwe divi remapurisa panyaya iyi .
Hurumende yakawedzera vashandi vayo mari dzemihoro svondo rapera asi iri kurambwa nemasangano ose anomirira vashandi vachiti havana kutanga vagarwa navo pasi .
Asi gurukota rezvevashandi nemabasa , Muzvinafundo Paul Mavhima vakaudza Studio 7 kuti hurumende yagara iri kuronga kusangana nevashandi vayo kuti vazeye nyaya dzemihoro mwedzi uno .
Munyori wesangano reARTUZ , VaRobson Chere vanoti neMuvhuro nhengo dzavo chete ndidzo dzakaratidzira , asi vanotarisira rutsigiro kubva kune mamwe masangano pamwe nevashandi vari kuda kuti mihoro yavo igadziriswe .
VaChere vanoti vacharamba vachiratidzira nyika yose kusvika hurumende yavabhadhara mihoro yavo nemadhora ekuAmerica ayo vanoti anokwanisa kutenga .
Varairidzi ava vanoti vari kuda kuti mihoro yavo ive mumadhora ekuAmerica anoita mazana mashanu nemakumi maviri pamwedzi .
Nhepfenyuro yeStudio7 yasvitsa makore gumi nemana itipfenyura zviri kuitika muZimbabwe .
Vanhu vazhinji munyika vanoti vari kufarira zvikuru nhepfeunyuro iyi , vamwe vachiti Studio7 inofanira kuwedzera nguva dzekutepfemyura .
Asi vamwe vanoti Studio7 inofanira kutepfenyura iri munyika sezviri kuitwa nedzimwe nhepfenyuro vachiti pari zvino zvairi kuita zviri kunze kwemutemo .
Mutauriri weMDC inotungamirirwa naVaMorgan Tsvangirai , VaObert Gutu , vakorokotedza Studio7 nekusvitsa kwayaita makore gumi nemana iri pamhepo .
VaGutu nevamwe vakawanda munyika vanosanganisira vanhuwo zvavo , pamwe nemasangano akazvimirira , vanoti Studio7 , inhepfenyuro inopa vanhu vese mukana wekutaura zvisinei nekuti vakarerekera divi ripi .
Mumwe mugari wemuHarare , Amai Winnie Mambo , vanoti Studio7 inhepfenyuro inovapa nhau dzakasiyana nedzimwe nhau dzavanonzwa pane dzimwe nhepfenyuro dzemuZimbabwe .
Vanotiwo vanonzwa paStudio7 nhau dzezvinhu zvinotika munyika dzichipakurwa pachena .
Mutauriri weMDC inotungamirirwa naVaWelshman Ncube , VaKurauone Chihwai , vanoti Studio7 inhepfenyuro inowanzopa mukana kumapato ese ezvematongerwo enyika uye inosvikawo kunzvimbo zhinji munyika dzisingasvikwe nedzimwe nhepfenyuror dziri munyika .
VaGutu vanoti mukurumbira une Studio7 kumaruwa unoratidza kune inofarirwa neveruzhinji zvakanyanya .
Asi kunyange hazvo paine mufaro nemabasa eStudio7 , vakawanda vanotiwo dai nhepfenyuro iyi yavandudzawo mashandiro ayo .
Asi Amai Mambo vanoti nhepfunyuro yeStudio 7 iri kuwanza nyaya dzemuHarare uye dai yatepfenyurawo nhau dzekumaruwa .
Ukuwo VaChihwai vanoti shuviro yavo ndeyekuti dai Studio7 yatepfenyurawo nemimwe mutauro inotaurwa munyika .
VaGutu vanoti kunyange hazvo pane nhepfenyuro dzakawanda dzakapihwa marezenisi makore mashonana apfuura , nhepfenyuro idzi dzinenge dzinotaura neizwi rimwe chete .
Chikumbiro chaVa Gutu nebato ravo ndechekuti dai yawedzera nguva yekutepfenyura uyewo kuti dai yatepfenyura nemimwe mitauro yakaita seVenda , Tonga nemimwe .
Mumwe wevechidiki muHarare , VaDenford Ngadziore , vanoti dai Studio7 yatotanga terevhizheni chaiyo .
Asi nhengo yeZanu PF zvakare vachimirira Makonde muparamende , VaKindness Paradza , vanoti ivo nebato ravo havafariri Studio7 nekuti inotepfenyura zvisiri pamutemo uye ichitepfenyura kubva kunyika inovengana neZimbabwe .
Vati Studio7 kana ichida kuwirirana nehurumende yeZanu PF , inofanira kunyoresa kuZimbabwe Media Commission yoshanda zviri pamutemo .
Vati semaonero avo nhepfenyuro yeStudio7 inotaura manyepo uye inotsigira mapato anopikisa .
Kunyange hazvo VaParadza vati bato ravo harifariri Studio7 , vazhinji kusanganisira makurukota ehurumende , vatsigiri pamwe nenhengo dzeparamende , kusanganisira dzeZanu PF , dzinoteerera nhepfenyuro iyi , kana kutaura paStudio7 .
Asi VaParadza vanoti havanganyarari kana vabvunzwa mubvunzo .
Asi veStudio7 vanoti vari kutepfenyura zviri pamutemo sezvinodiwa nemitemo yekutepfenyura pasi rose kunyange hazvo vamwe muhurumende yeZimbabwe vasingazvifarire .
Mukuru weMedia Centre , VaEnerst Mudzengi , vanoti Studio7 inhepfenyuro iri kuita basa guru munyika zvikurusei pakupakuranhau dzine mativi ese mungava munyaya dzezvematongerwo enyika , hupfumi nezvimwe .
Vanoti dai zvaibvira nguva inotepfenyura Studio7 yawedzerwa .
Mukuru weZimbabwe Democracy Institute , Doctor Pedzisai Ruhanya , avo vaive mutapi wenhau kuDaily News apo pakatanga Studio7 muna 2003 , vanoti nhepfenyuro iyi yakaita basa guru panyaya yekuburitsa nyaya yeZimbabwe .
VaRuhanya vanobvumirana naVaMudzengi vachiti Studio7 iri kutorwadzisa vateereri vayo nekutepfenyura kwenguva pfupi .
Vanoti dai Studio7 yaitawo nhau dzemangwanani nemasikati kwete kutepfenyura manheru chete .
VeMedia Insitute of Southern Africa - Zimbabwe Chapter , vatenda zvikuru Studio7 nekuramba yakashinga nebasa ravo zvisinei nekuti hurumende yakamira mira zvikuru sei panguva yehurumende yemubatanidzwa kuti nhepfenyuro iyi ivharwe .
Vanoona nezvekushambadzwa kwezvirongwa musangano iri , VaTabani Moyo , vanoti chimwe chasimbisa Studio7 inyaya yekuti nhepfunyuro iyi yaramba ichiburitsa nyaya dzinofarirwa neveruzhinji .
Vatsinhirawo mashoko evamwe ekuti Studio7 inofanirawo kupinda mumaruwa ichiburitsa nyaya dzevanhu vakawanda munzvimbo idzi avo vari kushaya kwekutaura nhunha dzavo .
Vatiwo kunyange hazvo munyika mave nenhepfenyuro dzakawanda , zhinji dzacho dzakarerekera divi rimwe izvo zvisingabatsire nyika neveruzhinji .
Studio7 yakaparurwa nechirongwa cheChirungu musi wa 27 Ndira , 2003 apo zvinhu zvakange zvakaoma munyika munyaya dzekutora nhau , kutepfenyura pamwe nekufambiswa kwemashoko munyika .
Zvirongwa zveNdebele neShona zvakazotanga kutepfenyurwa musi wa 7 Kubvumbi 2003 .
Mumwe mukomana wechidiki ane makore makumi matatu nematanhatu VaTafadzwa Chiwaridzo vanoti vari kushandisa chipo chavo chekuimba mukuparidza vhangeri .
VaChiwaridzo vakaburitsa madambarefu maviri kusvika parizvino .
Dambarefu rekutanga rinonzi Baba Ndadzoka .
VaChiwaridzo vanoti , """" Ndakaimba nokuda kwekuti ndakamborarama zvakashata ndichitaridza Mwari asi ndakazoparidzirwa kudzoka kunashe .
Saka ndinoda kuti ndiyedze nepose pandinogona kuti ndiite kuti vanhu vazive Mwari nokuti nguva yapera . """"
VaChiwaridzo vanoti vari kunetsekawo nedambudziko rekushaya magitare nezvimwe zvinodiwa pakuimba .
Muimbi wechitendero uyu anoti akabura rimwe dambarefu idzva rinonzi Munondichengeta .
VaChiwaridzo vari kukurudzira vechidiki kuti vararame munashe nekuti nyika yananga kumagumo .
VaChiwaridzo vanogara kuChegutu kuMashonaland West .
Vanhu vakawanda vanoti boka reZimbabwe Anti - Corruption Commission rinofanirwa kuita ongororo pane zvakabuda mugwaro raAuditor General vachiti kana izvi zvikasaitwa , kurwisa huwori mumapazi ehurumende kuchanetsa .
Vachipa maonero avo pane zvakabuda mugwaro raAuditor General regore ra2018 , vanhu vakasiyana siyana vataura neStudio7 vanoti zvakakosha Zimbabwe Anti - Corruption Commission iongorore nyaya dzose dzinonongedza kuti pane huwori hunogona kuve hwakaitwa mungave mumakanzuru kana mumapazi ehurumende pamwe nemakambani ehurumende .
Vakanangana nemakanzuru akasiyana siyana emunyika , Auditor General , Amai Mildred Chiri , vakati makanzuru mazhinji haazi kubudisa nenguva yakafanira , magwaro anoratidza mashandisirwo emari .
Gwaro iri rinoratidzawo kuti pane kusabatwa kwemari zvakanaka kwakaitika mune mamwe makanzuru kusanganisira eBulawayo , Gweru neHarare .
Sachigaro wekomiti yekanzuru inoona nezvekushandiswa kwemari muguta reBulawayo , VaSilas Chigora , vaudza Studio7 kuti vanogutsikana nezvakabuda mugwaro raAuditor General vachiti kanzuru yavo ichaferefeta nyaya yekuti pane mumwe mushandi akazvipa chikwereti zvisiri pamutemo .
Gwaro raAuditor General rakabudisa kuti muguta reGweru pane kusawirirana pamari yemitero yakabhadharwa nevagari nemari iri kubhanga rekanzuru iyi uyewo kuti pane vashandi vanonzi vange vasina kutora mazuva ezororo kwemakore akawanda .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa kukanzuru yeGweru kuti ichaita seyi negwaro raAmai Chiri .
Asi mukuru weGweru Residents Forum , VaCharles Mazorodze , vaudza Studio 7 kuti kusaitwa kwemagwaro emashandisirwo emari nenguva yakafanira uye kusabatwa kwemari zvakanaka , kunokanganisa zvikuru kuti makanzuru aite mabasa aanotarisirwa kuita nemazvo .
Vati Zimbabwe Anti - Corruption Commission inofanirwa kuongorora zvizere gwaro raAuditor General kuitira kuti vakapara mhosva vabatwe nemutemo .
Amai Chiri vanoti vakaendesa gwaro ravo kuZACC .
Asi Studio7 haina kukwanisa kubata sachigaro weZACC , Amai Loice Matanda Moyo , kuti tinzwe kuti vachafambisa seyi nyaya yakaiswa mumaoko ekomisheni yavo .
VaProctor Nyemba vesangano reAssociation of Certified Forensic Practitioners vabvuma kuti munguva yapfuura hapana chinobatika chiitwa kana pabudiswa ongororo dzinoratidza huwori mumapazi ehurumende .
Asi vati vane chokwadi kuti ZACC ichaita basa rayo sezvinotarisirwa .
VaNyemba vati zvakakoshawo kuti makanzuru , mapazi ehurumende pamwe nemakambani ehurumende , aite zvirongwa zvinobatsira kudzivirira huwori .
Mudzidzisi wezvidzidzo zvebudiriro paMidlands State Univeristy , VaVincent Chakunda , vachitaura semuongorori akazvimirira , vati huwori hunodzorera budiriro yenyika zvakanyanya vakatsinhirawo kuti ZACC inofanirwa kuita ongororo pamusoro pezvakabuda mugwaro raAuditor General .
Gore rega rega hofisi yaAuditor General inobudisa gwaro rinoratidza mashandisirwo emari nemapazi ehurumende , makambani ehurumende pamwe nemakanzuru emunyika .
Magwaro aya anogara achibudisa nyaya dzehuwori dzinoitika asi pasina matanho anotorwa nehurumende .
Muzvare Rushwaya vakaburitswa muhusungwa neMuvhuro mushure mekubhadhariswa mari yechibatiso , zvichitevera kusungirwa nyaya yekuita zvehuori nekutengesa mitambo kwavakaitwa neChishanu chapfuura
Komiti yedare reparamende inoona nezve dzidzo , tsika nezvemitambo nhasi yabvunzurudza munyori webazi re dzidzo , Va Steven Mahere , vakuru we Sports and Recreation Commission ne ZIFA pamusoro pe nyaya ye Asiagate umo vatambi vebhora vemu Zimbabwe vanonzi vaibhadharwa kuti vatengese mitambo yenhabvu iyo vaitamba kunyika dziri ku Asia .
Panguva iyi chief executive veZIFA , Muzvare Henrietta Rushwaya , ndivo vaironga mitambo iyi .
Muzvare Rushwaya vakaburitswa muhusungwa neMuvhuro mushure mekubhadhariswa mari yechibatiso , zvichitevera kusungirwa nyaya yekuita zvehuori nekutengesa mitambo kwavakaitwa neChishanu chapfuura .
Nhengo ye komiti iyi , Jeffreyson Chitando , vaudza Studio seven kuti mapato ose e MDC ne ZANU - PF muparamende akabatana mukuedza kutsvaga chokwadi munyaya iyi uye kuti nyaya ye huwori munhabvu nemitambo ibviswe .
Va Chitando vati Muzvare Rushwaya vainga vakabata vanhu vazhinji kubva kuhofisi yemutungamiriri wenyika , hofisi dzekupinda nekubuda munyika nevamwe vazhinji izvo zvakaita kuti nyaya iyi ienderere kwemakore pasina aizvibata .
Vanoongorora nyaya dzemitambo nevamwe vanotsigira chikwata cheZimbabwe Mighty Wariors vanoti chakatamba zvinodadisa kunyangwe chakakundwa neGermany 6 - 1 nemusi weChitatu mumutambo wacho wekutanga wenhabvu yemadzimai kumaOlympics .
Makwikwi aya ari kuitirwa kuSao Paolo , Brazil .
Zimbabwe neGermany dziri muGroup F pamwe nedzimwe nyika dzakaita seCanada neAustralia .
Pamitambo yakatambwa nemusi weChina , France yakakunda Colombia 4 - 0 .
Mimwe mitambo yakatambwa neChitatu , Sweden yakakunda South Africa 1 - 0 , Brazil ikakunda China 3 - 0 .
MuGroup G , United States of America yakakunda New Zealand 2 - 0 .
Makwikwi eCastle Premier Soccer League atsvuka ropa kwasara mitambo mipfumbamwe chete .
Chicken Inn , Dynamos ne FC Platinum ndidzo dziri panhongonya asi kune zvimwe zvikwata zviri kumucheto zvorwa semvumba kuti zvisanyure zvichienda kudivision one .
Mushure memitambo makumi maviri nemumwechete uyezve kwasara mitambo mipfumbamwe ,
Chikwata cheChicken Inn charamba chiripamusoro soro pecastle Premier Soccer League mushure mekurova Highlanders 3 - 2 .
Kukundwa uku hakuna kufadza vatsigiri vebosso avo vaiimba nekunyomba murairidzi wavo Bongani Mafu apo pakapera mutambo uyu .
Asi vatsigiri veChicken Inn vakapemberera zvikuru mushure mekunge Mitchell Katsvairo arova mambure apo muridzi wepembe ainge ave pedyo nekuridza kuti mutambo wapera .
Chibodzwa ichi chakasangana nemberero huru mushure mekunge magame Cocks anzwa kuti Dynamos yakundawao zvekare .
Chikwata che FC Platinum chave pachinhanho chechitatu mapoinzi mashanu pasi pechikwata chirikutungamira chChicken Inn .
Izvi zvinotevera kuenda kwavakaita nekunokunda chikwata chetriangle kuGibbo Stadium neSvondo izvo zvasiya zvekare vari poindi imwechete pasi pechikwata cheDynamos icho chiri pachinhanho chechipiri .
Chikwata chaVaNorman Mapeza cheFC Platinum chikakunda Chicken Inn neDynamos mumutambo yavo uyezve Dynamos neChicken Inn dzikaita mangange , mamoney Bags anoenda pamusoro pemakundao aya .
Mutambi wavo anemukurumbira Brian Muzondiwa anoti chinangwa chavo ndechekutora mukombe wakakosha uyu .
Asi vanotevera Dynamos vanoti mukombe ndewavo .
VaModercai Mapondera vanoti varikufara zvikuru nekukunda kwavakaita How Mine 1 - 0 neSvondo kuRufaro Stadium .
