Zvizvarwa zveZimbabwe zviri muSouth Africa zvakawanda zvinonzi zviri kutambira nemufaro danho rakatorwa nehurumende yeSouth Africa , rekurerutsa zvinodiwa pakufamba kuti mwana mudiki ange achibvumidzwa kupinda munyika iyi .
Asi vamwe vanoti danho rakatorwa neSouth Africa iri richawedzera kubiwa kwevana , kana kuona vabereki vanenge vachirwira vana vachipedzisira vatiza nevana vasina kupiwa mvumo nemumwe mubereki sezvanga zvichiitika .
Izvi zvinotevera danho rakatorwa negurukota rinoona nezvemukati meSouth Africa , VaAaron Motsoaledi svondo rapera , rekusaina mutemo mutsva unobvumidza kupinda nekubuda kwevana vasiri vemunyika iyi vasina mamwe magwaro pamusoro peekufambisa avanenge vainawo .
Mutemo uyu unonzi uchabatsira zvikuru vana vane vabereki vekune dzimwe nyika dzinosanganisira Zimbabwe , avo vanga vachimanikidzwa kuve nemagwaro akaita seekuberekwa , ma affidavit kana tsamba inobva kune mumwe wevabereki kana mwana achifamba nemubereki mumwechete , kana kufamba nemunhu anenge asiri mubereki wake .
Bazi rezvemukati meSouth Africa iri rinonzi rakatozivisa mamwe mapazi anosanganisira rekupinda nekubuda kwevanhu nezveshanduko iyi .
Mukuru wesangano re Immigration Advisory for Southern Africa , uye vari gweta rinorwira kodzero dzevanhu , Advocate Gabriel Shumba , vanoti sesangano vanozvitambira nemufaro sezvo zviri zvinhu zvavanga vagara vachitaura zvavo kuti magwaro akawanda anononotsa kufamba kwevanhu pamiganho .
Panyaya yekuti zvinogona kuwedzera nyaya dzekubiwa kana kufambiswa kwevana zvisina mvumo , Advocate Shumba vanoti kana mutemo wanga uripo wacho wanga usingambonyanyi kumisa kufambiswa kwevana zvisiri pamutemo nekuda kwehuwori hwaiitwa pamiganho .
Vaimbove murwiri werusununguko uye vakamboshandawo nevaimbove mutungamiri wenyika VaRobert Mugabe kwenguva yareba , Amai Margaret Dongo , vanoti hazvishamise kuti kusajeka kwekuti VaMugabe vacharadzikwa kupi inyaya yekuti bato reZanu PF rine mutemo wekuti anenge apanduka haaradzikwe kunovigwa magamba enyika , kuNational Heroes Acre muHarare .
Amai Dongo vanoti kana paine chokwadi pamashoko ari kubuda ekuti VaMugabe vakazivisa mhuri yavo kuti vaida kuradzikwa kumusha kwavo kwaZvimba pedyo naamai vavo VaBona , kwete kuNational Heroes Acre , zvinofanirwa kuremekedzwa .
"""" VaMugabe pavanga vachiri pachigaro nemakurukota avo ndivo vakadzika mutemo wekuti munhu anoshaya abuditswa mubato reZanu PF haaizofanira kuradzikwa kumarinda eHeroes Acre , """" Amai Dongo vanodaro .
Vanoti VaMugabe munhu aida kumira nezvaanenga atsidzira , izvo zvinoita kuti vagone kunge vakaudza mhuri yavo kuti vaizoda kuchengetedzwa zvavo kumusha kwavo kwaZvimba .
Pari zvino hurumende haisati yazivisa kuti hurongwa hwekuradzika VaMugabe hwakamira sei sezvo gurukota rekufambiswa kwemashoko Amai Monica Mutsvangwa vati basa iroro riri mumaoko ekomiti iri kutungamira hurongwa hwekuvigwa kwaVaMugabe .
Hurumende yazivisa kuti mhuri yekwaMugabe nevamwe vakuru muhurumende , vachitungamirwa nemutevedzeri wemutungamiri wenyika VaKembo Mohadi , vasimuka vakananga kuSingapore uko vari kunosangana naAmai Grace Mugabe nemhuri yavo vachigadzirira kudzosa mutumbi wamufi kumusha .
Mutumbi waVaMugabe uri kutarisirwa kusvika munyika neChitatu svondo rino .
Madzimai akawanda vari kuenda kuZambia kunoita basa rekurarama nekuita zvepabonde vachiti kuoma kwehupenyu munyika ndizvo zviri kuvatuma kuita zvepabonde vachibhadharisa .
Madzimai aya vakawanda vavo vanobva kunzvimbo dzakaita seKariba , Karoi , Chinhoyi , Chegutu , Kadoma pamwe nemaguta makuru akaita seHarare .
Vanoti kuita zvechipfambi kuZambia zviri kubhadhara sezvo vari kupihwa mari yekuAmerica .
Vazhinji vemadzimai aya vanoti vanozonochinja mari iyi voisa kuma bond notes zvinozoita kuti ive inowanda zvichienzaniswa nekupihwa ma bond notes .
Mumwe wemadzimai aya uyo anoti anoda kuzivikanwa saAmai Shupi vanobva kuKaroi vanoti zvinonzi muroyi royera kure kuti vepedyo vagokureverera nokudaro havadi kuzivikanwa zvavanoita munharaunda mavanogara .
Amai Shupikai vanoti chimwe chikonzero ndechekuti zvechipfambi zvinosungisa asi kuZambia hazvisungise nemapurisa sezvo vanenge vaine dzimba dzavanenge vachishandisa .
Chimwe chizvarwa chekuZambia , VaMaxwell Mwale , vanoti madzimai ekuZimbabwe vari kuita zvechipfambi vakawandisa zvakanyanya pamuganhu weZimbabwe neZambia .
Asi VaMwale vanoti havasi kuwana mari yakawanda sezvavanotaura sezvo vari kuva bhadhara mari inoita madhora matatu kusvika pamadhora mashanu panguva pfupi yavanenge vachitandadzana .
Asi mumwe mudzimai wekuDemocratic Republic of Congo anotyaira motokari dzinotakura zvinorema , Amai Elizabeth Lewis , vanoti kunyange madzimai ekuZimbabwe achiwanikwa kunyika yavo vachiita zvechipfambi vanoti hazvisi zvitsva sezvo madzimai edzimwe nyika achiwanikwa munyika dzisiri dzavo vachita basa rimwe chete rechipfambi .
Muzvari Sally Kanyakanyaka avo vanorwira kodzero dzevanorarama nehurema vanoti zvinhu zvinofanirwa kushanduka munyika munyaya dzezvematongerwo enyika kuti zvehupfumi zvigadzikane izvo zvinozoita kuti madzimai awane zvinovapa pundutso muhupenyu kuti vararamise mhuri dzavo .
Muzvari Kanyakanyaka vanoti zvechipfambi zviri kuita madzimai aya zvinokonzera mamwe matambudziko akaita sekubata HIV zvinoisa hupenyu hwavo panjodzi .
Madzimai anoita zvechipfambi aya vanonyanya kuda kunofara nanamutyairi vemotokari dzinotakura zvinorema vanenge vakamirira kufambiswa kwemapepa avo emotokari kuti vapinde kana kubuda munyika .
Vanoti vanoshanda masikati pamwe nemanheru apo vanowana mari inodarika madhora makumi maviri pazuva .
Meya veguta reHarare , VaHerbert Gomba , vanoti kushomeka kwemvura muguta re Harare kwazosvika pasisina kunaka zvekuti vanhu vese vanofanirwa kuisa misoro pamwe chete kugadzirisa dambudziko iri .
VaGomba vayambira nhengo dzeparamende kuti dzimborega zvekutukana kwavanogara vachiita muparamende vashande pamwe chete kugadzirisa dambudziko remvura muHarare .
VaGomba vati nhengo dzeparamende dzinogona kugadzirisa zvinhu kana dzikabvumirana kuti hapana bhajeti rinofanirwa kutambirwa kana risina mari yekuvaka madhamu emvura kana mari yekuvakidzira aripo acho kuti abate mvura zhinji pane yaari kubata ikozvino .
VaGomba vanoti mukuedza kwavo kugadzirisa nyaya iyi , vari kuronga kuti vasheedze musangano mukuru pakati pehurumende , mainjiniya , nhengo dzeparamende neavo vese vangabatsira panyaya iyi , pamwe chete nemakurukota ehurumende kuti dambudziko iri rizeyewe zvakakwana uye kuti pawanikwe gwara nekuti vanhu veHarare vaita moyo murefu naizvozvo vanofanira
kubatsirwa nekubviswa kwedambudziko iri .
Vakawanda muHarare vanoti kisimusi yegore rino yange isina mufaro wakanyanya nekuda kwekusamira zvakanaka kwehupfumi munyika .
Asi kunyangwe zvakaoma , vamwe vanoti mufaro wavo uri mukurangarira kuzvarwa kwaJesu Kristu .
Vakawanda munyika vari kuchema chema nekushaikwa kana kushomeka kwezvinhu zvakaita semafuta ekufambisa dzimotokari , magetsi , mvura yekunwa , mabasa nezvimwe .
Studio 7 yatenderera mumigwagwa yeHarare ichinzwa kubva kuvanhu nezvezuva rekisimusi .
Amai Chenai Shiri vekuDzivarasekwa 2 vanoti kisimusi yegore rino yange yakaoma kudarika mamwe makore nekuti vange vasina kana huku zvayo ukuwo vari murima sezvo kusina magetsi .
Vanoti pfungwa dzavo dzatove mugore ra2020 kufunga kuti vachawanepi mari yekubhadhara kuchikoro chevana nokuti yakakwidzwa zvakanyanyisa .

Amai Charity Mubaiwa vekuWestgate vaudza Studio 7 kuti vaswera vakarara nokuti vakashanda zvakanyanyisa gore rino zvokuti nyama dzomuviri wavo dziri kurwadza .
Mukomana wechidiki Tinotenda Mhundwa anoti akazvarwa musi wekisimusi saka atsvaga huku nenyama yokuti apembere bavhadhe rake aine shamwari yake yepamoyo Tinashe Kadende .
Amai Nyarai Chikwiri Chabika vanobva kuBuhera vanoti vachatora huku pane dzavanotengesa kuti vabikire mhuri yavo nhasi kupembera kisimusi .
Studio 7 yawanawo mukana wokutaura naMufundisi Sam Dube vekuTabernacle of FaithChurch iyo iripasi peApostolic Faith Mission kuHarare West .
Mufundisi Dube avo vakurudzira vatendi kuti vasarasa hunhu pamhembero yekisimusi .
Vatiwo zuva ranhasi nderekupemberera munhu akasunungura mweya yevanhu vese kuti hupenyu hwavo huyendeke zvakanaka .
Mufundisi Dube vakurudzira zvakare vatendi kuti vasatsauka munzira yokutenda Jesu Kristu chero zvazvo nyika iri kuvava nemarwadzo .
Ichokwadi kuti kare haagare ari kare uye matakadya kare haanyaradze mwana .
Mumakore adarika , vanhu vaiburitsa maradio avo panze vachiridza nziyo dzakaita sedzaPaul Matavire , kusanganisa Dhindindi Full Time , asi nekushaikwa kwemagetsi izvi zvave zviroto .
Dare remakurukota nhasi rabuda nechisungo chekuti mauto nemapurisa vapihwe mukana wekutenga zvinhu nemutengo wakaderera muzvitoro zviri kumakamba avo .
Vamwe vanopikisa nevanoongorora nyaya dzezvematongerwo enyika vanoti zviri pachena kuti hurumende iri kutya kupidigurwa nemauto zvakaitwa vaive mutungamiri wenyika VaRobert Mugabe .
Gurukota rinoona rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko Amai Monica Mutsvangwa vanoti kubatsira mauto hakunei nekutya kuti vanogona kupanduka hurumende vachiti pane zvirongwa zvekubatsira vanhu vose munyika .
Asi mutevedzeri wemunyori anoona nezvekudyidzana nedzimwe nyika mubato reMDC Senator Douglas Mwonzora vanoti kuvhundika chati kwatara hunge uine katukwa nekudaro zviri pachena kuti hurumende iri kutya kupandukirwa nemauto .
VaMwonzora vati hurumende inofanira kubatsira vanhu vose vanoshupika munyika kwete vanodzivirira nyika chete .
Hurumende inoti yaumbawo homwe yekuti vashandi vayo vakwanise kukwereta mari nemutero uri pasi kune vanenge vachida kubatirwa mari .
Makundano eCastle Lager Premier Soccer League ambomiswa kumbopa mukana kuChibuku Super Cup .
Makundano emukombe weChibuku Super Cup aya akatanga neChishanu masikati apo chikwata cheHarare City chakarakasha Border Strikers 4 - 0 .
Chikwata cheHarare City ndicho chine mukombe uyu mushure mekurova Dynamos 2 - 0 mufainari yegore rapera .
Dynamos yacho iri kutarisira kudarika zvayakaita gore rapera nekutora mukombe uyu gore rino apo varikusangana neHow Mine muRufaro Stadium .
Mubati wehomwe wechikwata ichi VaWebster Marechera vanoti chinangwa chavo kubuda munharaunda yekutanga iyo vanoti mutambo neHow Mine wakaoma zvikuru .
VaMarechera vanoti varikutarisira kutora mari yekukunda iri mumukombe uyu kuitira kuti vazvirerutsire munyaya dzemari idzo dzanetsa zvikuru munyika .
Mukombe weChibuku Super Cup ndiwo wega sirivha yasara kuDynamos sezvo zveligi zvakaramba svondo rapera apo yakarohwa 2 - 1 neHighlanders .
Asi Bosso irimowo mumukombe uyu , neMakepekepe zvekare .
Dynamos inofanira kurova zvikwata zvikuru izvi kana ichida kutora mukombe uyu nezviuru makumi manomwe nemakumi mashanu emadhora .
Highlanders iri kusanganda ne Mutare City mu Babourfields Stadium apo Makepeke achadamburana neTsholotsho Pirates muNational Sports Stadium .
Anotaura akamirira maGreen Machine Joyce Kapota anoti varairidzi vavo vakagadzirira zvakakwana mitambo yeChibuku Super Cup .
Chikwata chiri kutungamira makwikwi ePSL , uyezve chiriicho chakatora mukombe weChibuku Super Cup muna 2014 , cheFC Platinum chirimumuMandava Stadium umo chirikutatsurana masimba neChapungu .
Ngezi Platinum Stars iyo yakavaka nhandare yakanaka zvikuru iyi yeBaobab Stadium umo irikubandana neHwange panguva imwecheteyo ZPC Kariba iine Bulawayo City muNyamhunga .
Triangle neChicken Inn ndidzo dzichavhara musangano muGibbo Stadium neSvondo .
Makundano eChibuku Super Cup arikutarisirwa kupera musi wa 5 Mbudzi .

Izvi zvinotevera kukundwa kwakaita chikwata chemaSables muAfrica Cup umo chakarohwa mitambo yavo yese mitatu ndokubuda zvekare mumakwikwi e2019 World Cup .
MaLady Cheetahs arikurwira mukombe wemuAfrica muPolice Grounds neTunisia , Uganda , Zambia , Senegal , South Africa neNamibia .

Vamwe vatsigiri veZanu PF kuManicaland vanoti havazi kufara nedanho riri kuda kutorwa rekuita kongiresi yechimbi chimbi iyo vanoti yakanangana nekusimudzirwa kwemudzimai wemutungamiri wenyika , Amai Grace Mugabe , kuti vaitwe mumwe wevatevedzeri vemutungamiri weZanu PF .
Mashoko aya anotevera chisungo chakaitwa nedunhu reZanu PF mukupera kwesvondo .
Asi dzimwe nhengo dzebato iri dzinoti Amai Mugabe havana kukodzera kuti vapihwe chinzvimbo chekuva mutevedzeri wemutungamiri webato , izvo zvinozoita kuti vaitwe mutevedzeri wemutungamiri wenyika .
Mumwe wevanhu ava , avo vanopikisa kukwiridzirwa kwaAmai Mugabe , ndiVaRueben Bote avo vanoti nyaya yekusarudza mudzimai kuti ave muPresidium haina kushata asi chakaipa inyaya yekuisa vanhu pazvinzvimbo zvisina kubva muvanhu .
Imwe nhengo yeZanu PF , uye vaimbove murwiri wehondo yerusununguko , VaIrwin Mbengo , vanoti zviri kuda kuitwa zviri kunze kwemutemo uye zvinofanirwa kurambwa zvachose .
Vanoti bumbiro remitemo yeZanu PF harifanirwi kungoshandurwa chero nguva apo vamwe vanhu vanenge vaine zvavanoda kuzadzikisa kana kubvisa vamwe pazvigaro .
Bumbiro reZanu PF rakashandurwa zvakare muna 2005 kuitira kuti mumwe wevatevedzeri vemutungamiri webato ange ari munhukadzi , izvo zvakapa kuti Amai Joice Mujuru vatore chigaro chemutevedzeri wemutungamiriri weZanu PF .
Bumbiro iri rakashandurwa zvakare muna 2014 rikapa masimba mutungamiri webato kuti asarudze vatevedzeri vake , kwete kuti vasarudzwe nevanhu pakongiresi .
Izvi zvakapa kuti Amai Mujuru vabviswe mushure mekupomerwa mhosva yekuda kubvisa VaMugabe pachigaro .
Mumwe mutsigiri weZanu PF kuManicaland , VaProsper Tendengu , vanoti vanoona hurongwa hwekuda kusimudzira Amai Mugabe huri hwekuda kufadza rimwe boka rinozivikanwa nekuti G40 iro vanonzi vanotsigira .
VaTendengu vanoti kongiresi iyi vanoiona senzira yekuda kudzinga vamwe mubato iri vavasingawirirani naAmai Mugabe .
Studio 7 haina kukwanisa kutaura nemunyori weZanu PF mudunhu reManicaland , VaKenneth Saruchera , pamusoro penyaya iyi kunyange hazvo pamusangano weSvondo vakatsigira pfungwa yekusimudzira Amai Mugabe .
Chikwata cheG40 chiri kukikiritsana nechimwe chinozivikanwa nekuti Lacoste icho chinonzi chinoda kuti mumwe wevatevedzeri vaVaMugabe , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , vaende panyanga kana VaMugabe vachinge vazosiya chigaro .
Gurukota rinoona nezvevashandi Amai Sekai Nzenza vanoti hurumende iri kugadzirisa nyaya dzekodzero dzevashandi kuburikidza nemisangano yeTripartite Negotiating Forum kana kuti TNF nekudaro hapana chikonzero chekuti sangano reInternational Labour Orgnanization ritumire chikwata chevaongorori .
Asi munyori mukuru musangano reZimbabwe Congress of Trade Unions VaJaphet Moyo vanoti kuvhunduka chati kwatara hunge uine katurike .
Chisungo chekutumira nhumwa chakabuda pamusangano weILO wakapera nemusi weChishanu chapera kuGeneva , Switerland .
Danho reZimbabwe iri riri kutarisirwa kukanganisazve kudyidzana kwayo nenyika dzakaita seAmerica nesangano reILO .
Mumashoko avo kumusangano uyu , munyori anoona nezvekudyidzana nedzimwe nyika muhurumende yeAmerica VaMike Pompeo vakashora zvikuru kwavanoti kumbunyikidzwa kwevashandi nehurumende yeZimbabwe .

Vateveri vechikwa ichi havana kubvira vaziva chinonzi mufaro kubvira musi uyo chikwata chavo chakasimuka kuenda kuma 2019 Africa Cup of Nations uko chakanonyadzisa nekudzoka nepoindi imwe chete uyezve chazvambaradzwa 4 - 0 neDemocratic Republic of Congo .
Izvi zvakateverwa nekutatarika kunotyisa apo maWarriors akasangana neSomalia mumakwikwi e 2022 World Cup uyo akakunda asi zvekutamburira nechikwata chisina mukurumbira ichi .
Ndokuzouya mutambo weChishanu svondo rapera apo Zimbabwe yakatadza kurova Botswana pamusha muNational Sports Stadium mumutambo uyo yaitarisirwa kwete kukunda chete asi kubuda nezvibodzwa zvakawandisa .
Asi vateveri vemaWarriors havana kurasa chikwata chavo zvekuti kwaive nechaunga kumutambo weBotswana wacho , vamwe vacho ndokuperekedza chikwata ichi kuZambia neChipiri izvo zviri kufadza mukuru weZimbabwe National Soccer Supporters Association VaChama Mushamaidze .
Zvibodzwa zviviri kubva kuna Khama Billiart zvakapa Zimbabwe kuti ikunde Zambia izvo zvakasimudza manyuku nyuka zvekare muvatsigiri vechikwata ichi .
Mutambo weZambia ndiwo waive wekupedzisira Antipas ari pabasa , asi chibvumirano chake neZimbabwe Football Association , Zifa , chichipera musi wa 31 Zvita .
Zimbabwe haina mumwe mutambo musi wa 31 Zvita usati wasvika .
Antipas audza Studio7 kuti zvava kuZifa kuti inoda kuti arambe ari pabasa here kana kuti kwete , uye iye akamirira kunzwa kuZifa kuti vataurirane remangwana ravo .
Muongorori wemutambo wenhabvu , VaFarai Kambamura , vanoti Zimbabwe yakadadisa kuZambia zvekuti vari kuona ichitora chimwe chezvinzvimbo zviviri yezvikwata zvichaenda kumafainari eAfcon kubva mugungano iri .
Pari zvino , Zimbabwe iri pachinhanho chechipiri nemapoinzi mana , mapoinzi maviri pasi peAlgeria iyo iri kutungamira makwikwi aya asi iine mapoinzi matatu pamusoro peBotswana uyezve mapoinzi mana pamusoro peZambia iyo yarohwa mitambo yese miviri yayatamba .
Imwe nhengo yeZimbabwe National Soccer Supporters Association , VaWonder Gombera , vanoti vari kufara zvikuru nezvaitwa nemaWarriors asi vachiwedzera ivo kuti vanotungamira nhabvu veZifa vanofanira kugadzirisa maitiro avo kuti zvinhu zvifambe kudarika pazviri ikozvino .
Maneja wechikwata ichi , VaWellington Mpandare , vanoti pamusoro pekubudirira kuenda kumafainari eAfrica Cup of Nations , vari kuda zvekare kunoita mashiripiti kumakundano eChan uyezve nekuenda ku 2022 World Cup .
Asi vaimbove mubati wepembe muPremier Soccer League , VaSam Hamandawana , vanoti chikwata chemaWarriors chave nevatambi vatsva vakati wandei zvekuti kwave kudiwa kutamba mitambo yehushamwari yakawanda kuti vatambi ava vajairane vakatarisana nemitambo inotevera .
Zimbabwe yabudirira kuenda kumafainari eAfrica Cup of Nations kanokwana kana , muna 2004 , 2006 , 2017 na 2019 asi panguva dzese idzi yanga ichingobuditswa munharaunda yekutanga .
Asi nzira ye 2021 Africa Cup of Nations yapfaviswa nemapoinzi matatu ayatora kuZambia .

Vakafanobata chigaro chemukuru wesangano re Survival Vendors Union of Zimbabwe , VaObey Mwariwangu , vanoti kunyange hazvo hurumende iri kuita zvakawanda mukurerutsa zvinhu yakanangana nechirwere che coronavirus , kune vanotengesera mumigwagwa hapana chinhu chati charerutswa , sezvo vasiri kukwanisa kupinda mumigwagwa , munove mavanogara nekushandira .

Nekuda kwekushanduka kwemamiriro ekunze kuri kuramba kuchiwedzera , Zimbabwe inofanirwa kukoshesa kugadzirwa kwemagetsi kuchishandiswa dzimwe nzira dzisiri dzagara dzichishandiswa .
Kurudziro iyi yabuda pamusangano weWater Sanitation Hygiene and Energy kana kuti WASHen , uyo watanga nhasi muBulawayo .
Mutevedzeri wegurukota remhando dzemoto , Amai Magna Mudyiwa , vati kuti nyika ive yasvika panyika dzinoverengwa sedziri pakati nepakati pekubudirira mugore ra2030 , inenge yave kushandisa magetsi anosvika11 500 mega watts .
Amai Mudyiwa vati sezvo pari zvino nyika ichikwanisa kugaya magetsi anosvika 2600 mega watts chete , zvinoreva kuti pane basa guru rinoda kuitwa kuti nyika iwane magetsi akakwana vakakurudzira vemaindasitiri pamwe neveruzhinji kuti vashandise dzimwe mhando dzemoto .
Mukuru weConfederation of Zimbabwe Industries mudunhu reMatabeleland , VaShepherd Chawira , vabvuma kuti nyika yakatarisana nedambudziko guru munyaya dzekushomeka kwemagetsi nemvura vachiti maindasitiri nemakambani akawanda ari kutatarika nekuda kwedambudziko iri .
Vatiwo pane makambani anoda kusima mari mune zvemagetsi , asi izvi zviri kukundikana nepamusana pehurumende inochinja - chinja mitemo pamadiro .
Imwe nyanzvi munyaya dzezvemvura nemhando dzemoto , Engineer Panashe Chakawa , vaudza Studio7 kuti kana kuchitariswa dzimwe mhando dzemoto , Zimbabwe inofanirwa kufungawo nezvemagetsi anobva kuzuva .
VaChakawa vati Zimbabwe inofanirwa kukoshesawo kuve nenzira dzechizvino - zvino dzekuchenesa mvura yemumaguta idzo vati hadzidhure , kuitira kuti mvura iyi painoraswa , isasvibisa nzizi .
Panyaya yedambudziko rekushaikwa kwemvura yakakwana mumaguta akasiyana - siyana munyika , kanzura weHarare , Amai Kudzai Kadzombe , vati hurumende inofanirwa kukoshesa kuvakwa kwemamwe madhamu .

vaongorora nyaya iyi .

Dhora remuZimbabwe riri kushaya simba zvakanyanyisa zvekuti range richitengeswa nemadhora anosvika makumi mana nematanhatu zvichienzaniswa nedhora rimwe chete rekuAmerica .
Izvi zvapa kuti mitengo yezvinhu iite chamurambamhuri sezvakaburitswawo neZimbabwe National Statistics Agency kana kuti Zimstats nezuro kuti mutengo wekukwira kwezvinhu kana kuti inflation wainge wasvika pazvikamu mazana mashanu nemakumi mana kubva muzana zvinonzi nedzimwe nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfumi munongedzo wekuti nyika yananga kumawere .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfumi vachidzidzisa paNelson Mandela Metropolitan University , Muzvinafundo Gift Mugano , vanoti kushaya simba kwedhora zviri kukonzerwa nezviri kuitika pamusika mutema .
Vaimbova gurukota rezvemari VaTendai Biti vanova zvekare mutevedzeri wemutungamiri webato reMDC vanoti havashamiswe nekushaya simba kwedhora remunyika uku .
Munyori mukuru musangano revashandi reZCTU , VaJaphet Moyo , vanoti kushaya simba kwedhora remunyika kuri kuomesera mushandi zvakanyanya .
Mutungamiri weEmployers Confederation of Zimbabwe , Doctor Israel Murefu , vanoti vashandirwi vane chido chekuti dai nyika yashandisa hayo rand rekuSouth Africa kana zvedhora reZimbabwe zvakona n'anga murapwa achida .
Asi gurukota rinoona nezvevashandi , Muzvinafundo Paul Mavima , vanoti hurumende iri kuyedza kugadzirisa dambudziko iri .
Asi Muzvinfundo Mugano vanoti komiti yakagadzirwa negurukota rezvehupfumi , Muzvinafundo Mthuli Ncube , haikwanise kugadzirisa dambudziko rekushaya simba kwedhora remunyika .
Aka ndekekutanga Zimstats ichitenderwa kuti iburitse kuti mutengo wezvinhu wasvika papi mushure mekumbomiswa kuita izvi muna Nyamavhuvhu gore rapera negurukota rezvemari VaNcube .
Mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , vakazivisa kare kuti hapana kudududza pakushandisa dhora remunyika sezvo chiri chidadiso chenyika .
Nhasi kwapera gore kubva mutungamiri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa vatora mhiko yekuti vatungamire nyika kwemakore mashanu mushure mesarudzo dzakaramba kutambirwa nebato guru rinopikisa reMDC Alliance richiti dzakabirirwa zvemhando yepamusoro .
Asi dare repamusoro soro reConstitutional Court rakati MDC yainge isina kuripa humbowo hwakati tsvikiti hwekuti rirase zvakabuda musarudzo .
Sangano rinorwira kodzero dzevanhu pasi rose reAmnesty International nhasi raburitsa mashoko kuvatori venhau richiti hurumende yaVaMnangagwa iri kutyora kodzero dzevanhu zvakanyanya .
Amnesty International inoti kunze kwekukundikana kugadzirisa nyaya dzezvehupfumi , hurumende iri kumbunyikidza vanu zvakanyanya nekuvarambidza kuratidzira ichingoshandisa nzira dzimwe chete nedzaishandiswa nevaive mutungamiri wenyika VaRobert Mugabe .
Sangano iri rinoti apo VaMnangagwa vopinda mune rimwe gore vachitungamira , uyu mukana wekuona kuti hurumende yavo yaremekedza kodzero dzevanhu .
Asi mutevedzeri wegurukota rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko VaEnergy Mutodi vati VaMnangagwa vakwanisa kuita zvinhu zvakawanda .
Sezvo tichitema tisina divi ratinorerekera , nhasi tabata mutauriri webato rinopikisa reMDC VaDaniel Fortune Molokela avo vati VaMnangagwa vakudikana zvine nhoroondo .
Vati chinopa kuti nyika iite seyakageza negoka munyama kutonga nedemo kwaVaMnangagwa .

Zimbabwe yakwanisa kubatana nezvimwe zvikwata gumi nechimweche zvichange zviri munharaunda yechipiri mushure mekunge Australia yazvambura Sri Lanka 99 - 24 ndokusiya Sri Lanka iri iyo iri pasi pasi mugungano rezvikwata zvina iri .
Sri Lanka haina kana poindi imwechete mushure mekurohwa neZimbabwe 79 - 49 , ndokutevera izvi nekurohwa zvekare 67 - 50 neNorthern Ireland uye zvaitika nhasi apo yadonhedzwa neAustralia .
Zimbabwe ichapinda mune rimwe gungano zvekare richange riine zvikwata zvitanhatu munzira yavo yekurwira mukombe wakakosha uyu , uyo uri mumaoko meAustralia pari zvino .

Sangano reZimbabwe Medical Association rinoti harisi kufara kuti makambani anobhadharwa nevarwere kuti agozovabhadharira mabhiri kana vachinge varwara , haasi kuvabhadhara zvinonzi nesangano iri zvave kukonzera kuti vanachiremba vazhinji vatadze kuita basa ravo zvakanaka .
Sangano reZimbabwe Medical Association , kana kuti Zima , rinoti makambani aya ane zvikwereti zvakawanda uye ave nenguva yakareba asiri kubhadhara vana chiremba kana vachinge varapa varwere vanenge vari pachirongwa chekubhadharirwa nemakambani aya kana kuti medical aid .
Munyori mukuru muZima .
VaSacrifice Chirisa , vaudza vatori venhau kuti pamakambani ese aya , kambani yePublic Service Medical Aid Society , kana kuti PSMAS , ndiyo ine chikwereti chakakurisa chemari inosvika mamiriyoni makumi matanhatu emadhora ekuAmerica kana mari yakaringana nemari iyi iri yema RTGS pachishandiswa huremu huri kushandiswa mumabhanga kana kuti interbank rate .
Hatina kukwanisa kutaura nemukuru - mukuru wePSMAS , Farai Muchena , sezvo nharembozha yavo yanga isingadairwe uye vekuhofisi kwavo vanga vachiti havamo muhofisi pasvika Studio7 pamahofisi ePSMAS .
VaChirisa vati izvi zvave kupa kuti mamwe madhokotera atadze kuita basa rawo zvakanaka .
Tsvagiridzo yaitwa neStudio7 yaratidza kuti vamwe vana chiremba vave kuramba kutambira ma medical aid vachida kubhadharwa nemusvo kana mari dzepamafoni .
Zvataurwa naVaChirisa zvatsinhirwa nemumwe dhokotera , VaShingirirai Meki , avo vati vanachiremba vazhinji vave kunhonga svosve nemuromo sezvo vachiti mari yavari kutambiriswawo nehurumende yakafanana nemutero wembwa .
Zvichakadai , gurukota rezvehutano , VaObediah Moyo vaudza Studio 7 parunhare kuti vachaongorora nyaya iyi vozoona sehurumende kuti nyaya iyi ingagdziriswe sei .
VaChirisa vati makambani aya haasi kubhadhara nenguva uye vati paanozobhadhara ari kubhadhara mari isina kukwana zvavati zvinotyora mutemo weHealth Services Act .
Zima yaratidzawo kushushikana zvikuru nevakuru vemakambani aya avo vainoti vari kurarama hupenyu hwepamusoro - soro vasingabhadhare mabhiri evarwere zvavati zvave kutoda kuti komisheni inorwisana nehuori yeZimbabwe Anti Corruption Commission , Zacc , iferefete makambani aya .
Vaimbove mukuru wePremier Service Medical Aid , VaCuthbert Dube , vakaferefetwa neZaac yaivepo muna 2014 mushure mekupomerwa mhosva yekushandisa mari zvisiri pamwero , asi vakawanikwa vasina mhosva .
VaDube , avo vakanga vari mukuru wekambani iyi kubva muna 1992 kusvika muna 2014 , vaitambiriswa mari inodarika mazana maviri nemakumi matatu ezviuru zvemadhora ekuAmerica pamwedzi , vachiisa muhomwe mamiriyoni matanhatu nemazana mazana ezviuru zvemadhora pagore .
VaDube vaipomerwawo kuzvipa mari yechikwete inosvika mazana masere ezviuru zvemadhora , pamwe nekushandisa mari yekambani iyi apo vaiita basa reZifa pavaive mutungamiri wesangano renhabvu iri .
Asi Zaac yakati pakanga pasina humbowo hwakati tsvikiti hwairoverera VaDube nemhosva .
Zima yakurudzirawo hurumende kuti ikurumidze kupasisa bhiri Medical Aid Societies Bill iro rinobata mashandiro emakambani aya .
Kunyangwe hazvo hurumende yakapa kurudziro yekuti mitengo yezvinhu zvakawanda zvinodyiwa nevanhu idzikiswe kusvika payaive musi wa25 kurume , izvi zvinenge zviri kukona n'anga murapwa achida .
Mitengo yezvinhu haisi kudzika .
Hatina kukwanisa kubata vamwe vakuru veConfederation of Zimbabwe Industries kana Zimabwe National Chamber of Commerce tinzwe divi ravo .
Asi gurukota rezvemaindustry Doctor Sekai Nzenza vaudza Studio 7 kuti vari kushushikana nekukwira kwemitengo yezvinhu vakati pamisangano yavakaita nevamwe vemabhizimisi vakatenderana kuti mitengo yezvinhu idzikiswe .
Vatenda havo kuti vemabhizimisi varik kuti vari kuremerwawo nezvinhu kunyanya mari yekunze yekutenga zvinhu .
Imwe nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfumi muzvinafundo Gift Mugano vanodzidzisa paNelson Mandela Metropolitan University vanoti zvekuda kutara mitengo yezvinhu hazvishande uye zvichatopa kuti zvinhu zvishaikwe muzvitoro .
Komisheni inorwisana nehuwori munyika , yeZimbabwe Anti - Corruption Commission , ZACC , inoti iri kutarisira kunge yave nemahofisi anoshanda mumatunhu matanhatu emunyika mukupera kwegore rino senzira yekuedza kurerutsa mashandiro ayo .
Mashoko aya , ayo ataurwa nemumwe wemakomishina uye vari mutauriri weZACC , VaJohn Makamure , anotevera nyunyuto yabuda muvanhu vanga vari pamusangano waitwa maMutare wekuzeya mashandiro akanaka ekomisheni iyi , kana kuti Draft National Anti - Corruption Strategy .
VaTakashinga Mashayahanya mumwe wevagari vemaMutare vange vari pamusangano uyu .
VaMashayahanya vanoti sangano reZACC rinosungirwa kuwanzira mimwe yemisangano yaro kumaruwa kune vanhu vakawanda uye nekune mamwe maguta , kwete kungorambira vari kuguta guru reHarare .
"""" Tinoziva kuti ZACC iri kuedza kuita basa rakanaka asi inofanirwa kuonekwa kuti yambosungawo vamwe vanhu vachipika here kwete kungoti kune ZACC pasina asungwa .
Tinoda kuti ZACC iwonekwe kwese kumisha , kumaruwa ichiita basa kuti vanambuya nevana vechikoro vazive nezvebasa rayo , kwete kuwandira mumaguta makuru chete . """"
Mumwe wevanga vari pamusangano , VaFarai Matebvu vanoti ZACC iri kuita basa rayo zvakanaka , asi kuti vanovimba kuti kumhan'arwa nekuferefetwa kwedzimhosva kuitwe kwaaawanda , kwete mumaguta makuru chete .
"""" Kumaruwa kunosungirwa kunge kuchisvikwawo nekuti kune nyaya dzehuwori dziri kuitwa ikoko vanhu vasingazivi kwekuenda , saka misangano yekuzivisa vagari zvekuita panenge paitwa huwori ikodzero yemunhu wose kuti ange aine zivo .
Misangano yavo veZACC ngaiparadzirwe kwakawanda munyika yose . """"
Asi VaMakamure vanoti itarisiro yavo kuti panopera gore rino ZACC inge yave nemamwe mahofisi mumatunhu anoti Mutare , Masvingo uye Marondera kuwedzera pane mamwe ari MUHarare , Bulawayo nekuGweru .
"""" Tinofanirwa kunge tavhura ma - offices edu kumaprovinces ose emuZimbabwe , gore rino tinovhura anokwanisa kuita six , asi izvezvi tine three aripo , Harare , Gweru neBulawayo , saka ZACC inenge yave mamwe maregions six muZimbabwe kuti vanhu vakwanise kuzouya kurepota nyaya dzehuwolri , kana corruption nekunzwa mamwe maprogram edu
atinoita ane chekuita necorruption , """" VaMakamure vanodaro .
VaMakamure vanoti chimwe chechiri kunonotsa kuvepo kwemahofisi aya ndechekushaikwa kwemari yakakwana uye zvishandisiro zvinosanganisira vashandi vakadzidzira mabasa sezvo vachida kubhadharwa zvakaringana nemabasa avo .
"""" Chatinoda kuti tiite ndechekuti mahofisi atiri kuzovhura aya munofanirwa kunge muine nayanzvi ma - officers arimo achikwanisa kupindura nekugadzirisa zvichemo zvekotapusheni ; tinenge tichida kuti chinangwa chekuvhura mahofisi aya chinge chichozadzikiswa , by 2021 tinofanirwa kunge tatove kuna - districts akawanda emunyika kujti tipedze huwori . """"
VaMakamure vanoti komisheni yavo iri kugadzirawo zviverengwa zvevanhu vasingaone zveBraille nevamwe vanoshandisa mutauro wemaoko , kana kuti sign language .
Musangano wanhasi wapindwa nevemapoka ehurumende akasiyanasiyana uye vemapoka anoshanda akazvimirira akaita seTransparency International Zimbabwe nemamwe .
Hurumende yazivisa kuti ichawedzera mari yemudyandigere yevakarwa hondo yerusunguko pamwe nekuvabhadharira mari kuzvipatara pamwe neparufu .
Hurumende inoti chinangwa chayo ndechekuona kuti vanhu vakarwira rusununguko rwenyika vagara zvakanaka munyika yavakasungura .
Izvi zviri mubhiri riri kuda kuvandudza mitemo inobata vaimbove varwiri verusununguko .
Munyori mubazi rezvekudzivirirwa kwenyika pamwe nevakarwa hondo yerusununguko , Ambassador Mark Grey Marongwe , vazivisa komiti yeparamende inoona nezvemukati nekudzivirirwa kwenyika kuti hurongwa uhwu huri mubhiri rekushandura mutemo weWar Veterans Act iro riri kunyorwa nebazi ravo .
VaMarongwe , avo vaonovewo munhu aive murwiri wehondo yerusunguko vachizivikanwa nerekuti Tichatonga , vati maWar Veterans ari kutambura uye anotarisirwa pasi neveruzhinji izvo zviri kupa kuti bazi ravo ritore matanho ekugadzirisa chimiro chevanhu ava kuitira kuti vakwanise kugarawo zvakanaka .
Vati hurumende iri kuronga kuwedzera mari yemudyandigere yemaWar Veterans kubva pamadhora mazana matatu negumi nemashanu emaRTGS - kusvika pamari inotambirwa nemusoja ane chinzvimbo chameja muchiuto .
Meja muchiuto anotambira mari iri pakati pemazana mashanu nemazana matanhatu emadhora zvichienderana nemakore aanawo ari pachinzvimbo ichi .
Vatiwo vari kuronga kuti maWar Vets avewo neMedical Aid kuti akwanise kurapwa kana achinge aburitsa kadhi rinoratidza kuti aive murwi wehondo yerusununguko .
Asi vati pari zvino vanhu ava vari kurapwa kusvika vapora kana vachinge vapinda muzvipatara zvehurumende .
VaMarongwe , avo vakamboshanda semumwe wevakuru vakuru vezvirongwa zveZBC , vaenderera mberi vachiti vanodawo kuti maWar Veterans achengetedzwe zvakanakwa kana achinge ashaya nekudaro vari kuronga neimwe kambani inoviga vanhu kuti pese panoshaya murwiri wehondo yehondo rerusunguko , achengetedzwa zvine chiremerera .
Vazivisawo kuti pane maWar Veterans ari pakati pemazana mashanu nemazana matanhatu anoshaya gore rega .
Vati pari zvino pane maWar Veterans zviuru makumi matatu nezvishanu munyika .
Vati vamwe vavo vakawanda munyika havana kunyoreswa uye chirongwa chekuita izvi chiri kuenderera mberi nechinangwa chekuti vese vanokodzera vawane mari yemudya ndigere pamwe nekubatsirwa kupinza vana zvikoro .
Vati bazi ravo richapinza basa maDistrict War Veterans Officers makumi matanhatu nematanhatu mumatunhu ese munyika kuti agadzirise nyaya dzavo mumatunhu ese munyika .
Dzimwe nhengo dzekomiti iyi dzakaita saAmai Angeline Chipato vati kunyange hazvo chiri chinhu chakanaka kuchetengedza maWar Veterans , zvakakoshawo kuti hurumende ione zvaingaite pamusoro pana chimbwido nana mujibha avo vavati vakaitawo basa guru .
Asi VaMarongwe vati mutemo uri kutosandurwa kuti vana chimbwido nana mujiba varemekedzewo pamwe nekupihwa mari dzemudyandigere sezviri kuitwa maWar Veterans .
Vanoongorora nyaya dzehupfumi vakazvimirira , VaMasimba Manyanya , vaudza Studio 7 kuti kunyange hazvo pasina chakaipa pakuchetenegedza varwi vehondo yerusununguko , vanoona sekuti danho iri riri kuda kutorwa richavhiringa hupfumi sezvakaitika muna 1997 .
Vati vanhu havafaniri kuve nemweya wekuda kungomora chete vasingatarisi kuti remangwana renyika richange rakamira sei .
Kuma 80s hurumende yakadzika mitemo yeWar Veterans Act ne War Victims Compensation Fund iyo inosungira kuti vese vakarwira hondo yerusununguko vapihwe mari yemudyandigere pamwe nekubatsirwa panyaya dzehutano nedzidzo .
Muna 1997 sangano rinomirira varwi ava , reZimbabwe Liberation War Veterans Association , rakamanikdza hurumende kuti vapihwe zviuru makumi mashanu zvemadhora pamunhu mumwe izvo zvakadonhedza dhora remunyika nekukanganisa hupfumi wenyika .
Asi VaMarongwe vati rwendo runo havasi kuda kuti hurumende itore danho rinokanganisa hupfumi nekuda kwemaWar Veterans vachiti vachaumbawo Trust ichange ichiita mabhizimisi anotsvaga mari yekubatsira maWar Veterans .
Dynamos yavaka chikwata chitsva yakatarisana nemakundano enhabvu emwaka uno .
Dembare yatenga Jimmy Tigere na William Manhondo kubva kuHarare City iine chinangwa chekutora mukombe weCastle Lager Premier Soccer League uyo yakapedzisira kutora muna 2014 .
Pamusoro pezvo , Dynamos yawirirana neFC Platinum kuti irambe iine mutambi , Cleopas Kapupurika , uyo yaive yapihwa neKugona Kunenge Kudada kwegore rimwechete iro rakapera musi wa 31 Zvita .
Dynamos yabvumirana zvekare nemutambi Christian Epoupa uyo aitarisirwa kubva kuchikwata ichi achinzi ari kuenda kuBidvest Wits yekuSouth Africa , asi ave kuramba ari kuDembare kwerimwe gore .
Munyori mukuru weDynamos , VaWebster Marechera , vanoti Dembare haina zvekare kurasikirwa nemutambi kana mumwechete panguva yezororo vachiti ivo manyepo kuti kaputeni wavo , Ocean Mushure , ari kubva kuchikwata ichi .
VaMarechera vanoti gakava ranga riripo pakati peDynamos nevatambi Tichaona Chipunza , Obey Mwerahari naPearce Makaha , avo vanga vachiramba kunyorerana chibvumirano nechikwata ichi kusvikira vatambidzwa mari yavo yemwaka wapera , ragadziriswa .
VaMarechera vanoti vakapa murairidzi wavo , Lloyd Mutasa , simba rekutsvaga vamwe vatambi vatsva vachiti ivo varipo chete kupa ruyamuro rwemari kana pane mutambi waanenge achida .
Mutungamiri weDembare uyu anoti hapana chavari kutarisira kubva kuna Mutasa kunze kwekutora mukombe we league , vachiti izvi zvikasaitika , vanotora matanho makukutu .
Dynamos ine nhoroondo yekudzinga dzinga varairidzi .
Dembare yakapedzisira kutora mukombe we league muna 2014 apo yairairidzwa naKalisto Pasuwa .
Vaive vatambi venhabvu vechikwata chine mukurumbira munyika cheCaps United vari kuBritain vari kuronga kuita mabiko makuru ekuunganidza mari yekushandisa mukusimudzira nhabvu yemunyika .
Vatambi ava vakaumba chikwata chavo cheCaps United Legends , icho chiri kutungamira hurongwa hwekutsvaga mari uhwu .

Bato reMDC raita mhemberero munhandare yeRufaro yekusvitsa makore makumi maviri kubva parakaumbwa muna Gunyana 1999 .
Asi mhemberero idzi dzisati dzatanga , mapurisa afumobata jongwe muromo ndokuvhara muzinda webato iri weMorgan Tsvangirai House uye abva azara mumigwagwa yose yeHarare kusanganisira uko kunhandare yeRufaro kuMbare kwange kuchiitirwa musangano uyu ,
Mutungamiri weMDC , VaNelson Chamisa , vati havana kufara nezvange zvaitwa nemapurisa zvekuvhara muzinda wavo .
Vachitaura kumhomho yevatsigiri vavo vanga vari muRufaro , Chamisa vati vanoda kuita hurukuro nemutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , asi vati vanoda kugovana njere , kwete masimba .
VaChamisa vatiwo nhaurirano dziri kuitwa pari zvino naVaMnangagwa nemamwe mapato anopikisa , kutungana kwembudzi .
Mutungamiri weMDC ataurawo nezvenhoroondo yebato rake .
VaChamisa vavimbisawo kuti bato ravo rechine hurongwa hwekuratidzira zviri pamutemo kunyange pari zvino vari kurambidzwa nemapurisa ayo ari kuti anotya kuti vanozopanywa zvinhu .
Asi danho iri riri kushorwa nevemapato anorwira kodzero dzevanhu munyika nekunze achiti kutyora bumbiro remitemo .

Vamwe vechidiki vamiswa pamberi pedare ramajisitireti muBulawayo nhasi mushure mekunge vasungwa pakupera kwesvondo munzvimbo dzakasiyana - siyana dzeguta vachiita zvemafaro zvakapfurikidza mwero .
Vechidiki ava vapinzwa mudare vari muzvikwata zvakasiyana siyana uye pasvika Studio 7 paTredgold Magistrates Court taona vamwe vane chitsamwa vakaungana pamahofisi evachuchisi apo vange vachiongororwa kuti vabva zera here kana kuti kwete .
Pasi pemutemo wemunyika munhu ari pasi pemakore gumi nemasere anenge achinzi apara mhosva anonzi aiswe mumaoko evabereki vake kana vamwe vanhu vanomuchengeta .
Vakafanobata chinzvimbo chemutauriri wemapurisa muBulawayo Inspector Abednico Ncube vakaudza rimwe bepanhau rehurumende reChronicle kuti mapurisa akasunga vechidiki vasvika zana nemakumi matatu nemumwe vane makore ari pakati pegumi nemana nemakumi maviri nemana nemusi weMugovera .
Inspector Ncube vakatiwo vechidiki ava vakawanikwa vaine zvimwiwa zvinodhaka zvakasiyana siyana pamwe nemapiritsi .
Vamwe vevechidiki ava vatanhatu vamiswa pamberi pedare vachipomerwa mhosva yekutyora chimwe chikamu chemutemo weCriminal Law Codification and Reform Act vachinzi vakawanikwa vachitamba zvine ruzha vakavhurwa radio yavo yavairidza zviri pamusorosoro vari muCentenary Park .

Nyaya yaVaNgarivhume yange iri mudare zvekare nhasi gweta ravo VaMoses Nkomo vachikumbira kuti vaburitswe mujeri reChikurubi Maximum Prison sezvo kuratidzira kwavanonzi vaironga musi wa 31 Chikunguru kwakadarika pasina kana mhirizhonga .
Dare iri nerepamuso akambormba kupa VaNgarivhume mukana wekubvisa mari yechibatiso asi VaNkomo vakumbira kuti vabviswe madhora zviuru zvishanu semari yechibatiso pamwe nekuti vagare kumba kwavo kuWaterfalls kwavakasungirwa uye kuti vaende kunozviratidza kamwechete pasvondo kumapurisa .
Asi muchuchusi wehurumende VaMichael Reza vapikisa kupiwa mukana wekubhadhara mari yechibatiso uku vachiti kunyangwe hazvo musi wa31 Chikunguru wakapfuura pane boka rakaumbwa rinonzi July 31 Movement ravanoti rinogona kuda kuramba richikurudzira kuti mutungamiriri wenyika VaEmmerson Mnangagwa vabviswe pachigaro .
VaNkomo vaudza vatori venhau kuti mutongo uchapihwa svondo rino .
Vatiwo zvisinei nemutongo wakapiwa nedare svondo rapera wekuti VaNgarivhume vawaniswe zvekudya pamwe nekushanyirwa vari kujeri reChikurubi , izvi hazvisi kuitwa vachiti vekujeri vakati vaNgarivhume ngavaite zvekudya zvekutenga pamadandemutande izvo vati zvinoda mari yakawanda .

Munyori anoona nezvegwara remusangano muboka revechidiki , VaGodfrey Tsenengamu , vanoti vamwe vevanhu vane mazita ataurwa pamusangano uyu inhengo dzebato ravo reZanu PF , uye vane zvigaro muhurumende nemubato .

VaGumbo vanoti havasi kuzoshayiswa hope nenyaya iyi , vachipomera vechidiki ava kuteerera nyaya dzemakuhwa .
Sangano rinomirira vatori venhau vechidiki , reYoung Journalists Association , rinoti riri kushushikana zvikuru nekwarinoti kushungurudzwa pamwe nekurohwa nemapurisa kwevatori venhau pavanenge vachiita basa ravo .

Munhende anoti mapurisa akaona Muchenje akatakura kamera yake vakatanga kumupomera mhosva yekutora mifananidzo , vachibva vangotanga kumuzvindikita nemboma .
Aka hakasi kekutanga kuti vatori venhau vasangane netsaona dzekurohwa nemapurisa , sezvo iye Munhende ari mumwe wevatori venhau vakarohwa nemapurisa vachiita basa ravo .

Sangano revadzidzisi vekumaruwa reAmalgamated Rural Teachers Union of Zimbabwe , kana kuti ARTUZ , rinoti nhengo dzaro zhinji hadzina kuenda kubasa nechikonzero chekuti hadzisi kukwanirwa nemari dzemihoro .
Nekune rumwe rutivi , sangano reProgressive Teachers Union of Zimbabwe , PTUZ , riri kukurudzira hurumende kuti ikasike kugadzirisa nhuna dzevashandi vayo .
Sangano reARTUZ raburitsa mashoko ekuti nhengo dzaro dzinodarika zvikamu makumi mapfumbamwe nezvina kubva muzana dzakundikana kuenda kumabasa nhasi sezvo mari yemihoro isiri kudzikwanira .
Sangano iri rati nezuro huwandu hwenhengo dzaro dzisina kuenda kubasa dzaidarika zvikamu makumi masere nezviviri nechidimbu kubva muzana .
Mashoko aya atsinhirwa nemutauriri wesangano iri , VaNation Mudzitirwa , avo vati havasi kufara nemari yakapihwa vashandi vehurumende kuti vabatsirikane nebazi rezvemari .
VaMudzitirwa vati vanoda kuti mari dzemihoro dzibhadharwe ari maRTGS akaringana nemari inenge iri pamusika wemabhanga , kana kuti interbank rate , kuitira kuti zvavanoda zvese zvikwane pamari yavo yemihoro .
Zvichakadai , mutungamiri wesangano reProgressive Teachers Union of Zimbabwe , kana kuti PTUZ , VaTakavafira Zhou , vati mari yaburitswa nehurumende kuti vashandi vayo vabatsirikane haina chairi kukwana .
Hurumende yakaburitsa mari inoita madhora mamiriyoni mazana matatu ema RTGS kuitira kuti vashandi vayo vabatsirikane zvichaita kuti mushandi wayo wepasi pasi awane mari inoita madhora mazana manomwe .
VaZhou vati hurumende inofanira kugadzirisa nyaya dzemihoro nekukasika kuitira kuti vashandi vayo varerukirwe nehupenyu .
Munyori mubazi rezvemari , VaGeorge Guvamatanga , vaudza Studio7 parunhare kuti hurumende ine chido chekubhadhara vashandi vayo mari dzemihorodzinovakwanira asi homwe yayo yakabooka .
VaGuvamatanga vati hurumende iri kushingirira kuti hupfumi hwenyika husimukire kuti igokwanisa kubhadhara vashandi mari inovakwanira .
VaGuvamatanga vaudzawo bepanhau reHerald kuti mari yekuti vashandi vayo vabatsirikane yasvika kuvashandi sezvo vachiti mari iyi yakaiswa kumabhanga evashandi nemusi weChipiri .
Ongororo yaitwa neStudio7 yaburitsa pachena kuti vamwe vashandi vemamwe mapazi ehurumende vanga vari kumabasa .
Tsvagiridzo iyi yaburitsa pachena kuti vashandi vehurumende vari mudhorobha vari kukwanisa kuenda kubasa sezvo vachikwira mabhazi ehurumende anoita dhora rimwe chete pamunhu .

Hurumende yeBotswana inoti ichaita musenga bere kune zvizvarwa zveZimbabwe izvo zviri muhupoteri munyika iyi kana zvikasasarudza kunyoresa kuti zvidzoserwe kumusha musi wa31 Zvita usati wapera .
Asi hurongwa hweBotswana uhwu hwuri kushoropodzwa nenyanzvi munyaya dzekodzero dzevanhu pamwe nevapoteri avo vanoti vakatiza mhirizhonga nekumbunyikidzwa munyika nenhengo dzebato rinotonga reZANU PF .
Mudzidzisi wemitemo paGaborone University College of Law and Professional Studies , VaCharles Kungwengwe , vanoti danho iri rinoratidza kuti hurumende yeBotswana hairemedzi zvisungo zvakaitwa nesangano remubatanidzwa wenyika dzepasi rose , reUnited Nations .
Sangano rinochengetedza kodzero dzevapoteri pasi rose reUnited Nations High Commissioner of Refugees rakasunga kuti hakuna nyika inofanirwa kumanikidza kudzosera vapoteri kwavakatiza kana paine kuratidza kuti hupenyu hwavo huri munjodzi nokuda kwezvematongerwo enyika kana chii zvacho .
Chisungo ichi chakaitwa musi wa23 Nyamavhuvhu 1977 chichitsigira chimwe chisungo che United Nations Convention chakaitwa muna 1951 .
Imwewo nyanzvi munyaya dzekodzero dzevapoteri uye vachidzidzisa mitemo paUniversity of Botswana , VaTakudzwa Matambo , vashoropodza danho reBotswana vachiti vapoteri ava vanogona kukwidza nyaya yavo kumatare edzimhosva vachipikisa zviri kuitwa neBotswana .
Mukokeri wesangano remubatanidzwa wemapato anorwira kodzero dzevashandi muBotswana , reBotswana Federation of Trade Unions , VaGadzani Mhotsa , vanoti hurumende yeBotswana yatora danho iri isana kutsanangurira veruzhinji kuti yakaongorora here mamiriro ezvinhu muZimbabwe kana kuti kwete .
Mutauriri wevari muhupoteri muBotswana , VaBhekimpilo Weza , vaudza Studio7 kuti hurumende yeBotswana haisi kuda kuteerera nhunha dzeavo vakatiza mhirizhonga yakaitika munyika mushure mesarudzo yemutungamiri wenyika yakadzokororwa muna 2008 .
Vapoteri vari muBotswana vazhinji vakatiza kuZimbabwe muna 2008 , vazhinji vavo vachiti vatsigiri veMDC vakatiza misha yavo mushure mekurayirwa hama dzavo mumhirizhonga yakaitika mugore iri .
Mukuru anoona nezvekuchengetedzwa kwevapoteri muhurumende yeBotswana , Amai Gloria Letlhage , vanoti Botswana iri kuita hurongwa uhu zviri pamutemo asi varamba kutsanangura kuti sei vachidaro .
Asi Botswana inoti mupoteri anenge asina kuzvipira kudzokera ega kumusha kwake panopera gore rino , anozoita zvekumakidzwa kudzoserwa kuZimbabwe .
Sangano rinomirira vanotenga nekutengesa kunze kwenyika , reInternational Cross - Border Traders Association , riri kukurudzira vari kushandisa miganhu kubuda munyika , zvikuru vari kubuda nekuBeitbridge , kuti vashandise mimwe miganhu isina kuwandirwa nevanhu .
Muganhu weZimbabwe neSouth Africa weBeitbridge Border Post unonzi uzere nevanhu vari kuda kuyambuka kudzokera kuSouth Africa mushure mezororo reKisimusi negoredzva , izvo zvinonzi zvakonzera kuti paite mitsetse yakareba yevanhu nedzimotokari .
Mutungamiri wesangano reInternational Cross - Border Traders Association , VaDenis Juru , vanoti sesangano vari kukurudzira vanhu vari kubuda munyika kuti vashandise mimwe miganhu yakaita se Plumtree Border Post , vopinda nemuBotswana kuti vakwanise kupinda muSouth Africa zviri nyore .
VaJuru vanoti izvi zvinogona kuonekwa sekunge zvinodhura asi zvinorerukira vanhu sezvo vasingazopedzi mazuva vari paBeitbridge vakamirira kubatsirwa .
Vanoti vanofunga kuti huwandu hwevanhu uhwu hunogona kunge huri kukonzerwa nekusavepo kwemishina inokwanisa kufambisa basa nekukasika , kanawo kuti divi remuSouth Africa iro vanoti rinotarisa zvakawanda kwazvo risati rabvumidza munhu kupinda MUNYIKA IYI .
ZIMRA yakazivisa kuti yaizowedzera huwandu hwevashandi vayo pamuganhu weBeitbridge panguva yezororo richangibva kupera iri .
Studio 7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa divi reZIMRA kanawo vedivi reSouth Africa panyaya yekuwanda kwevanhu iyi .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzezvirwere zvepfungwa dzinoti huwandu hwevanhu vanorwara nepfungwa huri kuramba huchikura munyika .
Mukuru weZimbabwe National Association for Mental Health , VaIgnatius Murambidzi vanoti kuoma kwehupenyu nekushandiswa kwezvinodhaka zvakanyanya ndezvimwe zvezviri kukonzera kukwira kwehuwandu hwevanhu vane chirwere ichi .
VaMurambidzi vakurudzira hurumende kuti igadzirise mamiriro ehupfumi hwenyika kuderedza dambudziko rezvirwere zvepfungwa .
VaMurambidzi vachema - chemawo nekushomeka kwana chiremba vane hunyanzvi hwekurapa chirwere ichi .
Mumwe wevanachiremba vane hunyanzvi mukurapa chirwere ichi , VaNemache Mavedzenge vatsigirawo vakati kutambura kuri kuita vanhu munyika nekushandisa zvinodhaka zvakanyanya kuri kukwidza huwandu hwevarwere vepfungwa .
VaMavedzenge vatiwo mishonga yakawanda inoshandiswa nevane dambudziko rechirwere chepfungwa inotengwa kunze kwenyika uye haiwanikwi zvakanyanya kuzvipatara zvehurumende kwainofanirwa kuwanikwa nemitengo yakadzikira izvi zvinowedzera kukura kwedambudziko iri .
VaMavedzenge vanotiwo zvimwe zvizviratidzo zvechirwere ichi kuchinja kwemaitiro emunhu achiita zvisingatarisirwi pamwe nekunzwa manzwi asipo .
Studio 7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa kubazi rezvehutano kuti vanhu vanorwara nepfungwa munyika vakawanda zvakadii .
Asiwo vamwe vevakuru vemachechi vataurwa navo neStudio 7 vatsinhira kuti kushaikwa kwemabasa kuri kukonzera kunetsekana kweveruzhinji izvo zvinozoita kuti vafunge zvakanyanya kuti vobatanidza sei hupenyu .
Zimbabwe ine zvipatara zvina zvinorapa varwere vepfungwa zvinoti Harare Psychiatric Hospital , Parirenyatwa Annexe , Ingutsheni , neNgomahuru .
Sangano reWorld Health Organization gore rapera rakati vanhu vanosvika miriyoni nezviuru mazana matatu muZimbabwe vane chirwere chepfungwa .
Mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , vari kutarisirwa kusangana mumazuva mashoma anotevera nechikwata chichaongorora huori huri kupomerwa vamwe vakuru mubato reZanu - PF nevechidiki vebato iri veYouth League .
Asi nyaya iyi yakonzera mutauro munyika vamwe vachiti iri ibasa rinofanira kuitwa neZimbabwe Anti Corruption Commission kana kuti ZACC .
Asi kunyangwe havo vachitenda kuti nyoka huru haizvirume , munyori anoona nezvemutemo mubato reZanu - PF , VaPaul Munyaradzi Mangwana , vanoti vanopikisa kusanganisira veMDC vari kugunun'una nenyaya iyi sezvo vasingafanire kupindira kana dzemudanga dzotungana .
Vakapomerwa mhosva dzehuori vanosanganisira vaimbova makurukota , vanosanganisira munyori wezvemabasa eZanu PF , VaObert Mpofu , vakadzingwa basa segurukota rezvekushanyirwa kwenyika , Amai Priscah Mupfumira ; gavhuna webhanga guru renyika , VaJohn Mangudya ; muzvinabhizinesi anodyidzana neZanu PF , VaWicknel Chivayo ,
VaMlungisi Moyo , Muzvare Elizabeth Mutsvangwa , Muzvare Henrietta Rushywa , VaNevile Mutsvangwa , Va Tongayi Muzenda , VaLipson Mhonda , Dr . Shar naVaTafadzwa Musarara veGrain Millers Association of Zimbabwe .
Nhengo dzekomisheni iyi dzichaongorora vanhu ava dzinosanganisira VaWilliam Mutomba ( Manicaland ) , Amai Sheilla Mabasa ( Mashonaland West ) , VaMax Zvidzai ( Midlands ) , VaTshinga Dube ( Bulawayo ) , nevamwe .
Ko ivo vechidiki veZanu - PF vakarova bembera kuti mubato mapindwa naPongwe vari kutenderana here nedanho rekuumba komisheni sezvo pavaitaura vaiti vane chivimbo neZACC ?
Vanoona nezvekurongwa kwemabasa muZanu - PF Youth League , VaGodfrey Tsenengamu , vanoti vari kufara nedanho rePolitiburo yebato ravo rekudoma komisheni iyi .
Vanoongorora kufambiswa kwemabasa musangano reAnti Corruption Trust of Southern Africa , VaAlois Chaumba , vanoti ZACC ndiyo inofanira kunge ichiongorora nhengo dzeZanu - PF idzi .
Vachipawo pfungwa dzavo , nhengo yeMDC inomirira Kambuzuma vari nhengo yeAfrican Parliamentarians Against Corruption , VaWillas Madzimure , vanoti mitemo munyika yekurwisa huori iripo asi haisi kutevedzwa nemazvo .
Asi VaTsenengamu vanoti VaMnangagwa vari kuzadzikisa zvido zvevechidiki nezvavakavimbisa munguva yesarudzo pakurwisa huori .
Asi VaMadzimure vanoti muromo hauzarirwe nerwizi vachiti hapana zvinzhinji zviri kuitwa kusunga vanoita zvehuori .
Zvichakadaro , VaMnangagwa ndivo vange vari munyarikani pahurongwa hwekuyeuchidza vanhu nezvekurwisa huori hwange hwakarongwa ne ZACC neNational Prosecuting Authority .
Hurongwa hwekudzidzisa vanhu nezvehuori uhu huri kutarisirwa kuitwa kwemwedzi gumi nemishanu .
VaMnangagwa vatiwo zvirango zvakatemerwa nyika zvinopawo kuti munyika muite huori sezvo zvimwe zvinhu zvinenge zvoshaika zvopa makoronyera mukana wekuita zvechioko muhomwe .
Panyaya dzehuori pasi rose , sangano reTrasparency International rinoti nyika iri pachidanho chezana nemakumi matanhatu panyika zana nemakumi masere dzakaongororwa .
Musangano wechitatu wekudyidzana pakati peZimbabwe neSouth Africa weBi - National Commission wapera nhasi muHarare , mutungamiriri weSouth Africa VaCyril Ramaphosa , vachiti nyika yavo yakazvipira kubatsira Zimbabwe panyaya yekumutsiridza hupfumi hwayo pamwe nekuti zvirango zvayakatemerwa zvibviswe .
Kunyangwe hazvo South Africa ichiti yakazvipira kubatsira Zimbabwe , zvabuda pachena kuti nyika iyi haisi kuzopa Zimbabwe mari yechikwereti yairi kutsvaga inodarika bhiriyoni imwe chete .
Zimbabwe yakatanga kukumbira mari iyi muna Zvita gore rapera .
South Africa kubva nguva iyi yange ichingori haina mari yakadai .
VaRamaphosa vati nyika mbiri idzi dzatenderana kuvandudza hukama munyaya dzekutengeserana , nyaya dzemari nezvimwe uya vaudza makurukota avo kuti afambise mberi basa rekuona kuti zvirongwa makumi mana nezvishanu zvavakasainirana mukati memakore matatu apfuura zvatevedzwa .
Semuenzaniso vatiwo vanoda kuti nyaya yeOne Stop Border Post paBeitbridge ichigadziriswa nechimbi chimbi vachiti kana zvikagadziriswa zvinorerutsa kufamba kwevanhu nezvinhu pakati penyika mbiri idzi .
Vati vanoda kuona zvirango zvehupfumi zvakatemerwa Zimbabwe nenyika dzekumadokero zvichibviswa vachiti zvinokanganisa hupfumi hweZimbabwe uye zviri kuomesera veruzhinji .
Vati pakutanga chaipo , Zimbabwe yainge isingakodzeri kutemerwa zvirango zvehupfumi nekudaro South Africa ichagara ichitaura kuti zvirango izvi zvibviswe kuti Zimbabwe ikwanise kuwana mari nerubatsiro sezvinongoitawo dzimwe nyika .
Mutungamiriri weZimbabwe , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , vatenda VaRamaphosa neSouth Africa nekutsigira Zimbabwe panguva yakaoma kwezvinhu vachiti izvi ndizvo zvinoita shamwari yepedyo .
Vatiwo Zimbabwe iri kuedza napose painogona napo kugadzirisa hupfumi hwayo , kukwezva vekunze pamwe nekugadzirisa mitemo yavo kuti inoenderane nebumbiro remutemo .
Zimbabwe neSouth Africa nhasi dzasainirana chibvumirano chekudyidzana panyaya dzezvekurima pamwe nekutambira gwaro pamusoro pekuti zvimwe zvibvumirano makumi mana nezvishanu zvakasainwa munguva yapfuura zviri kufamba sei .
VaMnangagwa vati zvirango zvehupfumi zviri kuvhiringa hupfumi hwenyika asi hurumende iri kushandisa zviwanikwa zvirimunyika kugadzirisa hupfumi apo iri kugadzirisa hukama hwayo nenyika dzepasi rese .
Nhengo yebhodhi yesangano rePlatform for Youth Development , VaOwen Dhliwayo , vaudza Studio 7 kuti zviri kuitwa neSouth Africa pakubatsira Zimbabwe zvakanaka chose .
Nyanzvi munyaya dzehupfumi vachishanda vakazvimirira , VaJames Johwa , vaudza Studio 7 kuti South Africa iri kubatsira Zimbabwe semuvakidzani uyewo nekuti kunaka kwehupfumi hweZimbabwe kunoita kuti zvizvarwa zvemuno zviri munyika iyi zvidzoke kumusha .
Asi vati kunze kweSouth Africa , Zimbabwe inoramba ichida rubatsiro kubva kunyika dzepasi rese nemasangano akaita seInternational Monetary Fund neWorld Bank .
Mukuru weMedia Centre , VaEnerst Mudzengi , vaudza Studio 7 kuti havabvumirani naVaRamaphosa pazvirango zvehupfumi zvakatemerwa Zimbabwe vachiti VaRamaphosa vanofanira kutanga vanzwa kubva kuvanhu vese vemuZimbabwe kwete kutaura vanzwa divi rimwe chete .
Zimbabwe neSouth Africa dzave nenguva yekaraeba dzichidyidzana uye dzakakwidziridza hukama hwadzo kuenda pachinhanho chepamusoro cheBi - National Commission muna 2015 .
Nhasi kuNational Heroes Acre , Zimbabwe inocherechedza zuva remagamba , vanhu vachipiwa mukana wekurangarira nekukudza avo vakazvipira kusunungura nyika uye neavo vakaishandira nemoyo wose .
Dangandira regore rinoti ndi ' Lest We Forget , ' kukurudzira vanhu kuti vasakanganwa zvakaitwa nemagamba .
Mangwana kuNational Sports Stadium , pasi pedangandira rinoti ' ZDF : Guaranteeing Peace and Security for National Development ' , nyika ichapemberera zuva remauto .
Nyanzvi mune zvematongerwo enyika , VaTapiwa Kapurura , vanoti kunyange hazvo bato reZanu - PF , pamwe chete nehurumende , rakasvibisa hugamba uye vachituma mauto kunetsana nevanhu pachinhambo chekuvabatsira , mazuva maviri aya mazuva anokosha zvikuru .
Chikwata cheDynamos chawana mukana wekuenda pamusoro pemakundano eCastle Lager Premier Soccer League kekutanga kubvira makundano emwaka uno atanga .
Chikwata ichi chiri kungoda kurova Caps United mumutambo unodaidzwa kunzi Harare Derby muRufaro Stadium neSvondo kuti chiende panhongonya pemakundano aya nepoindi imwe chete vachisvetuka Chicken Inn ne FC Platinum idzo dzine mapoinzi makumi mashanu nerimwechete .
Pari zvino , Dynamos ine mapoinzi makumi mana nemapfumbamwe zvekuti ikaita mangange inoramba iri pachinhanho chechitatu chairi pasi pemaGame Cocks neKugona Kunenge Kudada nepoinzi imwechete .
MaGame Cocks neKugona Kunenge Kudada havana mitambo svondo rino sezvo vePremier Soccer League vari kupa nguva ino kuzvikwata zvine mitambo yeligi yakasaririra neizvo zviri kutamba mitambo yepasi pasi muChibuku Super Cup .
Pakapedzisira kusangana Dembare nemaGreen Machine masvondo matatu apfuura Makepekepe akazvambaradzwa 2 - 0 asi mumwe muteveri mukuru wechikwata ichi , VaPeter Mugwagwa , avo vanobva mumusha weRimuka muKadoma vanoti ikozvino rave janha ravo
Asi Dynamos yacho haisi yekudherera sezvo isati yarohwa pamitambo yayo minomwe yapera yakateverana .
Kunyange hazvo vakaita mangange neHighlanders svondo rapera , sachigaro wevatsigiri vechikwata ichi muHarare , VaChristopher Mandizha , vanoti hapana chiri kuvatadzisa kutora mukombe weligi mwaka uno .
Zvikwata izvi zviri kupinda zvisina vamwe vatambi varambidzwa kutamba mutambo uyu nePremier Soccer League nemhaka yemakadhi avo awandisa .
Caps United ichange isina Valentine Musarurwa panguva iyo Dynamos ichange isina Lincoln Zvasiya na Tichaona Chipunza .
Murairidzi weDynamos , Lloyd Mutasa , azivisa zvekare kuti haasi kutambisa Christian Epoupa uyo ane nyaya iri kunetsa yekadhi raakapihwa svondo rapera kunyange hazvo veZifa vamupa mukana wekumushandisa .
Mutasa ari kukurudzira vatsigiri vechikwata chake kuti vauye muhuwandu hwavo kuzobatsira chikwata chavo kukunda .
Zvakamira zvakadai , vePremier Soccer League varonga zvekare mimwe mitambo miviri svondo rino , kwete yeleague asi yeChibuku Super Cup .
Mitambo iyi iriko yese mangwana , uyezve munhandare imwe chete yeMandava Stadium , kuchitanga mutambo pakati peHwange neYadah uyo uchazoteverwa neuyo uchasangana Tsholotsho Pirates neBantu Rovers .
Zvichakadaro , akundano eEnglish Premiership ari kupinda munharaunda yechishanu chikwata chiri pamusoro che Manchester United chiri pamusha neEverton
MaRed Devils anofanira kusunga dzisimbe mumutambo uyu kuti vatore mapoinzi ese matatu nekuti kusaita izvi , kukasangana nekukunda kweMancheter City kuWatford vanobviswa pamusoro soro pavari apa .

Chikwata chenhabvu chemadzimai chemaMighty Warriors chabuda mumakwikwi eAfrica Cup of Nations yemadzimai mushure mekukundwa nechikwata cheZambia 2 - 1 kunhandare yeRufaro muHarare pamutambo wema qualifier .
Nyanzvi yezvemitambo VaMuziwethu Hadebe vanoti chikwata cheMighty Warriors hachina kuwana nguva yakanaka yekugadzirira mutambo uyu , uye kuzorora , mushure mekunge chaenda kuZambia nebhazi pakati pesvondo kumutambo wekutanga uyo chakakunda 1 - 0 .
VaHadebe vanoti chikwata cheZambia chakapinda munyika nendege panguva iyo Zimbabwe yakanga ichidzoka munyika nebhazi zvakare .
Zvikwata zviviri izvi zvanga zvaita mangange 2 - 2 , asi sezvo Zambia yakwanisa kunwisa zvibodzwa zviviri iri kunze , ukuwo Zimbabwe ikangonwisa chibodzwa chimwechete kuLusaka .
Mune mimwe mitambo yatambwawo munyika , Bulawayo Chiefs yarova Highlanders 1 - 0 , kuchitiwo Dynamos yazokwanisawo kuwana mapoinzi matatu mushure mekurova Mutare City 1 - 0 mumutambo watambirwa kwaRusape .
Yadah Stars yarova Chapungu 3 - 0 , kuchitiwo Shabanie Mine neBlack Rhinos dzaitawo mangange 2 - 2 .
Chimwe chizvarwa cheZimbabwe chinogara muSouth Africa , chakatanga chikoro chekudzidzisa vechidiki mutambo wenhabvu .
Cavin Muodzi anoti akatanga chikoro ichi achishandisa mari yake yaanotambira pamwedzi kubasa kwake .
Muodzi , uyo akatanga Harvest Soccer Academy muCape Town mugore ra2016 , ane makore makumi maviri nemana ekuzvarwa .
Anoshanda muhotera achipa vanhu chikafu .
Mari yaanotambira , pamwe neyemubhasera yaanopihwa , ndiyo yaakashandiswa mukuumba Harvest Soccer Academy .
Muodzi anoti ane vechidiki makumi mana nevatatu , uye chikoro chake chine zvikwata zvemazera zvitatu ; chokutanga chine vana vane makore anotangira pagumi nemaviri , chechipiri chine vana vane makore gumi nemana , uye chechitatu chine vatambi vane makore gumi nematanhatuzvicikwira .
Muodzi anoti chinangwa cheHarvest Academy ndechekusimudzira nhabvu yevechidiki , kuderedza misikanzwa , uye kudzidzisa vechidiki kuremekedza vanhu vakuru .
Muodzi anoti pane matambudziko akawanda akatarisana nechikoro che Harvest Academy , ayo anosanganisira kushaikwa kwezvekushandisa .
Muodzi , uyo anotambawo nhabvu , anodzidziswa nechimwewo chizvarwa cheZimbabwe chinotamba nhabvu uyewo chine ruziwo rwakadzama munyaya dzekudzidzisa nhabvu , Hilton Masunda .
Masunda anoti Harvest Academy izano rakabva kusvondo yavanopinda naMuodzi , yeNew Beginnings International Harvest Church , iyo inotungamirwa nechizvarwa cheZimbabwe , Pastor Irene Mapininga .
Masunda , uyo anodzidzisa vana vane makore ari pasi pegumi nemaviri pachikoro cheHarvest Academy , murairidziwo zvakare wenhabvu pachikoro cheSt Joseph's Marist College makare muCape Town .
Mumwe ari kudzidziswa nhabvu pa Harvest Academy , Ricky Bongani Majimbo , anoti ari kudzidziswa zvinhu zvakawanda pachikoro ichi .
Mumwe wechidiki , Tinotenda Zvinounye , anoti matambiro ake bhora ashanduka , nekuda kweruzivo rwaari kuwana pa Harvest Academy .
Kunyange hazvo Muodzi achisangana nezvipingaidzo mushuviro yake , anoti izvi hazvisi kuzofa zvakaodza moyo wake .
Hurumende yeZimbabwe inonzi haisi kukoshesa varapi vechivanhu pamwe nemishonga yavo sezvo isiri kupa rutsigiro rwakasimba kubazi kuvarapi kunyange hazvo paine humbowo hunoratidza kuti zvikamu masere kubva muzana zvevanhu vemuZimbabwe zvinoenda kun'anga kana kushandisa mushonga yechivanhu pane dzimwe nguva .
Ongororo yakaitwa nesangano reWorld Health Organisation yakaratidzawo kuti zvikamu makumi masere kubva muzana zvevanhu vane hutachiwana hweHIV / AIDS pamwe nezvikamu makumi mashanu nezviviri zvemadzimai akazvitakura vanoshandisawo mishonga yechivanhu .
Vachipa humbowo nemaererano nemabasa ari kuitwa nehurumende kusimudzira mabasa evarapi vemuno pamwe nemishonga yavo , munyori mukuru mubazi rezvehutano , Doctor Gerald Gwinji , vaudza komiti yeparamende inoona nezvehutano kuti kunyange hazvo vanhu vakawanda vachishandisa mishonga iyi , hurumende hasi kuvapa mari yavanoda kusimudzira kushandiswa kwemishona iyi .
Doctor Gwinji vati bazi ravo rine chikamu chinoona nezvemishonga iyi asi chikamu ichi hachiwani mari yachinoda .
Semuenzaniso , Doctor Gwinji vati gore rega rega , chikamu ichi chinoda zviuru mazana matanhatu zvemadhora nechidumbu asi chinowanzo pihwa churu chemadhora chete izvo zvinoita kuti chitadze kuita basa racho .
Vanoti kunze kwekushaya mari vane zvakawanda zvavari kuita zvekuona kuti mabasa evarapi vemuno pamwe nemishonga yavo yasimudzirwa .
Vati mutemo we Traditional Medical Practitioners Act 11 , Regulations on Complementary and the Traditional Medicine policy ndezvimwe zvavakaitwa kusimudzira mabasa evarapi vemuno .
Doctor Gwinji vati kunyange hazvo paine varapi vanodarika churu vakanyoreswa neTraditional Medical Practitioners Council , vanoziva kuti munyika mune n'anga nevarapi vakawanda kudarika apa uye mishonga yechivanhu iri kutengeswa pese pese kunyange munzvimbo dzisina kunyoreswa .
Vati zvingave zvakanaka chose kana varapi vese vakadzidziswa kubata mishonga yavo zvakanaka zvinoita kuti vanhu vasakanganiswa nemishonga iyi sezvinoitika pane dzimwe nguva .
Vati Zimbabwe inogona kudzidza zvakawanda kubva kune dzimwe nyika zvikuru sei kunyika dzakaita seIndia neChina idzo dzave kushandisa mishonga yechivanhu zvakanyanya .
Munyori anoona nezvedzidzo musangano reZimbabwe National Traditional Healers Association , VaPrince Mutandi Sibanda , vaudza Studio 7 kuti kunyange hazvo vaine ruzivo rwekusimudzira mushonga yechivanhu , havasi kuwana rutsigirwo rwemari kuti vaite izvi .
VaSibanda vati ZINATHA ine nhengo dzakawanda chose zvekuti hazvivanetsi kugadzira mishonga yechivanhu nekubatsira vanhu vese munyika .
Muzvare Juliet Chirenje avo vari kudzidzira zvekurapa nemishonga yechivanhu pachikoro cheZINATHA vaudza Studio 7 kuti hurumende inofanira kuisa mari parutivi yekutsigira vanoshandisa mishonga yechivanhu .
Doctor Gwinji vati pari zvino pave nemasangano gumi nematatu anomiriria varapi vemuno akanyoreswa zviri pamutemo uyewo kune makirinika emishonga yemuno gumi nemana .
Asi vati mishonga iyi yave kutengeswa pese pese , mumigwagwa nedzimwe nzvimbo zvekuti bazi ravo rinoda kuti itengeswe zviri pamutemo pachitevedzwa hurongwa hweMedicines Control Authority of Zimbabwe pamwe ne Medical Research Council of Zimbabwe .
Vaimbove mutungamiriri weSouth Africa , VaThabo Mbeki vange vachishanya mu Zimbabwe uko vakasangana nevatungamiriri vemapato ezve matongerwo enyika , kusanganisa mutungamiri wenyika , VaEmmerson Mnangagwa , nemutungamiriri weMDC , VaNelson Chamisa nevamwe .
VaMbeki varikuedza kuuyisa mapato aya pamwe chete nemamwe masangano kuti vagare pasi vaite hurukuro pamusoro pemamiriro akaita zvinhu munyika , izvo zvinonzi zvave kunyanya kukanganisa South Africa .
VaMbeki vakaitavo musangano nevemakereke .
Munyori weZimbabwe Council of Churches , Doctor Kenneth Mtata , vaudza Studio 7 kuti parizvino VaMbeki varikuedza kukurudzira kuti paitwe nhaurirano munyika , kwete kuti ndivo mutongi gava .
Mapurisa ekuMacheke asunga nhengo pfumbamwe dzesangano re Amalgamated Rural Teachers Union of Zimbabwe , ARTUZ , apo dzange dzichifora dzakananga kuHarare .

Vasungwa ava vanosanganisira mutungamiri wesangano iri , Va Obert Masaraure .
Mutevedzeri wemutungamiri weARTUZ , Amai Gaudencia Mandiopera , vanoti mushure mekutorwa nemapurisa , vamwe vavo vazondeswa kukamba yemapurisa kuMarondera .
Studio7 haina kukwanisa kunzwa divi remapurisa , sezvo mutauriri wemapurisa , Amai Charity Charamba , vanga vasingadaire nhare mbozha yavo .

Varairidzi ava vakatanga rwendo rwavo kwaMutare musi wa 9 Zvita vaine chinangwa chekuratidza hurumende kuti havasi kufara nemabatirwo avari kuitwa nehurumende yaVaEmmerson Mnangagwa .
Kufora uku kunonzi Salary Caravan , uye ARTUZ inoti ichaenderera mberi nekufamba netsoka kudzamara vapedza rwendo rwavo , uye kusvitsa nhuna dzavo kugurukota rezvemari , VaMthuli Ncube .

Mumwe wevanhu anga ari mutsetse , VaRobert Ganyani , vanoti vasvikonzwa kuti vanhu vaviri varasikirwa nehupenyu vakamira mumutsetse .
Vanhu vanga vachida kurapwa vaswera vari mumutsetse murefu pachipatara cheParirenyatwa muHarare asi pasina chavabatsirwa nacho mukuvira kwezuva .
Sezvo vana chiremba nana mukoti vasiri kuenda kubasa vachiti havana mari dzekufambisa dzinovakwanira , kurapwa pachipatara ichi kuri kunetsa izvo zvava kukonzera kuti vamwe varwere varasikirwe nehupenyu .
Mumwe anga achiperekedza hama yake kunorapwa , VaItai Mundondo , vati kunyange vauya kuma 8 dzemangwanani , vanga vasati vabatsirwa apo zuva range rave kudoka .
Vamwewo vanoti kusaenda kubasa kwana chiremba nana mukoti kwapa mukana kuvamwe vana chiremba kuti vati vanorwarirwa vabvise mari vasati vavatarisa .
Nyaya yange iri imweyo kuHarare Hospital , uko vana mukoti vachiri kudzidzira basa vange vachishanda zvine chinono mukati .
Sangano rinomirira vana chiremba , reZimbabwe Hospital Doctors Association , raburitsa gwaro richiti nhengo dzaro hadzisi kuzodzokera kumabasa kana hurumende isati yavapa mari yavo yemuhoro pamwe nemari yebhonasi .
Vanhu vazhinji vanoenda kuzvipatara zvehurumende vanhu vanotambura nekudaro kunyange kusina vana chiremba vanhu vakawanda vanongoramba vakagarira nechivimbo chekuti hurumende ichagadzirisa dambudiko iri mukuedza kuchengetedza hupenyu sezvo vasina mari dzekuenda kunoona vana chiremba kuzvipatara zvisiri zvehurumende .
Kuona chiremba kunoda mari inosvika madhora makumi matatu usati watanga kurapwa .
Hurumende iri kutora matanho akawanda anosanganisira kuvaka madhamu pamwe nekutenga mishonga inochenesa mvura senzira yekupedza dambudziko remvura mumadhora nemaguta munyika .
Vachizivisa zvazeyiwa nedare remakurukota nhasi , gurukota rezvekuburitswa kwemashoko , Amai Monica Mutsvangwa , vati dare razeya nyaya yekunetsa kwemvura uye harina kufara nenyaya yekuti kanzuru yeHarare yakavhara michina inochenesa mvura yeMorton Jaffray isina kunzwa pfungwa dzehurumende .
Vatiwo dare raumba komiti inosanganisira mapazi ezvemari neremvura kuti ishande nekanzuru yeHarare mukugadzirisa dambudziko remvura .
Amai Mutsvangwa vatiwo hurumende iri kuronga kuti pave nehwaro hwekuti mishonga yekuchenura mvura yemakanzuru ese itengwe pamwechete .
Vatiwo hurumende yaita chisungo chekuti madhamu eKunzwi , Muda neNyatsime , avakwe nekukasika senzira yekupedza dambudziko remvura muHarare .
Gurukota rezvemari , Muzvinafundo Mthuli Ncude , vatiwo hurumende yave kubatsira madhorobha nemaguta ese munyika kuti atenge mishonga yekuchenesa mvura vachiti pari zvino guta reKwekwe ndiro rega risati rabatsirwa nemvura .

Zvichakadai VaNcube vati hurumende ichaverenga vanhu zvakare muna 2022 uye chirongwa ichi chinokosha mamirioni makumi masere nemashanu emadhora .
Vati vanotarisira kuti zvichabuda muchirongwa ichi zvichaziviswa muna Kurume 2023 .
Mune imwewo nyaya , Amai Mutsvangwa vati pane mabhanga matatu anoti , CBZ , Agribank neStanbic achashanda nehurumende pachirongwa cheCommanda Agriculture .
Amai Mutsvangwa vatiwo vanoda kupinda muchirongwa ichi vanoenda kumabhanga matatu aya uye vanotarisira kuti mamwe mabhanga achapinda muchirongwa ichi .
Mumakore apfuura , chirongwa ichi chakange chisina kujeka asi VaNcube vati chave kuitwa pachena uye mabhanga ndiwo ane hunyanzvi hwekuziva vanokodzera kana kusakodzera kupihwa zvikwereti zvekurimisa .

Bazi rezvehutano rakazivisa nezuro kuti vanhu vakanga vabatwa nechirwere che Covid - 19 munyika vaive vasvika pazviuru zvina nemazana masere negumi nevasere , kana kuti 4 818 .
Vanhu vafa nechirwere cheCovid - 19 munyika yose vachiri zana nevana kana kuti 104 , uye vapona vasvika kuchiuru nemazana mashanu nemakumi mana nevana , kana kuti 1 544 .

Huwandu hwevanhu vabatwa nechirwere cheCovid - 19 munyika hwakakwira neMuvhuro kusvika pamazana mashanu negumi nevaviri ( 512 ) mushure mekunge vamwe vanhu makumi maviri nevatatu ( 23 ) vawanikwa vaine chirwere ichi pavanhu mazana mashanu nemakumi matatu nevashanu ( 535 ) vakaongororwa nezuro .
Huwandu hwevanhu vapona kubva kudenda iri huchiri pamakumi matanhatu nevana ( 64 ) , kuchitiwo vashaya vachiri vatanhatu kana kuti 6 .
Kuwanda kwevanhu vabatwa nechirwere cheCovid - 19 uku kwaita kuti bazi rezvehutano riburitse mashoko padandemutande reTwitter richiti rave kuzosimbisa nyaya yekudzidzisa veruzhinji pamusoro pechirwere ichi pachiteverwa zvisungo zvakatarwa neWorld Health Organisation .
Nyanzvi mune zvehutano dzakawanda dzagara dziri kukurudzira hurumende kuti iwedzere vanhu vari kuongororwa chirwere ichi pazuva , uye kuendesa dzidziso kumaruwa kuitira kuti veruzhinji vanzwisise nekukasika zviri kuitika kuitira kuti vasazobatwa vakavarairwa .
Johns Hopkins University Hospital yemuAmerica inoti vanhu vabatwa neCovid - 19 pasi rose vadarika mamiriyoni mapfumbamwe nezana rezviuru ( 9 . 1 million ) , America iri iyo ine vanhu vakawandisa vanodarika mamiriyoni maviri nemazana matatu ezviuru ( 2 . 3 million ) ichiteverwa neBrazil , iyo yadarikawo miriyoni nezana rezviuru ( 1 . 1 million ) .
Mumatunhu akawanda eAmerica chirwere ichi chinonzi chave kukwira zvakare zvichitevera kunyevenutswa kwemutemo unorambidza kufambafamba kwevanhu .
Nyanzvi mune zvehutano , Doctor Simbiso Ranga , avo vari muNorth Carolina muno muAmerica , vanoti huwandu hwevanhu vari kubatwa nechirwere ichi huri kukwira , kwete muZimbabwe chete , asi pasi rose , izvo anoti zvinofanirwa kutorerwa matanho nekukasika .
Panyaya yekukwira kwehuwandu munyika , Doctor Ranga vanoti hurumende inofanirwa kuendesa hurongwa hwekuongorora vanhu akaita sekukurudzira vanhu kupfeka mamasiki , kugeza maoko , uyewo kuchengetedza vanenge vawanikwa vaine chirwere ichi kwavo voga .

Boka rePublic Service Commission , rakayambira varairidzi vairamwa mabasa kuti vaizobatirwa mari dzemazuva avanenge vasina kushanda , kana kuti vaizotorerwa mazuva avo ezororo .

VaMpofu vaudza dare kuti komiti yepamusoro - soro muMDC pakati pemakongiresi yeNational Council yakatora danho rekugadza VaChamisa semutungamiri weMDC zvichitevera kufa kwavaimbova mutungamiri weMDC , VaMorgan Tsvangirai .

Asi nyaya iyi yakonzeresa mutauro wakanyanya munyika vamwe vachiti nyika yave kudzokera kumazivandadzoka sezvo kurembera kwayakaita ikozvino kuri nani pane kudonha .

Nyanzvi munyaya dzezvehupfumi vachitungamira zvidzidzo paZimbabwe Ezekiel Guti University , Doctor Gift Mugano , vati vanotenderanawo naVaBiti .

Doctor Mugano vati panyaya yekudzora dhora , hurumende inofanirawo kupa vanhu chivimbo kwete kuda kuvabata kumeso .
Mashoko aya atsinhirwawo naVaBiti vati hurumende inoziva zvinofanira kuitwa uye ikasadaro inenge yazvisikira moto muziso .
Bhanga rinokweretesa mari nyika dzepasi rino reInternational Monetary Fund , iro rakashora kuparurwa kwemabond notes , rinoti hurumende inofanira kurega kushandisa mari yaisina .
Muna 2009 Zimbabwe yakatanga kushandisa mari yekune dzimwe nyika mushure mekunge mabearer cheques ainge aparurwa nevaive gavhuna weReserve Bank of Zimbabwe , VaGideon Gono , anyanya kushaya simba kubva muna 2008 kusvika muna 2009 .
Vamwe vanoti zviri nani kuti Zimbabwe ishandise mari yekuSouth Africa , vamwe vachiti zviripo zviri nani asi hurumende inofanira kumira nyaya yekushandisa mari seyakabhejerwa .
Sangano re Plan International rinoti chirongwa charo chekuyedza kurwisa chirwere chemalaria nekupa vanhu mambure kana kuti mosquito nets ekushandisa chiri kufamba zvakanaka uye chiri kubatsira mukudzikisa huwandu hwevanhu varikubatwa nechirwere ichi .
Sangano re Zimbabwe District Health Information System Data , rinoti malaria inouraya vanhu vakawanda mumatunhu anoti Manicaland , Mashonaland East ne Mashonaland Central .
Kunyangwe zvinhu zvisina kumira zvakanaka , huwandu hwevanhu vanobatwa nemalaria munyika wakaderera nezvikamu makumi manomwe nemapfumbamwe kubva muzana kubva muna 2000 kusvika muna 2015 .
Huwandu hwevanhu vari kufa hwaderera nezvikamu makumi mashanu nemanomwe kubva muzana kubva muna 2003 kusvika muna 2015 .

Huwandu hwevanhu vakafa mutsaona yebhazi reKing Lion iro rakabheuka kuNyamakate apo raibva kuHarare richienda kuLusaka , Zambia hwakwira kusvika pamakumi mana nevashanu .

Vakafanobata chigaro chemukuru wechipatara cheChinhoyi , Matron Mavis Dube , vanoti pari zvino mitumbi inosvika makumi maviri nemipfumbamwe vazivikanwa nehama dzavo .

Muteveri wemutambo wetsiva , Muzvare Rosemary Makumbe , vanoti vari kurwadzikana zvikuru nekushaya kwaita Tinago vachiti ivo vari kurwadzikana kuti tsiva haina kuda kushandisa ruzivo rwaTinago kusimudzira mutambo uyu mune vechidiki .
Muna 1981 , Tinago ndiye akaita mutambi wekutanga kuita mukurumbira kunze kwenyika apo akatora mukombe wake wekutanga wemuAfrican mushure mekupunzira pasi Hogan Jimoh wekuNigeria .
Izvi hazvina kugumira ipapo sezvo Tinago akazoenderera mberi nekunotora mikombe mitatu yeCommonwealth muhuremu hwakasiyana - siyana .
Tinago akapinda mudariro achirwa kanokwa zana nemitambo minomwe , akakunda mitambo makumi masere nemitatu , gumi nemitanhatu achiita knock out vaairwa navo .
Mumitambo iyi , akakundwa mumitambo makumi maviri , mina achiitwa knock out . Muna 1999 , Tinago akadomwa pavatambi vairwira mukombe weZimbabwe Sportsperson of the Century , mukombe wacho ukazotorwa naNick Price wemutambo wegorofu .
Tinago akaberekerwa kuShurugwi muna 1949 .
